 </center>
 <hr>
  <h3 align="center">Young's Literal Translation: Psalms</h3> 
 <p><a name="an_1:1">1:1</a> O the happiness of that one, who Hath not walked in the  counsel of the wicked. And in the way of sinners hath not  stood, And in the seat of scorners hath not sat;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:2">1:2</a> But -- in the law of Jehovah [is] his delight, And in His  law he doth meditate by day and by night:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:3">1:3</a> And he hath been as a tree, Planted by rivulets of water,  That giveth its fruit in its season, And its leaf doth not  wither, And all that he doth he causeth to prosper.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:4">1:4</a> Not so the wicked: But -- as chaff that wind driveth away!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:5">1:5</a> Therefore the wicked rise not in judgment, Nor sinners in  the company of the righteous,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_1:6">1:6</a> For Jehovah is knowing the way of the righteous, And the way  of the wicked is lost!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:1">2:1</a> Why have nations tumultuously assembled? And do peoples  meditate vanity?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:2">2:2</a> Station themselves do kings of the earth, And princes have  been united together, Against Jehovah, and against His Messiah:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:3">2:3</a> `Let us draw off Their cords, And cast from us Their thick  bands.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:4">2:4</a> He who is sitting in the heavens doth laugh, The Lord doth  mock at them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:5">2:5</a> Then doth He speak unto them in His anger, And in His wrath  He doth trouble them:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:6">2:6</a> `And I -- I have anointed My King, Upon Zion -- My holy  hill.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:7">2:7</a> I declare concerning a statute: Jehovah said unto me, `My  Son Thou [art], I to-day have brought thee forth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:8">2:8</a> Ask of Me and I give nations -- thy inheritance, And thy  possession -- the ends of earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:9">2:9</a> Thou dost rule them with a sceptre of iron, As a vessel of a  potter Thou dost crush them.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:10">2:10</a> And now, O kings, act wisely, Be instructed, O judges of  earth,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:11">2:11</a> Serve ye Jehovah with fear, And rejoice with trembling.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_2:12">2:12</a> Kiss the Chosen One, lest He be angry, And ye lose the way,  When His anger burneth but a little, O the happiness of all  trusting in Him!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:1">3:1</a> A Psalm of David, in his fleeing from the face of Absalom  his son. Jehovah, how have my distresses multiplied! Many are  rising up against me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:2">3:2</a> Many are saying of my soul, `There is no salvation for him  in God.' Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:3">3:3</a> And Thou, O Jehovah, [art] a shield for me, My honour, and  lifter up of my head.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:4">3:4</a> My voice [is] unto Jehovah: I call: And He answereth me from  his holy hill, Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:5">3:5</a> I -- I have lain down, and I sleep, I have waked, for  Jehovah sustaineth me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:6">3:6</a> I am not afraid of myriads of people, That round about they  have set against me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:7">3:7</a> Rise, O Jehovah! save me, my God. Because Thou hast smitten  All mine enemies [on] the cheek. The teeth of the wicked Thou  hast broken.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_3:8">3:8</a> Of Jehovah [is] this salvation; On Thy people [is] Thy  blessing! Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:1">4:1</a> To the Overseer with Stringed Instruments. -- A Psalm of  David. In my calling answer Thou me, O God of my righteousness.  In adversity Thou gavest enlargement to me; Favour me, and hear  my prayer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:2">4:2</a> Sons of men! till when [is] my glory for shame? Ye love a vain  thing, ye seek a lie. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:3">4:3</a> And know ye that Jehovah Hath separated a saintly one to  Himself. Jehovah heareth in my calling to Him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:4">4:4</a> `Tremble ye, and do not sin;' Say ye [thus] in your heart  on your bed, And be ye silent. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:5">4:5</a> Sacrifice ye sacrifices of righteousness, And trust ye unto  Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:6">4:6</a> Many are saying, `Who doth show us good?' Lift on us the  light of Thy face, O Jehovah,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:7">4:7</a> Thou hast given joy in my heart, From the time their corn  and their wine Have been multiplied.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_4:8">4:8</a> In peace together I lie down and sleep, For Thou, O Jehovah,  alone, In confidence dost cause me to dwell!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:1">5:1</a> To the Overseer, `Concerning the Inheritances.' -- A Psalm  of David. My sayings hear, O Jehovah, Consider my meditation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:2">5:2</a> Be attentive to the voice of my cry, My king and my God, For  unto Thee I pray habitually.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:3">5:3</a> Jehovah, [at] morning Thou hearest my voice, [At] morning I  set in array for Thee, And I look out.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:4">5:4</a> For not a God desiring wickedness [art] Thou, Evil  inhabiteth Thee not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:5">5:5</a> The boastful station not themselves before Thine eyes: Thou  hast hated all working iniquity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:6">5:6</a> Thou destroyest those speaking lies, A man of blood and  deceit Jehovah doth abominate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:7">5:7</a> And I, in the abundance of Thy kindness, I enter Thy house,  I bow myself toward Thy holy temple in Thy fear.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:8">5:8</a> O Jehovah, lead me in Thy righteousness, Because of those  observing me, Make straight before me Thy way,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:9">5:9</a> For there is no stability in their mouth. Their heart [is]  mischiefs, An open grave [is] their throat, Their tongue they  make smooth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:10">5:10</a> Declare them guilty, O God, Let them fall from their own  counsels, In the abundance of their transgressions Drive them  away, Because they have rebelled against Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:11">5:11</a> And rejoice do all trusting in Thee, To the age they sing,  and Thou coverest them over, And those loving Thy name exult in  Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_5:12">5:12</a> For Thou blessest the righteous, O Jehovah, As a buckler  with favour dost compass him!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:1">6:1</a> To the Overseer with stringed instruments, on the octave. --  A Psalm of David. O Jehovah, in Thine anger reprove me not, Nor  in Thy fury chastise me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:2">6:2</a> Favour me, O Jehovah, for I [am] weak, Heal me, O Jehovah,  For troubled have been my bones,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:3">6:3</a> And my soul hath been troubled greatly, And Thou, O Jehovah,  till when?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:4">6:4</a> Turn back, O Jehovah, draw out my soul, Save me for Thy  kindness' sake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:5">6:5</a> For there is not in death Thy memorial, In Sheol, who doth  give thanks to Thee?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:6">6:6</a> I have been weary with my sighing, I meditate through all  the night [on] my bed, With my tear my couch I waste.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:7">6:7</a> Old from provocation is mine eye, It is old because of all  mine adversaries,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:8">6:8</a> Turn from me all ye workers of iniquity, For Jehovah heard  the voice of my weeping,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:9">6:9</a> Jehovah hath heard my supplication, Jehovah my prayer  receiveth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_6:10">6:10</a> Ashamed and troubled greatly are all mine enemies, They  turn back -- ashamed [in] a moment!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:1">7:1</a> `The Erring One,' by David, that he sung to Jehovah  concerning the words of Cush a Benjamite. O Jehovah, my God, in  Thee I have trusted, Save me from all my pursuers, and deliver  me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:2">7:2</a> Lest he tear as a lion my soul, Rending, and there is no  deliverer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:3">7:3</a> O Jehovah, my God, if I have done this, If there is iniquity  in my hands,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:4">7:4</a> If I have done my well-wisher evil, And draw mine adversary  without cause,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:5">7:5</a> An enemy pursueth my soul, and overtaketh, And treadeth down  to the earth my life, And my honour placeth in the dust. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:6">7:6</a> Rise, O Jehovah, in Thine anger, Be lifted up at the wrath  of mine adversaries, And awake Thou for me: Judgment Thou hast  commanded:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:7">7:7</a> And a company of peoples compass Thee, And over it on high  turn Thou back,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:8">7:8</a> Jehovah doth judge the peoples; Judge me, O Jehovah,  According to my righteousness, And according to mine integrity  on me,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:9">7:9</a> Let, I pray Thee be ended the evil of the wicked, And  establish Thou the righteous, And a trier of hearts and reins  is the righteous God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:10">7:10</a> My shield [is] on God, Saviour of the upright in heart!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:11">7:11</a> God [is] a righteous judge, And He is not angry at all  times.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:12">7:12</a> If [one] turn not, His sword he sharpeneth, His bow he hath  trodden -- He prepareth it,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:13">7:13</a> Yea, for him He hath prepared Instruments of death, His  arrows for burning pursuers He maketh.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:14">7:14</a> Lo, he travaileth [with] iniquity, And he hath conceived  perverseness, And hath brought forth falsehood.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:15">7:15</a> A pit he hath prepared, and he diggeth it, And he falleth  into a ditch he maketh.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:16">7:16</a> Return doth his perverseness on his head, And on his crown  his violence cometh down.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_7:17">7:17</a> I thank Jehovah, According to His righteousness, And praise  the name of Jehovah Most High!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:1">8:1</a> To the Overseer, `On the Gittith.' A Psalm of David. Jehovah,  our Lord, How honourable Thy name in all the earth! Who settest  thine honour on the heavens.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:2">8:2</a> From the mouths of infants and sucklings Thou hast founded  strength, Because of Thine adversaries, To still an enemy and a  self-avenger.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:3">8:3</a> For I see Thy heavens, a work of Thy fingers, Moon and stars  that Thou didst establish.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:4">8:4</a> What [is] man that Thou rememberest him? The son of man that  Thou inspectest him?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:5">8:5</a> And causest him to lack a little of Godhead, And with honour  and majesty compassest him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:6">8:6</a> Thou dost cause him to rule Over the works of Thy hands, All  Thou hast placed under his feet.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:7">8:7</a> Sheep and oxen, all of them, And also beasts of the field,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:8">8:8</a> Bird of the heavens, and fish of the sea, Passing through  the paths of the seas!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_8:9">8:9</a> Jehovah, our Lord, How honourable Thy name in all the earth!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:1">9:1</a> To the Overseer, `On the Death of Labben.' -- A Psalm of  David. I confess, O Jehovah, with all my heart, I recount all  Thy wonders,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:2">9:2</a> I rejoice and exult in Thee, I praise Thy Name, O Most High.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:3">9:3</a> In mine enemies turning backward, they stumble and perish  from Thy face.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:4">9:4</a> For Thou hast done my judgment and my right. Thou hast sat  on a throne, A judge of righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:5">9:5</a> Thou hast rebuked nations, Thou hast destroyed the wicked,  Their name Thou hast blotted out to the age and for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:6">9:6</a> O thou Enemy, Finished have been destructions for ever, As  to cities thou hast plucked up, Perished hath their memorial  with them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:7">9:7</a> And Jehovah to the age abideth, He is preparing for judgment  His throne.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:8">9:8</a> And He judgeth the world in righteousness, He judgeth the  peoples in uprightness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:9">9:9</a> And Jehovah is a tower for the bruised, A tower for times of  adversity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:10">9:10</a> They trust in Thee who do know Thy name, For Thou hast not  forsaken Those seeking Thee, O Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:11">9:11</a> Sing ye praise to Jehovah, inhabiting Zion, Declare ye  among the peoples His acts,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:12">9:12</a> For He who is seeking for blood Them hath remembered, He  hath not forgotten the cry of the afflicted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:13">9:13</a> Favour me, O Jehovah, See mine affliction by those hating  me, Thou who liftest me up from the gates of death,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:14">9:14</a> So that I recount all Thy praise, In the gates of the  daughter of Zion. I rejoice on Thy salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:15">9:15</a> Sunk have nations in a pit they made, In a net that they  hid hath their foot been captured.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:16">9:16</a> Jehovah hath been known, Judgment He hath done, By a work  of his hands Hath the wicked been snared. Meditation. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:17">9:17</a> The wicked do turn back to Sheol, All nations forgetting  God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:18">9:18</a> For not for ever is the needy forgotten, The hope of the  humble lost to the age.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:19">9:19</a> Rise, O Jehovah, let not man be strong, Let nations be  judged before Thy face.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_9:20">9:20</a> Appoint, O Jehovah, a director to them, Let nations know  they [are] men! Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:1">10:1</a> Why, Jehovah, dost Thou stand at a distance? Thou dost hide  in times of adversity,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:2">10:2</a> Through the pride of the wicked, Is the poor inflamed, They  are caught in devices that they devised.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:3">10:3</a> Because the wicked hath boasted Of the desire of his soul,  And a dishonest gainer he hath blessed, He hath despised  Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:4">10:4</a> The wicked according to the height of his face, inquireth  not. `God is not!' [are] all his devices.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:5">10:5</a> Pain do his ways at all times, On high [are] Thy judgments  before him, All his adversaries -- he puffeth at them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:6">10:6</a> He hath said in his heart, `I am not moved,' To generation  and generation not in evil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:7">10:7</a> Of oaths his mouth is full, And deceits, and fraud: Under  his tongue [is] perverseness and iniquity,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:8">10:8</a> He doth sit in an ambush of the villages, In secret places  he doth slay the innocent. His eyes for the afflicted watch  secretly,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:9">10:9</a> He lieth in wait in a secret place, as a lion in a covert.  He lieth in wait to catch the poor, He catcheth the poor,  drawing him into his net.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:10">10:10</a> He is bruised -- he boweth down, Fallen by his mighty ones  hath the afflicted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:11">10:11</a> He said in his heart, `God hath forgotten, He hath hid His  face, He hath never seen.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:12">10:12</a> Arise, O Jehovah! O God, lift up Thy hand! Forget not the  humble.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:13">10:13</a> Wherefore hath the wicked despised God? He hath said in  his heart, `It is not required.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:14">10:14</a> Thou hast seen, For Thou perverseness and anger beholdest;  By giving into Thy hand, On Thee doth the afflicted leave [it],  Of the fatherless Thou hast been an helper.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:15">10:15</a> Break the arm of the wicked and the evil, Seek out his  wickedness, find none;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:16">10:16</a> Jehovah [is] king to the age, and for ever, The nations  have perished out of His land!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:17">10:17</a> The desire of the humble Thou hast heard, O Jehovah. Thou  preparest their heart; Thou causest Thine ear to attend,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_10:18">10:18</a> To judge the fatherless and bruised: He addeth no more to  oppress -- man of the earth!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:1">11:1</a> To the Overseer. -- By David. In Jehovah I trusted, how say  ye to my soul, `They moved [to] Thy mountain for the bird?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:2">11:2</a> For lo, the wicked tread a bow, They have prepared their  arrow on the string, To shoot in darkness at the upright in  heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:3">11:3</a> When the foundations are destroyed, The righteous -- what  hath he done?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:4">11:4</a> `Jehovah [is] in his holy temple: Jehovah -- in the heavens  [is] His throne. His eyes see -- His eyelids try the sons of  men.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:5">11:5</a> Jehovah the righteous doth try. And the wicked and the  lover of violence, Hath His soul hated,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:6">11:6</a> He poureth on the wicked snares, fire, and brimstone, And a  horrible wind [is] the portion of their cup.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_11:7">11:7</a> For righteous [is] Jehovah, Righteousness He hath loved,  The upright doth His countenance see!'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:1">12:1</a> To the Overseer, on the octave. -- A Psalm of David. Save,  Jehovah, for the saintly hath failed, For the stedfast have  ceased From the sons of men:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:2">12:2</a> Vanity they speak each with his neighbour, Lip of flattery!  With heart and heart they speak.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:3">12:3</a> Jehovah doth cut off all lips of flattery, A tongue  speaking great things,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:4">12:4</a> Who said, `By our tongue we do mightily: Our lips [are] our  own; who [is] lord over us?'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:5">12:5</a> Because of the spoiling of the poor, Because of the  groaning of the needy, Now do I arise, saith Jehovah, I set in  safety [him who] doth breathe for it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:6">12:6</a> Sayings of Jehovah [are] pure sayings; Silver tried in a  furnace of earth refined sevenfold.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:7">12:7</a> Thou, O Jehovah, dost preserve them, Thou keepest us from  this generation to the age.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_12:8">12:8</a> Around the wicked walk continually, According as vileness  is exalted by sons of men!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:1">13:1</a> To the Overseer. -- A Psalm of David. Till when, O Jehovah,  Dost Thou forget me? -- for ever? Till when dost Thou hide Thy  face from me?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:2">13:2</a> Till when do I set counsels in my soul? Sorrow inn my heart  daily? Till when is mine enemy exalted over me?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:3">13:3</a> Look attentively; Answer me, O Jehovah, my God, Enlighten  mine eyes, lest I sleep in death,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:4">13:4</a> Lest mine enemy say, `I overcame him,' Mine adversaries joy  when I am moved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:5">13:5</a> And I, in Thy kindness I have trusted, Rejoice doth my  heart in Thy salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_13:6">13:6</a> I do sing to Jehovah, For He hath conferred benefits upon  me!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:1">14:1</a> To the Overseer. -- By David. A fool hath said in his  heart, `God is not;' They have done corruptly, They have done  abominable actions, There is not a doer of good.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:2">14:2</a> Jehovah from the heavens Hath looked on the sons of men, To  see if there is a wise one -- seeking God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:3">14:3</a> The whole have turned aside, Together they have been  filthy: There is not a doer of good, not even one.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:4">14:4</a> Have all working iniquity not known? Those consuming my  people have eaten bread, Jehovah they have not called.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:5">14:5</a> There they have feared a fear, For God [is] in the  generation of the righteous.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:6">14:6</a> The counsel of the poor ye cause to stink, Because Jehovah  [is] his refuge.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_14:7">14:7</a> `Who doth give from Zion the salvation of Israel? When  Jehovah doth turn back [To] a captivity of His people, Jacob  doth rejoice -- Israel is glad!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:1">15:1</a> A Psalm of David. Jehovah, who doth sojourn in Thy tent?  Who doth dwell in Thy holy hill?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:2">15:2</a> He who is walking uprightly, And working righteousness, And  speaking truth in his heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:3">15:3</a> He hath not slandered by his tongue, He hath not done to  his friend evil; And reproach he hath not lifted up Against his  neighbour.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:4">15:4</a> Despised in his eyes [is] a rejected one, And those fearing  Jehovah he doth honour. He hath sworn to suffer evil, and  changeth not;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_15:5">15:5</a> His silver he hath not given in usury, And a bribe against  the innocent Hath not taken; Whoso is doing these is not moved  to the age!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:1">16:1</a> A Secret Treasure of David. Preserve me, O God, for I did  trust in Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:2">16:2</a> Thou hast said to Jehovah, `My Lord Thou [art];' My good  [is] not for thine own sake;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:3">16:3</a> For the holy ones who [are] in the land, And the  honourable, all my delight [is] in them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:4">16:4</a> Multiplied are their griefs, [Who] have hastened backward;  I pour not out their libations of blood, Nor do I take up their  names on my lips.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:5">16:5</a> Jehovah [is] the portion of my share, and of my cup, Thou  -- Thou dost uphold my lot.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:6">16:6</a> Lines have fallen to me in pleasant places, Yea, a  beauteous inheritance [is] for me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:7">16:7</a> I bless Jehovah who hath counselled me; Also [in] the  nights my reins instruct me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:8">16:8</a> I did place Jehovah before me continually, Because -- at my  right hand I am not moved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:9">16:9</a> Therefore hath my heart been glad, And my honour doth  rejoice, Also my flesh dwelleth confidently:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:10">16:10</a> For Thou dost not leave my soul to Sheol, Nor givest thy  saintly one to see corruption.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_16:11">16:11</a> Thou causest me to know the path of life; Fulness of joys  [is] with Thy presence, Pleasant things by Thy right hand for  ever!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:1">17:1</a> A Prayer of David. Hear, O Jehovah, righteousness, attend  my cry, Give ear [to] my prayer, without lips of deceit.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:2">17:2</a> From before thee my judgment doth go out; Thine eyes do see  uprightly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:3">17:3</a> Thou hast proved my heart, Thou hast inspected by night,  Thou hast tried me, Thou findest nothing; My thoughts pass not  over my mouth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:4">17:4</a> As to doings of man, Through a word of Thy lips I have  observed The paths of a destroyer;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:5">17:5</a> To uphold my goings in Thy paths, My steps have not  slidden.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:6">17:6</a> I -- I called Thee, for Thou dost answer me, O God, incline  Thine ear to me, hear my speech.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:7">17:7</a> Separate wonderfully Thy kindness, O Saviour of the  confiding, By Thy right hand, from withstanders.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:8">17:8</a> Keep me as the apple, the daughter of the eye; In shadow of  Thy wings thou dost hide me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:9">17:9</a> From the face of the wicked who spoiled me. Mine enemies in  soul go round against me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:10">17:10</a> Their fat they have closed up, Their mouths have spoken  with pride:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:11">17:11</a> `Our steps now have compassed [him];' Their eyes they set  to turn aside in the land.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:12">17:12</a> His likeness as a lion desirous to tear, As a young lion  dwelling in secret places.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:13">17:13</a> Arise, O Jehovah, go before his face, Cause him to bend.  Deliver my soul from the wicked, Thy sword,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:14">17:14</a> From men, Thy hand, O Jehovah, From men of the world,  their portion [is] in life, And [with] Thy hidden things Thou  fillest their belly, They are satisfied [with] sons; And have  left their abundance to their sucklings.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_17:15">17:15</a> I -- in righteousness, I see Thy face; I am satisfied, in  awaking, [with] Thy form!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:1">18:1</a> To the Overseer. -- By a servant of Jehovah, by David, who  hath spoken to Jehovah the words of this song in the day  Jehovah delivered him from the hand of all his enemies, and  from the hand of Saul, and he saith: -- I love Thee, O Jehovah,  my strength.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:2">18:2</a> Jehovah [is] my rock, and my bulwark, And my deliverer, My  God [is] my rock, I trust in Him: My shield, and a horn of my  salvation, My high tower.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:3">18:3</a> The `Praised One' I call Jehovah, And from my enemies I am  saved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:4">18:4</a> Compassed me have cords of death, And streams of the  worthless make me afraid.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:5">18:5</a> Cords of Sheol have surrounded me, Before me have been  snares of death.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:6">18:6</a> In mine adversity I call Jehovah, And unto my God I cry. He  heareth from His temple my voice, And My cry before Him cometh  into His ears.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:7">18:7</a> And shake and tremble doth the earth, And foundations of  hills are troubled, And they shake -- because He hath wrath.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:8">18:8</a> Gone up hath smoke by His nostrils, And fire from His mouth  consumeth, Coals have been kindled by it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:9">18:9</a> And He inclineth the heavens, and cometh down, And thick  darkness [is] under His feet.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:10">18:10</a> And He rideth on a cherub, and doth fly, And He flieth on  wings of wind.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:11">18:11</a> He maketh darkness His secret place, Round about Him His  tabernacle, Darkness of waters, thick clouds of the skies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:12">18:12</a> From the brightness over-against Him His thick clouds have  passed on, Hail and coals of fire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:13">18:13</a> And thunder in the heavens doth Jehovah, And the Most  High giveth forth His voice, Hail and coals of fire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:14">18:14</a> And He sendeth His arrows and scattereth them, And much  lightning, and crusheth them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:15">18:15</a> And seen are the streams of waters, And revealed are  foundations of the earth. From Thy rebuke, O Jehovah, From the  breath of the spirit of Thine anger.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:16">18:16</a> He sendeth from above -- He taketh me, He draweth me out  of many waters.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:17">18:17</a> He delivereth me from my strong enemy, And from those  hating me, For they have been stronger than I.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:18">18:18</a> They go before me in a day of my calamity And Jehovah is  for a support to me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:19">18:19</a> And He bringeth me forth to a large place, He draweth me  out, because He delighted in me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:20">18:20</a> Jehovah doth recompense me According to my righteousness,  According to the cleanness of my hands, He doth return to me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:21">18:21</a> For I have kept the ways of Jehovah, And have not done  wickedly against my God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:22">18:22</a> For all His judgments [are] before me, And His statutes I  turn not from me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:23">18:23</a> And I am perfect with him, And I keep myself from mine  iniquity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:24">18:24</a> And Jehovah doth return to me, According to my  righteousness, According to the cleanness of my hands,  Over-against his eyes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:25">18:25</a> With the kind Thou showest Thyself kind, With a perfect  man showest Thyself perfect.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:26">18:26</a> With the pure Thou showest Thyself pure, And with the  perverse showest Thyself a wrestler,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:27">18:27</a> For Thou a poor people savest, And the eyes of the high  causest to fall.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:28">18:28</a> For Thou -- Thou lightest my lamp, Jehovah my God  enlighteneth my darkness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:29">18:29</a> For by Thee I run -- a troop! And by my God I leap a wall.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:30">18:30</a> God! perfect [is] His way, The saying of Jehovah is tried,  A shield [is] He to all those trusting in Him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:31">18:31</a> For who [is] God besides Jehovah? And who [is] a rock save  our God?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:32">18:32</a> God! who is girding me [with] strength, And He maketh  perfect my way.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:33">18:33</a> Making my feet like hinds, And on my high places causeth  me to stand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:34">18:34</a> Teaching my hands for battle, And a bow of brass was  brought down by my arms.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:35">18:35</a> And Thou givest to me the shield of Thy salvation, And Thy  right hand doth support me, And Thy lowliness maketh me great.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:36">18:36</a> Thou enlargest my step under me, And mine ankles have not  slidden.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:37">18:37</a> I pursue mine enemies, and overtake them, And turn back  not till they are consumed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:38">18:38</a> I smite them, and they are not able to rise, They fall  under my feet,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:39">18:39</a> And Thou girdest me [with] strength for battle, Causest my  withstanders to bow under me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:40">18:40</a> As to mine enemies -- Thou hast given to me the neck, As  to those hating me -- I cut them off.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:41">18:41</a> They cry, and there is no saviour, On Jehovah, and He doth  not answer them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:42">18:42</a> And I beat them as dust before wind, As mire of the  streets I empty them out.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:43">18:43</a> Thou dost deliver me From the strivings of the people,  Thou placest me for a head of nations, A people I have not  known do serve me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:44">18:44</a> At the hearing of the ear they hearken to me, Sons of a  stranger feign obedience to me,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:45">18:45</a> Sons of a stranger fade away, And are slain out of their  close places.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:46">18:46</a> Jehovah liveth -- and blessed [is] my rock, And exalted is  the God of my salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:47">18:47</a> God -- who is giving vengeance to me, And He subdueth  peoples under me,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:48">18:48</a> My deliverer from mine enemies, Above my withstanders Thou  raisest me, From a man of violence dost deliver me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:49">18:49</a> Therefore I confess Thee among nations, O Jehovah, And to  Thy name I sing praise,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_18:50">18:50</a> Magnifying the salvation of His king, And doing kindness  to His anointed, To David, and to his seed -- unto the age!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:1">19:1</a> To the Overseer. -- A Psalm of David. The heavens [are]  recounting the honour of God, And the work of His hands The  expanse [is] declaring.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:2">19:2</a> Day to day uttereth speech, And night to night sheweth  knowledge.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:3">19:3</a> There is no speech, and there are no words. Their voice  hath not been heard.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:4">19:4</a> Into all the earth hath their line gone forth, And to the  end of the world their sayings, For the sun He placed a tent in  them,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:5">19:5</a> And he, as a bridegroom, goeth out from his covering, He  rejoiceth as a mighty one To run the path.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:6">19:6</a> From the end of the heavens [is] his going out, And his  revolution [is] unto their ends, And nothing is hid from his  heat.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:7">19:7</a> The law of Jehovah [is] perfect, refreshing the soul, The  testimonies of Jehovah [are] stedfast, Making wise the simple,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:8">19:8</a> The precepts of Jehovah [are] upright, Rejoicing the heart,  The command of Jehovah [is] pure, enlightening the eyes,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:9">19:9</a> The fear of Jehovah [is] clean, standing to the age, The  judgments of Jehovah [are] true, They have been righteous --  together.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:10">19:10</a> They are more desirable than gold, Yea, than much fine  gold; and sweeter than honey, Even liquid honey of the comb.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:11">19:11</a> Also -- Thy servant is warned by them, `In keeping them  [is] a great reward.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:12">19:12</a> Errors! who doth understand? From hidden ones declare me  innocent,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:13">19:13</a> Also -- from presumptuous ones keep back Thy servant, Let  them not rule over me, Then am I perfect, And declared innocent  of much transgression,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_19:14">19:14</a> Let the sayings of my mouth, And the meditation of my  heart, Be for a pleasing thing before Thee, O Jehovah, my rock,  and my redeemer!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:1">20:1</a> To the Overseer. -- A Psalm of David. Jehovah doth answer  thee, In a day of adversity, The name of the God of Jacob doth  set thee on high,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:2">20:2</a> He doth send thy help from the sanctuary, And from Zion  doth support thee,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:3">20:3</a> He doth remember all thy presents, And thy burnt-offering doth reduce to ashes. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:4">20:4</a> He doth give to thee according to thy heart, And all thy  counsel doth fulfil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:5">20:5</a> We sing of thy salvation, And in the name of our God set up  a banner. Jehovah doth fulfil all thy requests.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:6">20:6</a> Now I have known That Jehovah hath saved His anointed, He  answereth him from His holy heavens, With the saving might of  His right hand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:7">20:7</a> Some of chariots, and some of horses, And we of the name of  Jehovah our God Make mention.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:8">20:8</a> They -- they have bowed and have fallen, And we have risen  and station ourselves upright.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_20:9">20:9</a> O Jehovah, save the king, He doth answer us in the day we  call!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:1">21:1</a> To the Overseer. -- A Psalm of David. Jehovah, in Thy  strength is the king joyful, In Thy salvation how greatly he  rejoiceth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:2">21:2</a> The desire of his heart Thou gavest to him, And the request  of his lips Thou hast not withheld. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:3">21:3</a> For Thou puttest before him blessings of goodness, Thou  settest on his head a crown of fine gold.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:4">21:4</a> Life he hath asked from Thee, Thou hast given to him --  length of days, Age-during -- and for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:5">21:5</a> Great [is] his honour in Thy salvation, Honour and majesty  Thou placest on him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:6">21:6</a> For Thou makest him blessings for ever, Thou dost cause him  to rejoice with joy, By Thy countenance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:7">21:7</a> For the king is trusting in Jehovah, And in the kindness of  the Most High He is not moved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:8">21:8</a> Thy hand cometh to all Thine enemies, Thy right hand doth  find Thy haters.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:9">21:9</a> Thou makest them as a furnace of fire, At the time of Thy  presence. Jehovah in His anger doth swallow them, And fire doth  devour them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:10">21:10</a> Their fruit from earth Thou destroyest, And their seed  from the sons of men.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:11">21:11</a> For they stretched out against Thee evil, They devised a  wicked device, they prevail not,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:12">21:12</a> For Thou makest them a butt, When Thy strings Thou  preparest against their faces.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_21:13">21:13</a> Be Thou exalted, O Jehovah in, Thy strength, We sing and  we praise Thy might!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:1">22:1</a> To the Overseer, on `The Hind of the Morning.' -- A Psalm  of David. My God, my God, why hast Thou forsaken me? Far from  my salvation, The words of my roaring?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:2">22:2</a> My God, I call by day, and Thou answerest not, And by  night, and there is no silence to me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:3">22:3</a> And Thou [art] holy, Sitting -- the Praise of Israel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:4">22:4</a> In Thee did our fathers trust -- they trusted, And Thou  dost deliver them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:5">22:5</a> Unto Thee they cried, and were delivered, In Thee they  trusted, and were not ashamed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:6">22:6</a> And I [am] a worm, and no man, A reproach of man, and  despised of the people.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:7">22:7</a> All beholding me do mock at me, They make free with the lip  -- shake the head,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:8">22:8</a> `Roll unto Jehovah, He doth deliver him, He doth deliver  him, for he delighted in him.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:9">22:9</a> For thou [art] He bringing me forth from the womb, Causing  me to trust, On the breasts of my mother.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:10">22:10</a> On Thee I have been cast from the womb, From the belly of  my mother Thou [art] my God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:11">22:11</a> Be not far from me, For adversity is near, for there is no  helper.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:12">22:12</a> Many bulls have surrounded me, Mighty ones of Bashan have  compassed me,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:13">22:13</a> They have opened against me their mouth, A lion tearing  and roaring.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:14">22:14</a> As waters I have been poured out, And separated themselves  have all my bones, My heart hath been like wax, It is melted in  the midst of my bowels.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:15">22:15</a> Dried up as an earthen vessel is my power, And my tongue  is cleaving to my jaws.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:16">22:16</a> And to the dust of death thou appointest me, For  surrounded me have dogs, A company of evil doers have compassed  me, Piercing my hands and my feet.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:17">22:17</a> I count all my bones -- they look expectingly, They look  upon me,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:18">22:18</a> They apportion my garments to themselves, And for my  clothing they cause a lot to fall.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:19">22:19</a> And Thou, O Jehovah, be not far off, O my strength, to  help me haste.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:20">22:20</a> Deliver from the sword my soul, From the paw of a dog mine  only one.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:21">22:21</a> Save me from the mouth of a lion: -- And -- from the horns  of the high places Thou hast answered me!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:22">22:22</a> I declare Thy name to my brethren, In the midst of the  assembly I praise Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:23">22:23</a> Ye who fear Jehovah, praise ye Him, All the seed of Jacob,  honour ye Him, And be afraid of Him, all ye seed of Israel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:24">22:24</a> For He hath not despised, nor abominated, The affliction  of the afflicted, Nor hath He hidden His face from him, And in  his crying unto Him He heareth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:25">22:25</a> Of Thee my praise [is] in the great assembly. My vows I  complete before His fearers.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:26">22:26</a> The humble do eat and are satisfied, Praise Jehovah do  those seeking Him, Your heart doth live for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:27">22:27</a> Remember and return unto Jehovah, Do all ends of the  earth, And before Thee bow themselves, Do all families of the  nations,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:28">22:28</a> For to Jehovah [is] the kingdom, And He is ruling among  nations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:29">22:29</a> And the fat ones of earth have eaten, And they bow  themselves, Before Him bow do all going down to dust, And he  [who] hath not revived his soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:30">22:30</a> A seed doth serve Him, It is declared of the Lord to the  generation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_22:31">22:31</a> They come and declare His righteousness, To a people that  is borne, that He hath made!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:1">23:1</a> A Psalm of David. Jehovah [is] my shepherd, I do not lack,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:2">23:2</a> In pastures of tender grass He causeth me to lie down, By  quiet waters He doth lead me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:3">23:3</a> My soul He refresheth, He leadeth me in paths of  righteousness, For His name's sake,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:4">23:4</a> Also -- when I walk in a valley of death-shade, I fear no  evil, for Thou [art] with me, Thy rod and Thy staff -- they  comfort me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:5">23:5</a> Thou arrangest before me a table, Over-against my  adversaries, Thou hast anointed with oil my head, My cup is  full!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_23:6">23:6</a> Only -- goodness and kindness pursue me, All the days of my  life, And my dwelling [is] in the house of Jehovah, For a  length of days!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:1">24:1</a> A Psalm of David. To Jehovah [is] the earth and its  fulness, The world and the inhabitants in it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:2">24:2</a> For He on the seas hath founded it, And on the floods He  doth establish it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:3">24:3</a> Who goeth up into the hill of Jehovah? And who riseth up in  His holy place?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:4">24:4</a> The clean of hands, and pure of heart, Who hath not lifted  up to vanity his soul, Nor hath sworn to deceit.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:5">24:5</a> He beareth away a blessing from Jehovah, Righteousness from  the God of his salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:6">24:6</a> This [is] a generation of those seeking Him. Seeking Thy  face, O Jacob! Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:7">24:7</a> Lift up, O gates, your heads, And be lifted up, O doors  age-during, And come in doth the king of glory!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:8">24:8</a> Who [is] this -- `the king of glory?' Jehovah -- strong and  mighty, Jehovah, the mighty in battle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:9">24:9</a> Lift up, O gates, your heads, And be lifted up, O doors  age-during, And come in doth the king of glory!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_24:10">24:10</a> Who [is] He -- this `king of glory?' Jehovah of hosts --  He [is] the king of glory! Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:1">25:1</a> By David. Unto Thee, O Jehovah, my soul I lift up.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:2">25:2</a> My God, in Thee I have trusted, Let me not be ashamed, Let  not mine enemies exult over me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:3">25:3</a> Also let none waiting on Thee be ashamed, Let the  treacherous dealers without cause be ashamed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:4">25:4</a> Thy ways, O Jehovah, cause me to know, Thy paths teach Thou  me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:5">25:5</a> Cause me to tread in Thy truth, and teach me, For Thou  [art] the God of my salvation, Near Thee I have waited all the  day.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:6">25:6</a> Remember Thy mercies, O Jehovah, And Thy kindnesses, for  from the age [are] they.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:7">25:7</a> Sins of my youth, and my transgressions, Do not Thou  remember. According to Thy kindness be mindful of me, For Thy  goodness' sake, O Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:8">25:8</a> Good and upright [is] Jehovah, Therefore He directeth  sinners in the way.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:9">25:9</a> He causeth the humble to tread in judgment, And teacheth  the humble His way.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:10">25:10</a> All the paths of Jehovah [are] kindness and truth, To  those keeping His covenant, And His testimonies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:11">25:11</a> For Thy name's sake, O Jehovah, Thou hast pardoned mine  iniquity, for it [is] great.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:12">25:12</a> Who [is] this -- the man fearing Jehovah? He directeth him  in the way He doth choose.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:13">25:13</a> His soul in good doth remain, And his seed doth possess  the land.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:14">25:14</a> The secret of Jehovah [is] for those fearing Him, And His  covenant -- to cause them to know.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:15">25:15</a> Mine eyes [are] continually unto Jehovah, For He bringeth  out from a net my feet.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:16">25:16</a> Turn Thou unto me, and favour me, For lonely and afflicted  [am] I.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:17">25:17</a> The distresses of my heart have enlarged themselves, From  my distresses bring me out.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:18">25:18</a> See mine affliction and my misery, And bear with all my  sins.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:19">25:19</a> See my enemies, for they have been many, And with violent  hatred they have hated me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:20">25:20</a> Keep my soul, and deliver me, Let me not be ashamed, for I  trusted in Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:21">25:21</a> Integrity and uprightness do keep me, For I have waited  [on] Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_25:22">25:22</a> Redeem Israel, O God, from all his distresses!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:1">26:1</a> By David. Judge me, O Jehovah, for I in mine integrity have  walked, And in Jehovah I have trusted, I slide not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:2">26:2</a> Try me, O Jehovah, and prove me, Purified [are] my reins  and my heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:3">26:3</a> For Thy kindness [is] before mine eyes, And I have walked  habitually in Thy truth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:4">26:4</a> I have not sat with vain men, And with dissemblers I enter  not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:5">26:5</a> I have hated the assembly of evil doers, And with the  wicked I sit not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:6">26:6</a> I wash in innocency my hands, And I compass Thine altar, O  Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:7">26:7</a> To sound with a voice of confession, And to recount all Thy  wonders.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:8">26:8</a> Jehovah, I have loved the habitation of Thy house, And the  place of the tabernacle of Thine honour.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:9">26:9</a> Do not gather with sinners my soul, And with men of blood  my life,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:10">26:10</a> In whose hand [is] a wicked device, And their right hand  [is] full of bribes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:11">26:11</a> And I, in mine integrity I walk, Redeem me, and favour me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_26:12">26:12</a> My foot hath stood in uprightness, In assemblies I bless  Jehovah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:1">27:1</a> By David. Jehovah [is] my light and my salvation, Whom do I  fear? Jehovah [is] the strength of my life, Of whom am I  afraid?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:2">27:2</a> When evil doers come near to me to eat my flesh, My  adversaries and mine enemies to me, They have stumbled and  fallen.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:3">27:3</a> Though a host doth encamp against me, My heart doth not  fear, Though war riseth up against me, In this I [am]  confident.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:4">27:4</a> One [thing] I asked of Jehovah -- it I seek. My dwelling in  the house of Jehovah, All the days of my life, To look on the  pleasantness of Jehovah, And to inquire in His temple.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:5">27:5</a> For He hideth me in a tabernacle in the day of evil, He  hideth me in a secret place of His tent, On a rock he raiseth  me up.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:6">27:6</a> And now, lifted up is my head, Above my enemies -- my  surrounders, And I sacrifice in His tent sacrifices of  shouting, I sing, yea, I sing praise to Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:7">27:7</a> Hear, O Jehovah, my voice -- I call, And favour me, and  answer me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:8">27:8</a> To Thee said my heart `They sought my face, Thy face, O  Jehovah, I seek.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:9">27:9</a> Hide not Thy face from me, Turn not aside in anger Thy  servant, My help Thou hast been. Leave me not, nor forsake me,  O God of my salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:10">27:10</a> When my father and my mother Have forsaken me, then doth  Jehovah gather me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:11">27:11</a> Shew me, O Jehovah, Thy way, And lead me in a path of  uprightness, For the sake of my beholders.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:12">27:12</a> Give me not to the will of my adversaries, For risen  against me have false witnesses, And they breathe out violence  to me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:13">27:13</a> I had not believed to look on the goodness of Jehovah In  the land of the living!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_27:14">27:14</a> Look unto Jehovah -- be strong, And He doth strengthen thy  heart, Yea, look unto Jehovah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:1">28:1</a> By David. Unto Thee, O Jehovah, I call, My rock, be not  silent to me! Lest Thou be silent to me, And I have been  compared With those going down to the pit.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:2">28:2</a> Hear the voice of my supplications, In my crying unto Thee,  In my lifting up my hands toward thy holy oracle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:3">28:3</a> Draw me not with the wicked, And with workers of iniquity,  Speaking peace with their neighbours, And evil in their heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:4">28:4</a> Give to them according to their acting, And according to  the evil of their doings. According to the work of their hands  give to them. Return their deed to them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:5">28:5</a> For they attend not to the doing of Jehovah, And unto the  work of His hands. He throweth them down, And doth not build  them up.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:6">28:6</a> Blessed [is] Jehovah, For He hath heard the voice of my  supplications.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:7">28:7</a> Jehovah [is] my strength, and my shield, In Him my heart  trusted, and I have been helped. And my heart exulteth, And  with my song I thank Him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:8">28:8</a> Jehovah [is] strength to him, Yea, the strength of the  salvation of His anointed [is] He.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_28:9">28:9</a> Save Thy people, and bless Thine inheritance, And feed  them, and carry them to the age!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:1">29:1</a> A Psalm of David. Ascribe to Jehovah, ye sons of the  mighty, Ascribe to Jehovah honour and strength.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:2">29:2</a> Ascribe to Jehovah the honour of His name, Bow yourselves  to Jehovah, In the beauty of holiness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:3">29:3</a> The voice of Jehovah [is] on the waters, The God of glory  hath thundered, Jehovah [is] on many waters.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:4">29:4</a> The voice of Jehovah [is] with power, The voice of Jehovah  [is] with majesty,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:5">29:5</a> The voice of Jehovah [is] shivering cedars, Yea, Jehovah  shivers the cedars of Lebanon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:6">29:6</a> And He causeth them to skip as a calf, Lebanon and Sirion  as a son of Reems,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:7">29:7</a> The voice of Jehovah is hewing fiery flames,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:8">29:8</a> The voice of Jehovah paineth a wilderness, Jehovah paineth  the wilderness of Kadesh.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:9">29:9</a> The voice of Jehovah paineth the oaks, And maketh bare the  forests, And in His temple every one saith, `Glory.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:10">29:10</a> Jehovah on the deluge hath sat, And Jehovah sitteth king  -- to the age,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_29:11">29:11</a> Jehovah strength to his people giveth, Jehovah blesseth  His people with peace!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:1">30:1</a> A Psalm. -- A song of the dedication of the house of David.  I exalt Thee, O Jehovah, For Thou hast drawn me up, and hast  not let mine enemies rejoice over me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:2">30:2</a> Jehovah my God, I have cried to Thee, And Thou dost heal  me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:3">30:3</a> Jehovah, Thou hast brought up from Sheol my soul, Thou hast  kept me alive, From going down [to] the pit.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:4">30:4</a> Sing praise to Jehovah, ye His saints, And give thanks at  the remembrance of His holiness,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:5">30:5</a> For -- a moment [is] in His anger, Life [is] in His  good-will, At even remaineth weeping, and at morn singing.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:6">30:6</a> And I -- I have said in mine ease, `I am not moved -- to  the age.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:7">30:7</a> O Jehovah, in Thy good pleasure, Thou hast caused strength  to remain for my mountain,' Thou hast hidden Thy face -- I have  been troubled.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:8">30:8</a> Unto Thee, O Jehovah, I call, And unto Jehovah I make  supplication.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:9">30:9</a> `What gain [is] in my blood? In my going down unto  corruption? Doth dust thank Thee? doth it declare Thy truth?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:10">30:10</a> Hear, O Jehovah, and favour me, O Jehovah, be a helper to  me.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:11">30:11</a> Thou hast turned my mourning to dancing for me, Thou hast  loosed my sackcloth, And girdest me [with] joy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_30:12">30:12</a> So that honour doth praise Thee, and is not silent, O  Jehovah, my God, to the age I thank Thee!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:1">31:1</a> To the Overseer. -- A Psalm of David. In Thee, O Jehovah, I  have trusted, Let me not be ashamed to the age, In Thy  righteousness deliver me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:2">31:2</a> Incline unto me Thine ear hastily, deliver me, Be to me for  a strong rock, For a house of bulwarks to save me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:3">31:3</a> For my rock and my bulwark [art] Thou, For Thy name's sake  lead me and tend me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:4">31:4</a> Bring me out from the net that they hid for me, For Thou  [art] my strength.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:5">31:5</a> Into Thy hand I commit my spirit, Thou hast redeemed me,  Jehovah God of truth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:6">31:6</a> I have hated the observers of lying vanities, And I toward  Jehovah have been confident.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:7">31:7</a> I rejoice, and am glad in Thy kindness, In that Thou hast  seen mine affliction, Thou hast known in adversities my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:8">31:8</a> And Thou hast not shut me up, Into the hand of an enemy,  Thou hast caused my feet to stand in a broad place.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:9">31:9</a> Favour me, O Jehovah, for distress [is] to me, Mine eye, my  soul, and my body Have become old by provocation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:10">31:10</a> For my life hath been consumed in sorrow And my years in  sighing. Feeble because of mine iniquity hath been my strength,  And my bones have become old.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:11">31:11</a> Among all mine adversaries I have been a reproach, And to  my neighbours exceedingly, And a fear to mine acquaintances,  Those seeing me without -- fled from me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:12">31:12</a> I have been forgotten as dead out of mind, I have been as  a perishing vessel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:13">31:13</a> For I have heard an evil account of many, Fear [is] round  about. In their being united against me, To take my life they  have devised,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:14">31:14</a> And I on Thee -- I have trusted, O Jehovah, I have said,  `Thou [art] my God.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:15">31:15</a> In Thy hand [are] my times, Deliver me from the hand of my  enemies, And from my pursuers.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:16">31:16</a> Cause Thy face to shine on Thy servant, Save me in Thy  kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:17">31:17</a> O Jehovah, let me not be ashamed, For I have called Thee,  let the wicked be ashamed, Let them become silent to Sheol.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:18">31:18</a> Let lips of falsehood become dumb, That are speaking  against the righteous, Ancient sayings, in pride and contempt.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:19">31:19</a> How abundant is Thy goodness, That Thou hast laid up for  those fearing Thee,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:20">31:20</a> Thou hast wrought for those trusting in Thee, Before sons  of men. Thou hidest them in the secret place of Thy presence,  From artifices of man, Thou concealest them in a tabernacle,  From the strife of tongues.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:21">31:21</a> Blessed [is] Jehovah, For He hath made marvellous His  kindness To me in a city of bulwarks.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:22">31:22</a> And I -- I have said in my haste, `I have been cut off  from before Thine eyes,' But Thou hast heard the voice of my  supplications, In my crying unto Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:23">31:23</a> Love Jehovah, all ye His saints, Jehovah is keeping the  faithful, And recompensing abundantly a proud doer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_31:24">31:24</a> Be strong, and He strengtheneth your heart, All ye who are  waiting for Jehovah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:1">32:1</a> By David. -- An Instruction. O the happiness of him whose  transgression [is] forgiven, Whose sin is covered.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:2">32:2</a> O the happiness of a man, To whom Jehovah imputeth not  iniquity, And in whose spirit there is no deceit.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:3">32:3</a> When I have kept silence, become old have my bones, Through  my roaring all the day.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:4">32:4</a> When by day and by night Thy hand is heavy upon me, My  moisture hath been changed Into the droughts of summer. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:5">32:5</a> My sin I cause Thee to know, And mine iniquity I have not  covered. I have said, `I confess concerning My transgressions  to Jehovah,' And Thou -- Thou hast taken away, The iniquity of  my sin. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:6">32:6</a> For this doth every saintly one pray to Thee, As the time  to find. Surely at an overflowing of many waters, Unto him they  come not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:7">32:7</a> Thou [art] a hiding-place for me, From distress Thou dost  keep me, [With] songs of deliverance dost compass me. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:8">32:8</a> I cause thee to act wisely, And direct thee in the way that  thou goest, I cause mine eye to take counsel concerning thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:9">32:9</a> Be ye not as a horse -- as a mule, Without understanding,  With bridle and bit, its ornaments, to curb, Not to come near  unto thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:10">32:10</a> Many [are] the pains of the wicked; As to him who is  trusting in Jehovah, Kindness doth compass him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_32:11">32:11</a> Be glad in Jehovah, and rejoice, ye righteous, And sing,  all ye upright of heart!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:1">33:1</a> Sing, ye righteous, in Jehovah, For upright ones praise  [is] comely.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:2">33:2</a> Give ye thanks to Jehovah with a harp, With psaltery of ten  strings sing praise to Him,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:3">33:3</a> Sing ye to Him a new song, Play skilfully with shouting.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:4">33:4</a> For upright [is] the word of Jehovah, And all His work [is]  in faithfulness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:5">33:5</a> Loving righteousness and judgment, Of the kindness of  Jehovah is the earth full.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:6">33:6</a> By the word of Jehovah The heavens have been made, And by  the breath of His mouth all their host.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:7">33:7</a> Gathering as a heap the waters of the sea, Putting in  treasuries the depths.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:8">33:8</a> Afraid of Jehovah are all the earth, Of Him are all the  inhabitants of the world afraid.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:9">33:9</a> For He hath said, and it is, He hath commanded, and it  standeth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:10">33:10</a> Jehovah made void the counsel of nations, He disallowed  the thoughts of the peoples.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:11">33:11</a> The counsel of Jehovah to the age standeth, The thoughts  of His heart to all generations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:12">33:12</a> O the happiness of the nation whose God [is] Jehovah, Of  the people He did choose, For an inheritance to Him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:13">33:13</a> From the heavens hath Jehovah looked, He hath seen all the  sons of men.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:14">33:14</a> From the fixed place of His dwelling, He looked unto all  inhabitants of the earth;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:15">33:15</a> Who is forming their hearts together, Who is attending  unto all their works.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:16">33:16</a> The king is not saved by the multitude of a force. A  mighty man is not delivered, By abundance of power.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:17">33:17</a> A false thing [is] the horse for safety, And by the  abundance of his strength He doth not deliver.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:18">33:18</a> Lo, the eye of Jehovah [is] to those fearing Him, To those  waiting for His kindness,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:19">33:19</a> To deliver from death their soul, And to keep them alive  in famine.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:20">33:20</a> Our soul hath waited for Jehovah, Our help and our shield  [is] He,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:21">33:21</a> For in Him doth our heart rejoice, For in His holy name we  have trusted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_33:22">33:22</a> Let Thy kindness, O Jehovah, be upon us, As we have waited  for Thee!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:1">34:1</a> By David, in his changing his behaviour before Abimelech,  and he driveth him away, and he goeth. I do bless Jehovah at  all times, Continually His praise [is] in my mouth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:2">34:2</a> In Jehovah doth my soul boast herself, Hear do the humble  and rejoice.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:3">34:3</a> Ascribe ye greatness to Jehovah with me, And we exalt His  name together.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:4">34:4</a> I sought Jehovah, and He answered me, And from all my fears  did deliver me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:5">34:5</a> They looked expectingly unto Him, And they became bright,  And their faces are not ashamed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:6">34:6</a> This poor [one] called, and Jehovah heard, And from all his  distresses saved him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:7">34:7</a> A messenger of Jehovah is encamping, Round about those who  fear Him, And He armeth them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:8">34:8</a> Taste ye and see that Jehovah [is] good, O the happiness of  the man who trusteth in Him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:9">34:9</a> Fear Jehovah, ye His holy ones, For there is no lack to  those fearing Him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:10">34:10</a> Young lions have lacked and been hungry, And those seeking  Jehovah lack not any good,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:11">34:11</a> Come ye, children, hearken to me, The fear of Jehovah I do  teach you.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:12">34:12</a> Who [is] the man that is desiring life? Loving days to see  good?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:13">34:13</a> Keep thy tongue from evil, And thy lips from speaking  deceit.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:14">34:14</a> Turn aside from evil and do good, Seek peace and pursue  it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:15">34:15</a> The eyes of Jehovah [are] unto the righteous, And His ears  unto their cry.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:16">34:16</a> (The face of Jehovah [is] on doers of evil, To cut off  from earth their memorial.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:17">34:17</a> They cried, and Jehovah heard, And from all their  distresses delivered them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:18">34:18</a> Near [is] Jehovah to the broken of heart, And the bruised  of spirit He saveth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:19">34:19</a> Many [are] the evils of the righteous, Out of them all  doth Jehovah deliver him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:20">34:20</a> He is keeping all his bones, One of them hath not been  broken.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:21">34:21</a> Evil doth put to death the wicked, And those hating the  righteous are desolate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_34:22">34:22</a> Jehovah redeemeth the soul of His servants, And none  trusting in Him are desolate!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:1">35:1</a> By David. Strive, Jehovah, with my strivers, fight with my  fighters,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:2">35:2</a> Take hold of shield and buckler, and rise for my help,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:3">35:3</a> And draw out spear and lance, To meet my pursuers. Say to  my soul, `Thy salvation I [am].'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:4">35:4</a> They are ashamed and blush, those seeking my soul, Turned  backward and confounded, Those devising my evil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:5">35:5</a> They are as chaff before wind, And a messenger of Jehovah  driving away.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:6">35:6</a> Their way is darkness and slipperiness, And a messenger of  Jehovah their pursuer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:7">35:7</a> For without cause they hid for me their netpit, Without  cause they digged for my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:8">35:8</a> Meet him doth desolation -- he knoweth not, And his net  that he hid catcheth him, For desolation he falleth into it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:9">35:9</a> And my soul is joyful in Jehovah, It rejoiceth in His  salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:10">35:10</a> All my bones say, `Jehovah, who is like Thee, Delivering  the poor from the stronger than he, And the poor and needy from  his plunderer.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:11">35:11</a> Violent witnesses rise up, That which I have not known  they ask me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:12">35:12</a> They pay me evil for good, bereaving my soul,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:13">35:13</a> And I -- in their sickness my clothing [is] sackcloth, I  have humbled with fastings my soul, And my prayer unto my bosom  returneth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:14">35:14</a> As [if] a friend, as [if] my brother, I walked habitually,  As a mourner for a mother, Mourning I have bowed down.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:15">35:15</a> And -- in my halting they have rejoiced, And have been  gathered together, Gathered against me were the smiters, And I  have not known, They have rent, and they have not ceased;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:16">35:16</a> With profane ones, mockers in feasts, Gnashing against me  their teeth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:17">35:17</a> Lord, how long dost thou behold? Keep back my soul from  their desolations, From young lions my only one.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:18">35:18</a> I thank Thee in a great assembly, Among a mighty people I  praise Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:19">35:19</a> Mine enemies rejoice not over me [with] falsehood, Those  hating me without cause wink the eye.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:20">35:20</a> For they speak not peace, And against the quiet of the  land, Deceitful words they devise,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:21">35:21</a> And they enlarge against me their mouth, They said, `Aha,  aha, our eye hath seen.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:22">35:22</a> Thou hast seen, O Jehovah, Be not silent, O Lord -- be not  far from me,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:23">35:23</a> Stir up, and wake to my judgment, My God, and my Lord, to  my plea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:24">35:24</a> Judge me according to Thy righteousness, O Jehovah my God,  And they do not rejoice over me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:25">35:25</a> They do not say in their heart, `Aha, our desire.' They do  not say, `We swallowed him up.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:26">35:26</a> They are ashamed and confounded together, Who are  rejoicing at my evil. They put on shame and confusion, Who are  magnifying themselves against me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:27">35:27</a> They sing and rejoice, who are desiring my righteousness,  And they say continually, `Jehovah is magnified, Who is  desiring the peace of His servant.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_35:28">35:28</a> And my tongue uttereth Thy righteousness, All the day Thy  praise!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:1">36:1</a> To the Overseer. -- By a servant of Jehovah, by David. The  transgression of the wicked Is affirming within my heart, `Fear  of God is not before his eyes,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:2">36:2</a> For he made [it] smooth to himself in his eyes, To find his  iniquity to be hated.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:3">36:3</a> The words of his mouth [are] iniquity and deceit, He ceased  to act prudently -- to do good.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:4">36:4</a> Iniquity he deviseth on his bed, He stationeth himself on a  way not good, Evil he doth not refuse.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:5">36:5</a> O Jehovah, in the heavens [is] Thy kindness, Thy  faithfulness [is] unto the clouds.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:6">36:6</a> Thy righteousness [is] as mountains of God, Thy judgments  [are] a great deep. Man and beast Thou savest, O Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:7">36:7</a> How precious [is] Thy kindness, O God, And the sons of men  In the shadow of Thy wings do trust.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:8">36:8</a> They are filled from the fatness of Thy house, And the  stream of Thy delights Thou dost cause them to drink.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:9">36:9</a> For with Thee [is] a fountain of life, In Thy light we see  light.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:10">36:10</a> Draw out Thy kindness to those knowing Thee, And Thy  righteousness to the upright of heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:11">36:11</a> Let not a foot of pride meet me, And a hand of the wicked  let not move me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_36:12">36:12</a> There have workers of iniquity fallen, They have been  overthrown, And have not been able to arise!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:1">37:1</a> By David. Do not fret because of evil doers, Be not envious  against doers of iniquity,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:2">37:2</a> For as grass speedily they are cut off, And as the  greenness of the tender grass do fade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:3">37:3</a> Trust in Jehovah, and do good, Dwell [in] the land, and  enjoy faithfulness,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:4">37:4</a> And delight thyself on Jehovah, And He giveth to thee the  petitions of thy heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:5">37:5</a> Roll on Jehovah thy way, And trust upon Him, and He  worketh,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:6">37:6</a> And hath brought out as light thy righteousness, And thy  judgment as noon-day.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:7">37:7</a> Be silent for Jehovah, and stay thyself for Him, Do not  fret because of him Who is making prosperous his way, Because  of a man doing wicked devices.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:8">37:8</a> Desist from anger, and forsake fury, Fret not thyself only  to do evil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:9">37:9</a> For evil doers are cut off, As to those waiting on Jehovah,  they possess the land.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:10">37:10</a> And yet a little, and the wicked is not, And thou hast  considered his place, and it is not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:11">37:11</a> And the humble do possess the land, And they have  delighted themselves In the abundance of peace.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:12">37:12</a> The wicked is devising against the righteous, And gnashing  against him his teeth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:13">37:13</a> The Lord doth laugh at him, For He hath seen that his day  cometh.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:14">37:14</a> A sword have the wicked opened, And they have trodden  their bow, To cause to fall the poor and needy, To slaughter  the upright of the way.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:15">37:15</a> Their sword doth enter into their own heart, And their  bows are shivered.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:16">37:16</a> Better [is] the little of the righteous, Than the store of  many wicked.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:17">37:17</a> For the arms of the wicked are shivered, And Jehovah is  sustaining the righteous.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:18">37:18</a> Jehovah knoweth the days of the perfect, And their  inheritance is -- to the age.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:19">37:19</a> They are not ashamed in a time of evil, And in days of  famine they are satisfied.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:20">37:20</a> But the wicked perish, and the enemies of Jehovah, As the  preciousness of lambs, Have been consumed, In smoke they have  been consumed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:21">37:21</a> The wicked is borrowing and repayeth not, And the  righteous is gracious and giving.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:22">37:22</a> For His blessed ones do possess the land, And His reviled  ones are cut off.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:23">37:23</a> From Jehovah [are] the steps of a man, They have been  prepared, And his way he desireth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:24">37:24</a> When he falleth, he is not cast down, For Jehovah is  sustaining his hand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:25">37:25</a> Young I have been, I have also become old, And I have not  seen the righteous forsaken, And his seed seeking bread.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:26">37:26</a> All the day he is gracious and lending, And his seed [is]  for a blessing.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:27">37:27</a> Turn aside from evil, and do good, and dwell to the age.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:28">37:28</a> For Jehovah is loving judgment, And He doth not forsake  His saintly ones, To the age they have been kept, And the seed  of the wicked is cut off.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:29">37:29</a> The righteous possess the land, And they dwell for ever on  it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:30">37:30</a> The mouth of the righteous uttereth wisdom, And his tongue  speaketh judgment.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:31">37:31</a> The law of his God [is] his heart, His steps do not slide.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:32">37:32</a> The wicked is watching for the righteous, And is seeking  to put him to death.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:33">37:33</a> Jehovah doth not leave him in his hand, Nor condemn him in  his being judged.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:34">37:34</a> Look unto Jehovah, and keep His way, And He doth exalt  thee to possess the land, In the wicked being cut off -- thou  seest!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:35">37:35</a> I have seen the wicked terrible, And spreading as a green  native plant,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:36">37:36</a> And he passeth away, and lo, he is not, And I seek him,  and he is not found!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:37">37:37</a> Observe the perfect, and see the upright, For the latter  end of each [is] peace.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:38">37:38</a> And transgressors were destroyed together, The latter end  of the wicked was cut off.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:39">37:39</a> And the salvation of the righteous [is] from Jehovah,  Their strong place in a time of adversity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_37:40">37:40</a> And Jehovah doth help them and deliver them, He delivereth  them from the wicked, And saveth them, Because they trusted in  Him!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:1">38:1</a> A Psalm of David, `To cause to remember.' Jehovah, in Thy  wrath reprove me not, Nor in Thy fury chastise me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:2">38:2</a> For Thine arrows have come down on me, And Thou lettest  down upon me Thy hand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:3">38:3</a> Soundness is not in my flesh, Because of Thine indignation,  Peace is not in my bones because of my sin.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:4">38:4</a> For mine iniquities have passed over my head, As a heavy  burden -- too heavy for me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:5">38:5</a> Stunk -- become corrupt have my wounds, Because of my  folly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:6">38:6</a> I have been bent down, I have been bowed down -- unto  excess, All the day I have gone mourning.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:7">38:7</a> For my flanks have been full of drought, And soundness is  not in my flesh.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:8">38:8</a> I have been feeble and smitten -- unto excess, I have  roared from disquietude of heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:9">38:9</a> Lord, before Thee [is] all my desire, And my sighing from  Thee hath not been hid.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:10">38:10</a> My heart [is] panting, my power hath forsaken me, And the  light of mine eyes, Even they are not with me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:11">38:11</a> My lovers and my friends over-against my plague stand. And  my neighbours afar off have stood.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:12">38:12</a> And those seeking my soul lay a snare, And those seeking  my evil Have spoken mischievous things, And they do deceits  meditate all the day.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:13">38:13</a> And I, as deaf, hear not. And as a dumb one who openeth  not his mouth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:14">38:14</a> Yea, I am as a man who heareth not, And in his mouth are  no reproofs.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:15">38:15</a> Because for Thee, O Jehovah, I have waited, Thou dost  answer, O Lord my God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:16">38:16</a> When I said, `Lest they rejoice over me, In the slipping  of my foot against me they magnified themselves.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:17">38:17</a> For I am ready to halt, And my pain [is] before me  continually.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:18">38:18</a> For mine iniquity I declare, I am sorry for my sin.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:19">38:19</a> And mine enemies [are] lively, They have been strong, and  those hating me without cause, Have been multiplied.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:20">38:20</a> And those paying evil for good accuse me, Because of my  pursuing good.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:21">38:21</a> Do not forsake me, O Jehovah, My God, be not far from me,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_38:22">38:22</a> Haste to help me, O Lord, my salvation!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:1">39:1</a> To the Overseer, to Jeduthun. -- A Psalm of David. I have  said, `I observe my ways, Against sinning with my tongue, I  keep for my mouth a curb, while the wicked [is] before me.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:2">39:2</a> I was dumb [with] silence, I kept silent from good, and my  pain is excited.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:3">39:3</a> Hot [is] my heart within me, In my meditating doth the fire  burn, I have spoken with my tongue.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:4">39:4</a> `Cause me to know, O Jehovah, mine end, And the measure of  my days -- what it [is],' I know how frail I [am].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:5">39:5</a> Lo, handbreadths Thou hast made my days, And mine age [is]  as nothing before Thee, Only, all vanity [is] every man set up.  Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:6">39:6</a> Only, in an image doth each walk habitually, Only, [in]  vain, they are disquieted, He heapeth up and knoweth not who  gathereth them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:7">39:7</a> And, now, what have I expected? O Lord, my hope -- it [is]  of Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:8">39:8</a> From all my transgressions deliver me, A reproach of the  fool make me not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:9">39:9</a> I have been dumb, I open not my mouth, Because Thou -- Thou  hast done [it].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:10">39:10</a> Turn aside from off me Thy stroke, From the striving of  Thy hand I have been consumed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:11">39:11</a> With reproofs against iniquity, Thou hast corrected man,  And dost waste as a moth his desirableness, Only, vanity [is]  every man. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:12">39:12</a> Hear my prayer, O Jehovah, And [to] my cry give ear, Unto  my tear be not silent, For a sojourner I [am] with Thee, A  settler like all my fathers.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_39:13">39:13</a> Look from me, and I brighten up before I go and am not!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:1">40:1</a> To the Overseer. -- A Psalm of David. I have diligently  expected Jehovah, And He inclineth to me, and heareth my cry,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:2">40:2</a> And He doth cause me to come up From a pit of desolation --  from mire of mud, And He raiseth up on a rock my feet, He is  establishing my steps.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:3">40:3</a> And He putteth in my mouth a new song, `Praise to our God.'  Many do see and fear, and trust in Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:4">40:4</a> O the happiness of the man Who hath made Jehovah his trust,  And hath not turned unto the proud, And those turning aside to  lies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:5">40:5</a> Much hast Thou done, Jehovah my God; Thy wonders and Thy  thoughts toward us, There is none to arrange unto Thee, I  declare and speak: They have been more than to be numbered.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:6">40:6</a> Sacrifice and present Thou hast not desired, Ears Thou hast  prepared for me, Burnt and sin-offering Thou hast not asked.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:7">40:7</a> Then said I, `Lo, I have come,' In the roll of the book it  is written of me,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:8">40:8</a> To do Thy pleasure, my God, I have delighted, And Thy law  [is] within my heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:9">40:9</a> I have proclaimed tidings of righteousness In the great  assembly, lo, my lips I restrain not, O Jehovah, Thou hast  known.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:10">40:10</a> Thy righteousness I have not concealed In the midst of my  heart, Thy faithfulness and Thy salvation I have told, I have  not hidden Thy kindness and Thy truth, To the great assembly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:11">40:11</a> Thou, O Jehovah, restrainest not Thy mercies from me, Thy  kindness and Thy truth do continually keep me.</p>
