 <p><a name="an_40:12">40:12</a> For compassed me have evils innumerable, Overtaken me have  mine iniquities, And I have not been able to see; They have  been more than the hairs of my head, And my heart hath forsaken  me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:13">40:13</a> Be pleased, O Jehovah, to deliver me, O Jehovah, for my  help make haste.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:14">40:14</a> They are ashamed and confounded together, Who are seeking  my soul to destroy it, They are turned backward, And are  ashamed, who are desiring my evil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:15">40:15</a> They are desolate because of their shame, Who are saying  to me, `Aha, aha.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:16">40:16</a> All seeking Thee rejoice and are glad in Thee, Those  loving Thy salvation say continually, `Jehovah is magnified.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_40:17">40:17</a> And I [am] poor and needy, The Lord doth devise for me. My  help and my deliverer [art] Thou, O my God, tarry Thou not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:1">41:1</a> To the Overseer. -- A Psalm of David. O the happiness of  him Who is acting wisely unto the poor, In a day of evil doth  Jehovah deliver him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:2">41:2</a> Jehovah doth preserve him and revive him, He is happy in  the land, And Thou givest him not into the will of his enemies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:3">41:3</a> Jehovah supporteth on a couch of sickness, All his bed Thou  hast turned in his weakness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:4">41:4</a> I -- I said, `O Jehovah, favour me, Heal my soul, for I did  sin against Thee,'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:5">41:5</a> Mine enemies say evil of me: When he dieth -- his name hath  perished!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:6">41:6</a> And if he came to see -- vanity he speaketh, His heart  gathereth iniquity to itself, He goeth out -- at the street he  speaketh.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:7">41:7</a> All hating me whisper together against me, Against me they  devise evil to me:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:8">41:8</a> A thing of Belial is poured out on him, And because he lay  down he riseth not again.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:9">41:9</a> Even mine ally, in whom I trusted, One eating my bread,  made great the heel against me,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:10">41:10</a> And Thou, Jehovah, favour me, And cause me to rise, And I  give recompence to them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:11">41:11</a> By this I have known, That Thou hast delighted in me,  Because my enemy shouteth not over me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:12">41:12</a> As to me, in mine integrity, Thou hast taken hold upon me,  And causest me to stand before Thee to the age.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_41:13">41:13</a> Blessed [is] Jehovah, God of Israel, From the age -- and  unto the age. Amen and Amen.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:1">42:1</a> To the Overseer. -- An Instruction. By sons of Korah. As a  hart doth pant for streams of water, So my soul panteth toward  Thee, O God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:2">42:2</a> My soul thirsted for God, for the living God, When do I  enter and see the face of God?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:3">42:3</a> My tear hath been to me bread day and night, In their  saying unto me all the day, `Where [is] thy God?'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:4">42:4</a> These I remember, and pour out my soul in me, For I pass  over into the booth, I go softly with them unto the house of  God, With the voice of singing and confession, The multitude  keeping feast!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:5">42:5</a> What! bowest thou thyself, O my soul? Yea, art thou  troubled within me? Wait for God, for still I confess Him: The  salvation of my countenance -- My God!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:6">42:6</a> In me doth my soul bow itself, Therefore I remember Thee  from the land of Jordan, And of the Hermons, from the hill  Mizar.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:7">42:7</a> Deep unto deep is calling At the noise of Thy  water-spouts, All Thy breakers and Thy billows passed over me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:8">42:8</a> By day Jehovah commandeth His kindness, And by night a song  [is] with me, A prayer to the God of my life.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:9">42:9</a> I say to God my rock, `Why hast Thou forgotten me? Why go I  mourning in the oppression of an enemy?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:10">42:10</a> With a sword in my bones Have mine adversaries reproached  me, In their saying unto me all the day, `Where [is] thy God?'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_42:11">42:11</a> What! bowest thou thyself, O my soul? And what! art thou  troubled within me? Wait for God, for still I confess Him, The  salvation of my countenance, and my God!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:1">43:1</a> Judge me, O God, And plead my cause against a nation not  pious, From a man of deceit and perverseness Thou dost deliver  me,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:2">43:2</a> For thou [art] the God of my strength. Why hast Thou cast  me off? Why mourning do I go up and down, In the oppression of  an enemy?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:3">43:3</a> Send forth Thy light and Thy truth, They -- they lead me,  they bring me in, Unto Thy holy hill, and unto Thy tabernacles.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:4">43:4</a> And I go in unto the altar of God, Unto God, the joy of my  rejoicing. And I thank Thee with a harp, O God, my God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_43:5">43:5</a> What! bowest thou thyself, O my soul? And what! art thou  troubled within me? Wait for God, for still I confess Him, The  salvation of my countenance, and my God!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:1">44:1</a> To the Overseer. -- By sons of Korah. An Instruction. O  God, with our ears we have heard, Our fathers have recounted to  us, The work Thou didst work in their days, In the days of old.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:2">44:2</a> Thou, [with] Thy hand, nations hast dispossessed. And Thou  dost plant them. Thou afflictest peoples, and sendest them  away.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:3">44:3</a> For, not by their sword Possessed they the land, And their  arm gave not salvation to them, But Thy right hand, and Thine  arm, And the light of Thy countenance, Because Thou hadst  accepted them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:4">44:4</a> Thou [art] He, my king, O God, Command the deliverances of  Jacob.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:5">44:5</a> By Thee our adversaries we do push, By Thy name tread down  our withstanders,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:6">44:6</a> For, not in my bow do I trust, And my sword doth not save  me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:7">44:7</a> For Thou hast saved us from our adversaries, And those  hating us Thou hast put to shame.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:8">44:8</a> In God we have boasted all the day, And Thy name to the age  we thank. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:9">44:9</a> In anger Thou hast cast off and causest us to blush, And  goest not forth with our hosts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:10">44:10</a> Thou causest us to turn backward from an adversary, And  those hating us, Have spoiled for themselves.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:11">44:11</a> Thou makest us food like sheep, And among nations Thou  hast scattered us.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:12">44:12</a> Thou sellest Thy people -- without wealth, And hast not  become great by their price.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:13">44:13</a> Thou makest us a reproach to our neighbours, A scorn and a  reproach to our surrounders.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:14">44:14</a> Thou makest us a simile among nations, A shaking of the  head among peoples.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:15">44:15</a> All the day my confusion [is] before me, And the shame of  my face hath covered me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:16">44:16</a> Because of the voice of a reproacher and reviler, Because  of an enemy and a self-avenger.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:17">44:17</a> All this met us, and we did not forget Thee, Nor have we  dealt falsely in Thy covenant.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:18">44:18</a> We turn not backward our heart, Nor turn aside doth our  step from Thy path.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:19">44:19</a> But Thou hast smitten us in a place of dragons, And dost  cover us over with death-shade.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:20">44:20</a> If we have forgotten the name of our God, And spread our  hands to a strange God,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:21">44:21</a> Doth not God search out this? For He knoweth the secrets  of the heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:22">44:22</a> Surely, for Thy sake we have been slain all the day,  Reckoned as sheep of the slaughter.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:23">44:23</a> Stir up -- why dost Thou sleep, O Lord? Awake, cast us not  off for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:24">44:24</a> Why Thy face hidest Thou? Thou forgettest our afflictions  and our oppression,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:25">44:25</a> For bowed to the dust hath our soul, Cleaved to the earth  hath our belly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_44:26">44:26</a> Arise, a help to us, And ransom us for thy kindness' sake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:1">45:1</a> To the Overseer. -- `On the Lilies.' -- By sons of Korah.  -- An Instruction. -- A song of loves. My heart hath indited a  good thing, I am telling my works to a king, My tongue [is] the  pen of a speedy writer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:2">45:2</a> Thou hast been beautified above the sons of men, Grace hath  been poured into thy lips, Therefore hath God blessed thee to  the age.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:3">45:3</a> Gird Thy sword upon the thigh, O mighty, Thy glory and Thy  majesty!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:4">45:4</a> As to Thy majesty -- prosper! -- ride! Because of truth,  and meekness -- righteousness, And Thy right hand showeth Thee  fearful things.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:5">45:5</a> Thine arrows [are] sharp, -- Peoples fall under Thee -- In  the heart of the enemies of the king.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:6">45:6</a> Thy throne, O God, [is] age-during, and for ever, A sceptre  of uprightness [Is] the sceptre of Thy kingdom.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:7">45:7</a> Thou hast loved righteousness and hatest wickedness,  Therefore God, thy God, hath anointed thee, Oil of joy above  thy companions.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:8">45:8</a> Myrrh and aloes, cassia! all thy garments, Out of palaces  of ivory Stringed instruments have made thee glad.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:9">45:9</a> Daughters of kings [are] among thy precious ones, A queen  hath stood at thy right hand, In pure gold of Ophir.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:10">45:10</a> Hearken, O daughter, and see, incline thine ear, And  forget thy people, and thy father's house,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:11">45:11</a> And the king doth desire thy beauty, Because he [is] thy  lord -- bow thyself to him,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:12">45:12</a> And the daughter of Tyre with a present, The rich of the  people do appease thy face.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:13">45:13</a> All glory [is] the daughter of the king within, Of  gold-embroidered work [is] her clothing.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:14">45:14</a> In divers colours she is brought to the king, Virgins --  after her -- her companions, Are brought to thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:15">45:15</a> They are brought with joy and gladness, They come into the  palace of the king.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:16">45:16</a> Instead of thy fathers are thy sons, Thou dost appoint  them for princes in all the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_45:17">45:17</a> I make mention of Thy name in all generations, Therefore  do peoples praise Thee, To the age, and for ever!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:1">46:1</a> To the Overseer. -- By sons of Korah. `For the Virgins.' --  A song. God [is] to us a refuge and strength, A help in  adversities found most surely.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:2">46:2</a> Therefore we fear not in the changing of earth, And in the  slipping of mountains Into the heart of the seas.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:3">46:3</a> Roar -- troubled are its waters, Mountains they shake in  its pride. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:4">46:4</a> A river -- its rivulets rejoice the city of God, Thy holy  place of the tabernacles of the Most High.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:5">46:5</a> God [is] in her midst -- she is not moved, God doth help  her at the turn of the morn!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:6">46:6</a> Troubled have been nations, Moved have been kingdoms, He  hath given forth with His voice, earth melteth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:7">46:7</a> Jehovah of Hosts [is] with us, A tower for us [is] the God  of Jacob. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:8">46:8</a> Come ye, see the works of Jehovah, Who hath done  astonishing things in the earth,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:9">46:9</a> Causing wars to cease, Unto the end of the earth, the bow  he shivereth, And the spear He hath cut asunder, Chariots he  doth burn with fire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:10">46:10</a> Desist, and know that I [am] God, I am exalted among  nations, I am exalted in the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_46:11">46:11</a> Jehovah of hosts [is] with us, A tower for us [is] the God  of Jacob! Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:1">47:1</a> To the Overseer. -- By sons of Korah. A Psalm. All ye  peoples, clap the hand, Shout to God with a voice of singing,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:2">47:2</a> For Jehovah Most High [is] fearful, A great king over all  the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:3">47:3</a> He leadeth peoples under us, and nations under our feet.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:4">47:4</a> He doth choose for us our inheritance, The excellency of  Jacob that He loves. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:5">47:5</a> God hath gone up with a shout, Jehovah with the sound of a  trumpet.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:6">47:6</a> Praise God -- praise -- give praise to our king, praise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:7">47:7</a> For king of all the earth [is] God, Give praise, O  understanding one.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:8">47:8</a> God hath reigned over nations, God hath sat on His holy  throne,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_47:9">47:9</a> Nobles of peoples have been gathered, [With] the people of  the God of Abraham, For to God [are] the shields of earth,  Greatly hath He been exalted!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:1">48:1</a> A Song, a Psalm, by sons of Korah. Great [is] Jehovah, and  praised greatly, In the city of our God -- His holy hill.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:2">48:2</a> Beautiful [for] elevation, A joy of all the land, [is]  Mount Zion, The sides of the north, the city of a great king.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:3">48:3</a> God in her high places is known for a tower.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:4">48:4</a> For, lo, the kings met, they passed by together,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:5">48:5</a> They have seen -- so they have marvelled, They have been  troubled, they were hastened away.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:6">48:6</a> Trembling hath seized them there, Pain, as of a travailing  woman.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:7">48:7</a> By an east wind Thou shiverest ships of Tarshish.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:8">48:8</a> As we have heard, so we have seen, In the city of Jehovah  of hosts, In the city of our God, God doth establish her -- to  the age. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:9">48:9</a> We have thought, O God, of Thy kindness, In the midst of  Thy temple,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:10">48:10</a> As [is] Thy name, O God, so [is] Thy praise, Over the ends  of the earth, Righteousness hath filled Thy right hand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:11">48:11</a> Rejoice doth Mount Zion, The daughters of Judah are  joyful, For the sake of Thy judgments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:12">48:12</a> Compass Zion, and go round her, count her towers,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:13">48:13</a> Set your heart to her bulwark, Consider her high places,  So that ye recount to a later generation,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_48:14">48:14</a> That this God [is] our God -- To the age and for ever, He  -- he doth lead us over death!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:1">49:1</a> To the Overseer. -- By sons of Korah. A Psalm. Hear this,  all ye peoples, Give ear, all ye inhabitants of the world.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:2">49:2</a> Both low and high, together rich and needy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:3">49:3</a> My mouth speaketh wise things, And the meditations of my  heart [are] things of understanding.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:4">49:4</a> I incline to a simile mine ear, I open with a harp my  riddle:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:5">49:5</a> Why do I fear in days of evil? The iniquity of my  supplanters doth compass me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:6">49:6</a> Those trusting on their wealth, And in the multitude of  their riches, Do shew themselves foolish.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:7">49:7</a> A brother doth no one at all ransom, He doth not give to  God his atonement.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:8">49:8</a> And precious [is] the redemption of their soul, And it hath  ceased -- to the age.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:9">49:9</a> And still he liveth for ever, He seeth not the pit.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:10">49:10</a> For he seeth wise men die, Together the foolish and  brutish perish, And have left to others their wealth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:11">49:11</a> Their heart [is]: Their houses [are] to the age, Their  tabernacles to all generations. They proclaimed their names  over the lands.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:12">49:12</a> And man in honour doth not remain, He hath been like the  beasts, they have been cut off.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:13">49:13</a> This their way [is] folly for them, And their posterity  with their sayings are pleased. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:14">49:14</a> As sheep for Sheol they have set themselves, Death doth  afflict them, And the upright rule over them in the morning,  And their form [is] for consumption. Sheol [is] a dwelling for  him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:15">49:15</a> Only, God doth ransom my soul from the hand of Sheol, For  He doth receive me. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:16">49:16</a> Fear not, when one maketh wealth, When the honour of his  house is abundant,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:17">49:17</a> For at his death he receiveth nothing, His honour goeth  not down after him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:18">49:18</a> For his soul in his life he blesseth, (And they praise  thee when thou dost well for thyself.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:19">49:19</a> It cometh to the generation of his fathers, For ever they  see not the light.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_49:20">49:20</a> Man in honour, who understandest not, Hath been like the  beasts, they have been cut off!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:1">50:1</a> A Psalm of Asaph. The God of gods -- Jehovah -- hath  spoken, And He calleth to the earth From the rising of the sun  unto its going in.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:2">50:2</a> From Zion, the perfection of beauty, God shone.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:3">50:3</a> Our God cometh, and is not silent, Fire before Him doth  devour, And round about him it hath been very tempestuous.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:4">50:4</a> He doth call unto the heavens from above, And unto the  earth, to judge His people.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:5">50:5</a> Gather ye to Me My saints, Making covenant with Me over a  sacrifice.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:6">50:6</a> And the heavens declare His righteousness, For God Himself  [is] judge. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:7">50:7</a> Hear, O My people, and I speak, O Israel, and I testify  against thee, God, thy God [am] I.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:8">50:8</a> Not for thy sacrifices do I reprove thee, Yea, thy  burnt-offerings [Are] before Me continually.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:9">50:9</a> I take not from thy house a bullock, From thy folds  he goats.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:10">50:10</a> For Mine [is] every beast of the forest, The cattle on the  hills of oxen.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:11">50:11</a> I have known every fowl of the mountains, And the wild  beast of the field [is] with Me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:12">50:12</a> If I am hungry I tell not to thee, For Mine [is] the world  and its fulness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:13">50:13</a> Do I eat the flesh of bulls, And drink the blood of  he-goats?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:14">50:14</a> Sacrifice to God confession, And complete to the Most High  thy vows.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:15">50:15</a> And call Me in a day of adversity, I deliver thee, and  thou honourest Me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:16">50:16</a> And to the wicked hath God said: What to thee -- to  recount My statutes? That thou liftest up My covenant on thy  mouth?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:17">50:17</a> Yea, thou hast hated instruction, And dost cast My words  behind thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:18">50:18</a> If thou hast seen a thief, Then thou art pleased with him,  And with adulterers [is] thy portion.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:19">50:19</a> Thy mouth thou hast sent forth with evil, And thy tongue  joineth deceit together,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:20">50:20</a> Thou sittest, against thy brother thou speakest, Against a  son of thy mother givest slander.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:21">50:21</a> These thou didst, and I kept silent, Thou hast thought  that I am like thee, I reprove thee, and set in array before  thine eyes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:22">50:22</a> Understand this, I pray you, Ye who are forgetting God,  Lest I tear, and there is no deliverer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_50:23">50:23</a> He who is sacrificing praise honoureth Me, As to him who  maketh a way, I cause him to look on the salvation of God!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:1">51:1</a> To the Overseer. -- A Psalm of David, in the coming inn  unto him of Nathan the prophet, when he hath gone in unto  Bath-Sheba. Favour me, O God, according to Thy kindness,  According to the abundance of Thy mercies, Blot out my  transgressions.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:2">51:2</a> Thoroughly wash me from mine iniquity, And from my sin  cleanse me,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:3">51:3</a> For my transgressions I do know, And my sin [is] before me  continually.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:4">51:4</a> Against Thee, Thee only, I have sinned, And done the evil  thing in Thine eyes, So that Thou art righteous in Thy words,  Thou art pure in Thy judging.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:5">51:5</a> Lo, in iniquity I have been brought forth, And in sin doth  my mother conceive me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:6">51:6</a> Lo, truth Thou hast desired in the inward parts, And in the  hidden part Wisdom Thou causest me to know.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:7">51:7</a> Thou cleansest me with hyssop and I am clean, Washest me,  and than snow I am whiter.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:8">51:8</a> Thou causest me to hear joy and gladness, Thou makest  joyful bones Thou hast bruised.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:9">51:9</a> Hide Thy face from my sin. And all mine iniquities blot  out.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:10">51:10</a> A clean heart prepare for me, O God, And a right spirit  renew within me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:11">51:11</a> Cast me not forth from Thy presence, And Thy Holy Spirit  take not from me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:12">51:12</a> Restore to me the joy of Thy salvation, And a willing  spirit doth sustain me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:13">51:13</a> I teach transgressors Thy ways, And sinners unto Thee do  return.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:14">51:14</a> Deliver me from blood, O God, God of my salvation, My  tongue singeth of Thy righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:15">51:15</a> O Lord, my lips thou dost open, And my mouth declareth Thy  praise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:16">51:16</a> For Thou desirest not sacrifice, or I give [it],  Burnt-offering Thou acceptest not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:17">51:17</a> The sacrifices of God [are] a broken spirit, A heart  broken and bruised, O God, Thou dost not despise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:18">51:18</a> Do good in Thy good pleasure with Zion, Thou dost build  the walls of Jerusalem.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_51:19">51:19</a> Then Thou desirest sacrifices of righteousness,  Burnt-offering, and whole burnt-offering, Then they offer  bullocks on thine altar!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:1">52:1</a> To the Overseer. -- An instruction, by David, in the coming  in of Doeg the Edomite, and he declareth to Saul, and saith to  him, `David came in unto the house of Ahimelech.' What,  boasteth thou in evil, O mighty one? The kindness of God [is]  all the day.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:2">52:2</a> Mischiefs doth thy tongue devise, Like a sharp razor,  working deceit.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:3">52:3</a> Thou hast loved evil rather than good, Lying, than speaking  righteousness. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:4">52:4</a> Thou hast loved all devouring words, O thou deceitful  tongue.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:5">52:5</a> Also -- God doth break thee down for ever, Taketh thee, and  pulleth thee out of the tent, And He hath uprooted thee Out of  the land of the living. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:6">52:6</a> And the righteous see, And fear, and laugh at him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:7">52:7</a> `Lo, the man who maketh not God his strong place, And  trusteth in the abundance of his riches, He is strong in his  mischiefs.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:8">52:8</a> And I, as a green olive in the house of God, I have trusted  in the kindness of God, To the age and for ever,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_52:9">52:9</a> I thank Thee to the age, because Thou hast done [it], And I  wait [on] Thy name for [it is] good before Thy saints!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:1">53:1</a> To the Overseer. -- `On a disease.' -- An instruction, by  David. A fool said in his heart, `There is no God.' They have  done corruptly, Yea, they have done abominable iniquity, There  is none doing good.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:2">53:2</a> God from the heavens looked on the sons of men, To see if  there be an understanding one, [One] seeking God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:3">53:3</a> Every one went back, together they became filthy, There is  none doing good -- not even one.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:4">53:4</a> Have not workers of iniquity known, Those eating my people  have eaten bread, God they have not called.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:5">53:5</a> There they feared a fear -- there was no fear, For God hath  scattered the bones of him Who is encamping against thee, Thou  hast put to shame, For God hath despised them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_53:6">53:6</a> Who doth give from Zion the salvation of Israel? When God  turneth back [to] a captivity of His people, Jacob doth rejoice  -- Israel is glad!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:1">54:1</a> To the Overseer with stringed instruments. -- An  instruction, by David, in the coming in of the Ziphim, and they  say to Saul, `Is not David hiding himself with us?' O God, by  Thy name save me, and by Thy might judge me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:2">54:2</a> O God, hear my prayer, Give ear to the sayings of my mouth,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:3">54:3</a> For strangers have risen up against me And terrible ones  have sought my soul, They have not set God before them. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:4">54:4</a> Lo, God [is] a helper to me, The Lord [is] with those  supporting my soul,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:5">54:5</a> Turn back doth the evil thing to mine enemies, In Thy truth  cut them off.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:6">54:6</a> With a free will-offering I sacrifice to Thee, I thank Thy  name, O Jehovah, for [it is] good,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_54:7">54:7</a> For, from all adversity He delivered me, And on mine  enemies hath mine eye looked!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:1">55:1</a> To the Overseer with stringed instruments. -- An  instruction, by David. Give ear, O God, [to] my prayer, And  hide not from my supplication.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:2">55:2</a> Attend to me, and answer me, I mourn in my meditation, and  make a noise,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:3">55:3</a> Because of the voice of an enemy, Because of the oppression  of the wicked, For they cause sorrow to move against me, And in  anger they hate me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:4">55:4</a> My heart is pained within me, And terrors of death have  fallen on me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:5">55:5</a> Fear and trembling come in to me, And horror doth cover me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:6">55:6</a> And I say, `Who doth give to me a pinion as a dove? I fly  away and rest,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:7">55:7</a> Lo, I move far off, I lodge in a wilderness. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:8">55:8</a> I hasten escape for myself, From a rushing wind, from a  whirlwind.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:9">55:9</a> Swallow up, O Lord, divide their tongue, For I saw violence  and strife in a city.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:10">55:10</a> By day and by night they go round it, on its walls. Both  iniquity and perverseness [are] in its midst,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:11">55:11</a> Mischiefs [are] in its midst. Fraud and deceit depart not  from its street.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:12">55:12</a> For an enemy reproacheth me not, or I bear [it], He who is  hating me Hath not magnified himself against me, Or I hide from  him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:13">55:13</a> But thou, a man -- as mine equal, My familiar friend, and  mine acquaintance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:14">55:14</a> When together we sweeten counsel, Into the house of God we  walk in company.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:15">55:15</a> Desolations [are] upon them, They go down [to] Sheol --  alive, For wickedness [is] in their dwelling, in their midst.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:16">55:16</a> I -- to God I call, and Jehovah saveth me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:17">55:17</a> Evening, and morning, and noon, I meditate, and make a  noise, and He heareth my voice,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:18">55:18</a> He hath ransomed in peace my soul From him who is near to  me, For with the multitude they were with me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:19">55:19</a> God doth hear and afflict them, And He sitteth of old.  Selah. Because they have no changes, and fear not God,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:20">55:20</a> He hath sent forth his hands against his well-wishers, He  hath polluted his covenant.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:21">55:21</a> Sweeter than honey hath been his mouth, And his heart [is]  war! Softer have been his words than oil, And they [are] drawn  [swords].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:22">55:22</a> Cast on Jehovah that which He hath given thee, And He doth  sustain thee, He doth not suffer for ever the moving of the  righteous.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_55:23">55:23</a> And Thou, O God, dost bring them down To a pit of  destruction, Men of blood and deceit reach not to half their  days, And I -- I do trust in Thee!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:1">56:1</a> To the Overseer. -- `On the Dumb Dove far off.' -- A secret  treasure of David, in the Philistines' taking hold of him in  Gath. Favour me, O God, for man swallowed me up, All the day  fighting he oppresseth me,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:2">56:2</a> Mine enemies have swallowed up all the day, For many [are]  fighting against me, O most High,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:3">56:3</a> The day I am afraid I am confident toward Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:4">56:4</a> In God I praise His word, in God I have trusted, I fear not  what flesh doth to me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:5">56:5</a> All the day they wrest my words, Concerning me all their  thoughts [are] for evil,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:6">56:6</a> They assemble, they hide, they watch my heels, When they  have expected my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:7">56:7</a> By iniquity they escape, In anger the peoples put down, O  God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:8">56:8</a> My wandering Thou hast counted, Thou -- place Thou my tear  in Thy bottle, Are they not in Thy book?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:9">56:9</a> Then turn back do mine enemies in the day I call. This I  have known, that God [is] for me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:10">56:10</a> In God I praise the word, In Jehovah I praise the word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:11">56:11</a> In God I trusted, I fear not what man doth to me,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:12">56:12</a> On me, O God, [are] Thy vows, I repay thank-offerings to  Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_56:13">56:13</a> For Thou hast delivered my soul from death, Dost Thou not  my feet from falling? To walk habitually before God in the  light of the living!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:1">57:1</a> To the Overseer. -- `Destroy not.' -- A secret treasure of  David, in his fleeing from the face of Saul into a cave. Favour  me, O God, favour me, For in Thee is my soul trusting, And in  the shadow of Thy wings I trust, Until the calamities pass  over.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:2">57:2</a> I call to God Most High, To God [who] is perfecting for me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:3">57:3</a> He sendeth from the heaven, and saveth me, He reproached --  who is panting after me. Selah. God sendeth forth His kindness  and His truth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:4">57:4</a> My soul [is] in the midst of lions, I lie down [among]  flames -- sons of men, Their teeth [are] a spear and arrows,  And their tongue a sharp sword.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:5">57:5</a> Be Thou exalted above the heavens, O God, Above all the  earth Thine honour.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:6">57:6</a> A net they have prepared for my steps, Bowed down hath my  soul, They have digged before me a pit, They have fallen into  its midst. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:7">57:7</a> Prepared is my heart, O God, Prepared is my heart, I sing  and praise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:8">57:8</a> Awake, mine honour, awake, psaltery and harp, I awake the  morning dawn.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:9">57:9</a> I thank Thee among the peoples, O Lord, I praise Thee among  the nations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:10">57:10</a> For great unto the heavens [is] Thy kindness, And unto the  clouds Thy truth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_57:11">57:11</a> Be thou exalted above the heavens, O God. Above all the  earth Thine honour!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:1">58:1</a> To the Overseer. -- `Destroy not.' -- A secret treasure, by  David. Is it true, O dumb one, righteously ye speak? Uprightly  ye judge, O sons of men?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:2">58:2</a> Even in heart ye work iniquities, In the land the violence  of your hands ye ponder.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:3">58:3</a> The wicked have been estranged from the womb, They have  erred from the belly, speaking lies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:4">58:4</a> Their poison [is] as poison of a serpent, As a deaf asp  shutting its ear,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:5">58:5</a> Which hearkeneth not to the voice of whisperers, A charmer  of charms most skilful.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:6">58:6</a> O God, break their teeth in their mouth, The jaw-teeth of  young lions break down, O Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:7">58:7</a> They are melted as waters, They go up and down for  themselves, His arrow proceedeth as they cut themselves off.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:8">58:8</a> As a snail that melteth he goeth on, [As] an untimely birth  of a woman, They have not seen the sun.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:9">58:9</a> Before your pots discern the bramble, As well the raw as  the heated He whirleth away.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:10">58:10</a> The righteous rejoiceth that he hath seen vengeance, His  steps he washeth in the blood of the wicked.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_58:11">58:11</a> And man saith: `Surely fruit [is] for the righteous:  Surely there is a God judging in the earth!'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:1">59:1</a> To the Overseer. -- `Destroy not,' by David. -- A secret  treasure, in Saul's sending, and they watch the house to put  him to death. Deliver me from mine enemies, O my God, From my  withstanders set me on high.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:2">59:2</a> Deliver me from workers of iniquity, And from men of blood  save me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:3">59:3</a> For, lo, they laid wait for my soul, Assembled against me  are strong ones, Not my transgression nor my sin, O Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:4">59:4</a> Without punishment they run and prepare themselves, Stir up  to meet me, and see.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:5">59:5</a> And Thou, Jehovah, God of Hosts, God of Israel, Awake to  inspect all the nations. Favour not any treacherous dealers of  iniquity. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:6">59:6</a> They turn back at evening, They make a noise like a dog,  And go round about the city.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:7">59:7</a> Lo, they belch out with their mouths, Swords [are] in their  lips, for `Who heareth?'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:8">59:8</a> And Thou, O Jehovah dost laugh at them, Thou dost mock at  all the nations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:9">59:9</a> O my Strength, unto Thee I take heed, For God [is] my tower  -- the God of my kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:10">59:10</a> God doth go before me, He causeth me to look on mine  enemies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:11">59:11</a> Slay them not, lest my people forget, Shake them by Thy  strength, And bring them down, O Lord our shield.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:12">59:12</a> The sin of their mouth [is] a word of their lips, And they  are captured in their pride, And from the curse and lying they  recount.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:13">59:13</a> Consume in fury, consume and they are not, And they know  that God is ruling in Jacob, To the ends of the earth. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:14">59:14</a> And they turn back at evening, They make a noise like a  dog, And they go round about the city.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:15">59:15</a> They -- they wander for food, If they are not satisfied --  then they murmur.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:16">59:16</a> And I -- I sing [of] Thy strength, And I sing at morn [of]  Thy kindness, For thou hast been a tower to me, And a refuge  for me in a day of adversity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_59:17">59:17</a> O my Strength, unto Thee I sing praise, For God [is] my  tower, the God of my kindness!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:1">60:1</a> To the Overseer. -- `Concerning the Lily of Testimony,' a  secret treasure of David, to teach, in his striving with  Aram-Naharaim, and with Aram-Zobah, and Joab turneth back and  smiteth Edom in the valley of Salt -- twelve thousand. O God,  Thou hadst cast us off, Thou hadst broken us -- hadst been  angry! -- Thou dost turn back to us.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:2">60:2</a> Thou hast caused the land to tremble, Thou hast broken it,  Heal its breaches, for it hath moved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:3">60:3</a> Thou hast shewn Thy people a hard thing, Thou hast caused  us to drink wine of trembling.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:4">60:4</a> Thou hast given to those fearing thee an ensign. To be  lifted up as an ensign Because of truth. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:5">60:5</a> That Thy beloved ones may be drawn out, Save [with] Thy  right hand, and answer us.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:6">60:6</a> God hath spoken in His holiness: I exult -- I apportion  Shechem, And the valley of Succoth I measure,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:7">60:7</a> Mine [is] Gilead, and mine [is] Manasseh, And Ephraim [is]  the strength of my head, Judah [is] my lawgiver,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:8">60:8</a> Moab [is] my pot for washing, over Edom I cast my shoe,  Shout, concerning me, O Philistia.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:9">60:9</a> Who doth bring me [to] a city of bulwarks? Who hath led me  unto Edom?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:10">60:10</a> Is it not Thou, O God? hast Thou cast us off? And dost  Thou not go forth, O God, with our hosts!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:11">60:11</a> Give to us help from adversity, And vain [is] the  deliverance of man.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_60:12">60:12</a> In God we do mightily, And He treadeth down our  adversaries!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:1">61:1</a> To the Overseer, on stringed instruments. -- By David.  Hear, O God, my loud cry, attend to my prayer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:2">61:2</a> From the end of the land unto Thee I call, In the  feebleness of my heart, Into a rock higher than I Thou dost  lead me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:3">61:3</a> For Thou hast been a refuge for me, A tower of strength  because of the enemy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:4">61:4</a> I sojourn in Thy tent to the ages, I trust in the secret  place of Thy wings. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:5">61:5</a> For Thou, O God, hast hearkened to my vows, Thou hast  appointed the inheritance Of those fearing Thy name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:6">61:6</a> Days to the days of the king Thou addest, His years as  generation and generation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:7">61:7</a> He dwelleth to the age before God, Kindness and truth  appoint -- they keep him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_61:8">61:8</a> So do I praise Thy name for ever, When I pay my vows day by  day!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:1">62:1</a> To the Overseer, for Jeduthun. -- A Psalm of David. Only --  toward God [is] my soul silent, From Him [is] my salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:2">62:2</a> Only -- He [is] my rock, and my salvation, My tower, I am  not much moved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:3">62:3</a> Till when do ye devise mischief against a man? Ye are  destroyed all of you, As a wall inclined, a hedge that is cast  down.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:4">62:4</a> Only -- from his excellency They have consulted to drive  away, They enjoy a lie, with their mouth they bless, And with  their heart revile. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:5">62:5</a> Only -- for God, be silent, O my soul, For from Him [is] my  hope.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:6">62:6</a> Only -- He [is] my rock and my salvation, My tower, I am  not moved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:7">62:7</a> On God [is] my salvation, and my honour, The rock of my  strength, my refuge [is] in God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:8">62:8</a> Trust in Him at all times, O people, Pour forth before Him  your heart, God [is] a refuge for us. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:9">62:9</a> Only -- vanity [are] the low, a lie the high. In balances  to go up they than vanity [are] lighter.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:10">62:10</a> Trust not in oppression, And in robbery become not vain,  Wealth -- when it increaseth -- set not the heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:11">62:11</a> Once hath God spoken, twice I heard this, That `strength  [is] with God.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_62:12">62:12</a> And with Thee, O Lord, [is] kindness, For Thou dost  recompense to each, According to his work!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:1">63:1</a> A Psalm of David, in his being in the wilderness of Judah.  O God, Thou [art] my God, earnestly do I seek Thee, Thirsted  for Thee hath my soul, Longed for Thee hath my flesh, In a land  dry and weary, without waters.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:2">63:2</a> So in the sanctuary I have seen Thee, To behold Thy  strength and Thine honour.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:3">63:3</a> Because better [is] Thy kindness than life, My lips do  praise Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:4">63:4</a> So I bless Thee in my life, in Thy name I lift up my hands.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:5">63:5</a> As [with] milk and fatness is my soul satisfied, And [with]  singing lips doth my mouth praise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:6">63:6</a> If I have remembered Thee on my couch, In the watches -- I  meditate on Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:7">63:7</a> For Thou hast been a help to me, And in the shadow of Thy  wings I sing.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:8">63:8</a> Cleaved hath my soul after Thee, On me hath Thy right hand  taken hold.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:9">63:9</a> And they who for desolation seek my soul, Go in to the  lower parts of the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:10">63:10</a> They cause him to run on the edge of the sword, A portion  for foxes they are.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_63:11">63:11</a> And the king doth rejoice in God, Boast himself doth every  one swearing by Him, But stopped is the mouth of those speaking  lies!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:1">64:1</a> To the Overseer. -- A Psalm of David. Hear, O God, my  voice, in my meditation, From the fear of an enemy Thou keepest  my life,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:2">64:2</a> Hidest me from the secret counsel of evil doers, From the  tumult of workers of iniquity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:3">64:3</a> Who sharpened as a sword their tongue, They directed their  arrow -- a bitter word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:4">64:4</a> To shoot in secret places the perfect, Suddenly they shoot  him, and fear not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:5">64:5</a> They strengthen for themselves an evil thing, They recount  of the hiding of snares, They have said, `Who doth look at it?'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:6">64:6</a> They search out perverse things, `We perfected a searching  search,' And the inward part of man, and the heart [are] deep.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:7">64:7</a> And God doth shoot them [with] an arrow, Sudden have been  their wounds,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:8">64:8</a> And they cause him to stumble, Against them [is] their own  tongue, Every looker on them fleeth away.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:9">64:9</a> And all men fear, and declare the work of God, And His deed  they have considered wisely.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_64:10">64:10</a> The righteous doth rejoice in Jehovah, And hath trusted in  Him, And boast themselves do all the upright of heart!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:1">65:1</a> To the Overseer. -- A Psalm of David. A Song. To Thee,  silence -- praise, O God, [is] in Zion, And to Thee is a vow  completed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:2">65:2</a> Hearer of prayer, to Thee all flesh cometh.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:3">65:3</a> Matters of iniquities were mightier than I, Our  transgressions -- Thou dost cover them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:4">65:4</a> O the happiness of [him whom] Thou choosest, And drawest  near, he inhabiteth Thy courts, We are satisfied with the  goodness of Thy house, Thy holy temple.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:5">65:5</a> By fearful things in righteousness Thou answerest us, O God  of our salvation, The confidence of all far off ends of earth  and sea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:6">65:6</a> Establishing mountains by His power, He hath been girded  with might,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:7">65:7</a> Restraining the noise of seas, the noise of their billows,  And the multitude of the peoples.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:8">65:8</a> And the inhabitants of the uttermost parts From Thy signs  are afraid, The outgoings of morning and evening Thou causest  to sing.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:9">65:9</a> Thou hast inspected the earth, and waterest it, Thou makest  it very rich, the rivulet of God [is] full of water, Thou  preparest their corn, When thus Thou dost prepare it,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:10">65:10</a> Its ridges have been filled, Deepened hath been its  furrow, With showers Thou dost soften it, Its springing up Thou  blessest.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:11">65:11</a> Thou hast crowned the year of Thy goodness, And Thy paths  drop fatness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:12">65:12</a> Drop do the pastures of a wilderness, And joy of the  heights Thou girdest on.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_65:13">65:13</a> Clothed have lambs the flock, And valleys are covered with  corn, They shout -- yea, they sing!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:1">66:1</a> To the Overseer. -- A Song, a Psalm. Shout ye to God, all  the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:2">66:2</a> Praise ye the honour of His name, Make ye honourable His  praise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:3">66:3</a> Say to God, `How fearful [are] Thy works, By the abundance  of Thy strength, Thine enemies feign obedience to Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:4">66:4</a> All the earth do bow to Thee, They sing praise to Thee,  they praise Thy name.' Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:5">66:5</a> Come ye, and see the works of God, Fearful acts toward the  sons of men.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:6">66:6</a> He hath turned a sea to dry land, Through a river they pass  over on foot, There do we rejoice in Him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:7">66:7</a> Ruling by His might to the age, His eyes among the nations  do watch, The refractory exalt not themselves. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:8">66:8</a> Bless, ye peoples, our God, And sound the voice of His  praise,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:9">66:9</a> Who hath placed our soul in life, And suffered not our feet  to be moved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:10">66:10</a> For Thou hast tried us, O God, Thou hast refined us as the  refining of silver.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:11">66:11</a> Thou hast brought us into a net, Thou hast placed pressure  on our loins.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:12">66:12</a> Thou hast caused man to ride at our head. We have entered  into fire and into water, And Thou bringest us out to a watered  place.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:13">66:13</a> I enter Thy house with burnt-offerings, I complete to Thee  my vows,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:14">66:14</a> For opened were my lips, And my mouth spake in my  distress:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:15">66:15</a> `Burnt-offerings of fatlings I offer to Thee, With perfume  of rams, I prepare a bullock with he-goats.' Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:16">66:16</a> Come, hear, all ye who fear God, And I recount what he did  for my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:17">66:17</a> Unto Him [with] my mouth I have called, And exaltation  [is] under my tongue.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:18">66:18</a> Iniquity, if I have seen in my heart, The Lord doth not  hear.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:19">66:19</a> But God hath heard, He hath attended to the voice of my  prayer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_66:20">66:20</a> Blessed [is] God, Who hath not turned aside my prayer, And  His loving-kindness, from me!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:1">67:1</a> To the Overseer, with stringed instruments. -- A Psalm, a  Song. God doth favour us and bless us, Doth cause His face to  shine with us. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:2">67:2</a> For the knowledge in earth of Thy way, among all nations of  Thy salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:3">67:3</a> Praise Thee do peoples, O God, Praise Thee do peoples, all  of them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:4">67:4</a> Rejoice and sing do nations, For Thou judgest peoples  uprightly, And peoples on earth comfortest. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:5">67:5</a> Confess Thee do peoples, O God, Confess Thee do peoples --  all of them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:6">67:6</a> Earth hath given her increase, God doth bless us -- our  God,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_67:7">67:7</a> God doth bless us, and all ends of earth fear Him!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:1">68:1</a> To the Overseer. -- A Psalm, a song of David. Rise doth God  -- scattered are His enemies! And those hating Him flee from  His face.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:2">68:2</a> As the driving away of smoke Thou drivest away, As the  melting of wax before fire, The wicked perish at the presence  of God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:3">68:3</a> And the righteous rejoice, they exult before God, And they  joy with gladness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:4">68:4</a> Sing ye to God -- praise His name, Raise up a highway for  Him who is riding in deserts, In Jah [is] His name, and exult  before Him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:5">68:5</a> Father of the fatherless, and judge of the widows, [Is] God  in His holy habitation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:6">68:6</a> God -- causing the lonely to dwell at home, Bringing out  bound ones into prosperity, Only -- the refractory have  inhabited a dry place.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:7">68:7</a> O God, in Thy going forth before Thy people, In Thy  stepping through the wilderness, Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:8">68:8</a> The earth hath shaken, Yea, the heavens have dropped before  God, This Sinai -- before God, the God of Israel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:9">68:9</a> A shower of free-will gifts thou shakest out, O God. Thine  inheritance, when it hath been weary, Thou hast established it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:10">68:10</a> Thy company have dwelt in it, Thou preparest in Thy  goodness for the poor, O God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:11">68:11</a> The Lord doth give the saying, The female proclaimers  [are] a numerous host.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:12">68:12</a> Kings of hosts flee utterly away, And a female inhabitant  of the house apportioneth spoil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:13">68:13</a> Though ye do lie between two boundaries, Wings of a dove  covered with silver, And her pinions with yellow gold.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:14">68:14</a> When the Mighty spreadeth kings in it, It doth snow in  Salmon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:15">68:15</a> A hill of God [is] the hill of Bashan, A hill of heights  [is] the hill of Bashan.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:16">68:16</a> Why do ye envy, O high hills, The hill God hath desired  for His seat? Jehovah also doth tabernacle for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:17">68:17</a> The chariots of God [are] myriads, thousands of changes,  The Lord [is] among them, in Sinai, in the sanctuary.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:18">68:18</a> Thou hast ascended on high, Thou hast taken captive  captivity, Thou hast taken gifts for men, That even the  refractory may rest, O Jah God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:19">68:19</a> Blessed [is] the Lord, day by day He layeth on us. God  Himself [is] our salvation. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:20">68:20</a> God Himself [is] to us a God for deliverances, And Jehovah  Lord hath the outgoings of death.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:21">68:21</a> Only -- God doth smite The head of His enemies, The hairy  crown of a habitual walker in his guilt.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:22">68:22</a> The Lord said: `From Bashan I bring back, I bring back  from the depths of the sea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:23">68:23</a> So that thou dashest thy foot in blood, [In the blood of]  enemies -- the tongue of Thy dogs.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:24">68:24</a> They have seen Thy goings, O God, Goings of my God, my  king, in the sanctuary.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:25">68:25</a> Singers have been before, Behind [are] players on  instruments, In the midst virgins playing with timbrels.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:26">68:26</a> In assemblies bless ye God, The Lord -- from the fountain  of Israel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:27">68:27</a> There [is] little Benjamin their ruler, Heads of Judah  their defence, Heads of Zebulun -- heads of Naphtali.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:28">68:28</a> Thy God hath commanded thy strength, Be strong, O God,  this Thou hast wrought for us.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:29">68:29</a> Because of Thy temple at Jerusalem, To Thee do kings bring  a present.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:30">68:30</a> Rebuke a beast of the reeds, a company of bulls, With  calves of the peoples, Each humbling himself with pieces of  silver, Scatter Thou peoples delighting in conflicts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:31">68:31</a> Come do fat ones out of Egypt, Cush causeth her hands to  run to God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:32">68:32</a> Kingdoms of the earth, sing ye to God, Praise ye the Lord.  Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:33">68:33</a> To him who is riding on the heavens of the heavens of old,  Lo, He giveth with His voice a strong voice.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:34">68:34</a> Ascribe ye strength to God, Over Israel [is] His  excellency, and His strength in the clouds.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_68:35">68:35</a> Fearful, O God, out of Thy sanctuaries, The God of Israel  Himself, Giving strength and might to the people. Blessed [is]  God!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:1">69:1</a> To the Overseer. -- `On the Lilies,' by David. Save me, O  God, for come have waters unto the soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:2">69:2</a> I have sunk in deep mire, And there is no standing, I have  come into the depths of the waters, And a flood hath overflown  me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:3">69:3</a> I have been wearied with my calling, Burnt hath been my  throat, Consumed have been mine eyes, waiting for my God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:4">69:4</a> Those hating me without cause Have been more than the hairs  of my head, Mighty have been my destroyers, My lying enemies,  That which I took not away -- I bring back.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:5">69:5</a> O God, Thou -- Thou hast known Concerning my overturn, And  my desolations from Thee have not been hid.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:6">69:6</a> Let not those waiting on Thee be ashamed because of me, O  Lord, Jehovah of Hosts, Let not those seeking Thee Blush  because of me, O God of Israel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:7">69:7</a> For because of Thee I have borne reproach, Shame hath  covered my face.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:8">69:8</a> A stranger I have been to my brother, And a foreigner to  sons of my mother.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:9">69:9</a> For zeal for Thy house hath consumed me, And the reproaches  of Thy reproachers Have fallen upon me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:10">69:10</a> And I weep in the fasting of my soul, And it is for a  reproach to me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:11">69:11</a> And I make my clothing sackcloth, And I am to them for a  simile.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:12">69:12</a> Those sitting at the gate meditate concerning me, And  those drinking strong drink, Play on instruments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:13">69:13</a> And I -- my prayer [is] to Thee, O Jehovah, A time of good  pleasure, O God, In the abundance of Thy kindness, Answer me in  the truth of Thy salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:14">69:14</a> Deliver me from the mire, and let me not sink, Let me be  delivered from those hating me, And from deep places of waters.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:15">69:15</a> Let not a flood of waters overflow me, Nor let the deep  swallow me up, Nor let the pit shut her mouth upon me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:16">69:16</a> Answer me, O Jehovah, for good [is] Thy kindness,  According to the abundance Of Thy mercies turn Thou unto me,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:17">69:17</a> And hide not Thy face from Thy servant, For I am in  distress -- haste, answer me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:18">69:18</a> Be near unto my soul -- redeem it, Because of mine enemies  ransom me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:19">69:19</a> Thou -- Thou hast known my reproach, And my shame, and my  blushing, Before Thee [are] all mine adversaries.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:20">69:20</a> Reproach hath broken my heart, and I am sick, And I look  for a bemoaner, and there is none, And for comforters, and I  have found none.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:21">69:21</a> And they give for my food gall, And for my thirst cause me  to drink vinegar.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:22">69:22</a> Their table before them is for a snare, And for a  recompence -- for a trap.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:23">69:23</a> Darkened are their eyes from seeing, And their loins  continually shake Thou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:24">69:24</a> Pour upon them Thine indignation, And the fierceness of  Thine anger doth seize them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:25">69:25</a> Their tower is desolated, In their tents there is no  dweller.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:26">69:26</a> For they have pursued him Thou hast smitten, And recount  of the pain of Thy pierced ones.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:27">69:27</a> Give punishment for their iniquity, And they enter not  into Thy righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:28">69:28</a> They are blotted out of the book of life, And with the  righteous are not written.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:29">69:29</a> And I [am] afflicted and pained, Thy salvation, O God,  doth set me on high.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:30">69:30</a> I praise the name of God with a song, And I magnify Him  with thanksgiving,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:31">69:31</a> And it is better to Jehovah than an ox, A bullock --  horned -- hoofed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:32">69:32</a> The humble have seen -- they rejoice, Ye who seek God --  and your heart liveth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:33">69:33</a> For Jehovah hearkeneth unto the needy, And His bound ones  He hath not despised.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:34">69:34</a> The heavens and earth do praise Him, Seas, and every  moving thing in them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:35">69:35</a> For God doth save Zion, And doth build the cities of  Judah, And they have dwelt there, and possess it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_69:36">69:36</a> And the seed of His servants inherit it, And those loving  His name dwell in it!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:1">70:1</a> To the Overseer, by David. -- `To cause to remember.' O  God, to deliver me, O Jehovah, for my help, haste.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:2">70:2</a> Let them be ashamed and confounded Who are seeking my soul,  Let them be turned backward and blush Who are desiring my evil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:3">70:3</a> Let them turn back because of their shame, Who are saying,  `Aha, aha.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:4">70:4</a> Let all those seeking Thee joy and be glad in Thee, And let  those loving Thy salvation Say continually, `God is magnified.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_70:5">70:5</a> And I [am] poor and needy, O God, haste to me, My help and  my deliverer [art] Thou, O Jehovah, tarry Thou not!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:1">71:1</a> In Thee, O Jehovah, I have trusted, Let me not be ashamed  to the age.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:2">71:2</a> In Thy righteousness Thou dost deliver me, And dost cause  me to escape, Incline unto me Thine ear, and save me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:3">71:3</a> Be to me for a rock -- a habitation, To go in continually,  Thou hast given command to save me, For my rock and my bulwark  [art] Thou.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:4">71:4</a> O my God, cause me to escape From the hand of the wicked,  From the hand of the perverse and violent.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:5">71:5</a> For Thou [art] my hope, O Lord Jehovah, My trust from my  youth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:6">71:6</a> By Thee I have been supported from the womb, From my  mother's bowels Thou dost cut me out, In Thee [is] my praise  continually.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:7">71:7</a> As a wonder I have been to many, And Thou [art] my strong  refuge.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:8">71:8</a> Filled is my mouth [with] Thy praise, All the day [with]  Thy beauty.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:9">71:9</a> Cast me not off at the time of old age, According to the  consumption of my power forsake me not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:10">71:10</a> For mine enemies have spoken against me, And those  watching my soul have taken counsel together,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:11">71:11</a> Saying, `God hath forsaken him, Pursue and catch him, for  there is no deliverer.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:12">71:12</a> O God, be not far from me, O my God, for my help make  haste.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:13">71:13</a> They are ashamed, they are consumed, Who are opposing my  soul, They are covered [with] reproach and blushing, Who are  seeking my evil,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:14">71:14</a> And I continually do wait with hope, And have added unto  all Thy praise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:15">71:15</a> My mouth recounteth Thy righteousness, All the day Thy  salvation, For I have not known the numbers.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:16">71:16</a> I come in the might of the Lord Jehovah, I mention Thy  righteousness -- Thine only.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:17">71:17</a> God, Thou hast taught me from my youth, And hitherto I  declare Thy wonders.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:18">71:18</a> And also unto old age and grey hairs, O God, forsake me  not, Till I declare Thy strength to a generation, To every one  that cometh Thy might.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:19">71:19</a> And Thy righteousness, O God, [is] unto the heights,  Because Thou hast done great things, O God, who [is] like Thee?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:20">71:20</a> Because Thou hast showed me many and sad distresses, Thou  turnest back -- Thou revivest me, And from the depths of the  earth, Thou turnest back -- Thou bringest me up.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:21">71:21</a> Thou dost increase my greatness, And Thou surroundest --  Thou comfortest me,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:22">71:22</a> I also thank Thee with a vessel of psaltery, Thy truth, O  my God, I sing to Thee with a harp, O Holy One of Israel,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:23">71:23</a> My lips cry aloud when I sing praise to Thee, And my soul  that Thou hast redeemed,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_71:24">71:24</a> My tongue also all the day uttereth Thy righteousness,  Because ashamed -- because confounded, Have been those seeking  my evil!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:1">72:1</a> By Solomon. O God, Thy judgments to the king give, And Thy  righteousness to the king's son.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:2">72:2</a> He judgeth Thy people with righteousness, And Thy poor with  judgment.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:3">72:3</a> The mountains bear peace to the people, And the heights by  righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:4">72:4</a> He judgeth the poor of the people, Giveth deliverance to  the sons of the needy, And bruiseth the oppressor.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:5">72:5</a> They fear Thee with the sun, and before the moon,  Generation -- generations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:6">72:6</a> He cometh down as rain on mown grass, As showers --  sprinkling the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:7">72:7</a> Flourish in his days doth the righteous, And abundance of  peace till the moon is not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:8">72:8</a> And he ruleth from sea unto sea, And from the river unto  the ends of earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:9">72:9</a> Before him bow do the inhabitants of the dry places, And  his enemies lick the dust.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:10">72:10</a> Kings of Tarshish and of the isles send back a present.  Kings of Sheba and Seba a reward bring near.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:11">72:11</a> And all kings do bow themselves to him, All nations do  serve him,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:12">72:12</a> For he delivereth the needy who crieth, And the poor when  he hath no helper,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:13">72:13</a> He hath pity on the poor and needy, And the souls of the  needy he saveth,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:14">72:14</a> From fraud and from violence he redeemeth their soul, And  precious is their blood in his eyes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:15">72:15</a> And he liveth, and giveth to him of the gold of Sheba, And  prayeth for him continually, All the day he doth bless him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:16">72:16</a> There is a handful of corn in the earth, On the top of  mountains, Shake like Lebanon doth its fruit, And they flourish  out of the city as the herb of the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:17">72:17</a> His name is to the age, Before the sun is his name  continued, And they bless themselves in him, All nations do  pronounce him happy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:18">72:18</a> Blessed is Jehovah God, God of Israel, He alone is doing  wonders,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:19">72:19</a> And blessed [is] the Name of His honour to the age, And  the whole earth is filled [with] His honour. Amen, and amen!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_72:20">72:20</a> The prayers of David son of Jesse have been ended.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:1">73:1</a> A Psalm of Asaph. Only -- good to Israel [is] God, to the  clean of heart. And I -- as a little thing, My feet have been  turned aside,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:2">73:2</a> As nothing, have my steps slipped, For I have been envious  of the boastful,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:3">73:3</a> The peace of the wicked I see, That there are no bands at  their death,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:4">73:4</a> And their might [is] firm.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:5">73:5</a> In the misery of mortals they are not, And with common men  they are not plagued.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:6">73:6</a> Therefore hath pride encircled them, Violence covereth them  as a dress.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:7">73:7</a> Their eye hath come out from fat. The imaginations of the  heart transgressed;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:8">73:8</a> They do corruptly, And they speak in the wickedness of  oppression, From on high they speak.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:9">73:9</a> They have set in the heavens their mouth, And their tongue  walketh in the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:10">73:10</a> Therefore do His people return hither, And waters of  fulness are wrung out to them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:11">73:11</a> And they have said, `How hath God known? And is there  knowledge in the Most High?'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:12">73:12</a> Lo, these [are] the wicked and easy ones of the age, They  have increased strength.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:13">73:13</a> Only -- a vain thing! I have purified my heart, And I wash  in innocency my hands,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:14">73:14</a> And I am plagued all the day, And my reproof [is] every  morning.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:15">73:15</a> If I have said, `I recount thus,' Lo, a generation of Thy  sons I have deceived.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:16">73:16</a> And I think to know this, Perverseness it [is] in mine  eyes,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:17">73:17</a> Till I come in to the sanctuaries of God, I attend to  their latter end.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:18">73:18</a> Only, in slippery places Thou dost set them, Thou hast  caused them to fall to desolations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:19">73:19</a> How have they become a desolation as in a moment, They  have been ended -- consumed from terrors.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:20">73:20</a> As a dream from awakening, O Lord, In awaking, their image  Thou despisest.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:21">73:21</a> For my heart doth show itself violent, And my reins prick  themselves,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:22">73:22</a> And I am brutish, and do not know. A beast I have been  with Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:23">73:23</a> And I [am] continually with Thee, Thou hast laid hold on  my right hand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:24">73:24</a> With Thy counsel Thou dost lead me, And after honour dost  receive me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:25">73:25</a> Whom have I in the heavens? And with Thee none I have  desired in earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:26">73:26</a> Consumed hath been my flesh and my heart, The rock of my  heart and my portion [is] God to the age.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:27">73:27</a> For, lo, those far from Thee do perish, Thou hast cut off  every one, Who is going a whoring from Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_73:28">73:28</a> And I -- nearness of God to me [is] good, I have placed in  the Lord Jehovah my refuge, To recount all Thy works!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:1">74:1</a> An Instruction of Asaph. Why, O God, hast Thou cast off for  ever? Thine anger smoketh against the flock of Thy pasture.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:2">74:2</a> Remember Thy company. Thou didst purchase of old, Thou  didst redeem the rod of Thy inheritance, This mount Zion --  Thou didst dwell in it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:3">74:3</a> Lift up Thy steps to the perpetual desolations, Everything  the enemy did wickedly in the sanctuary.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:4">74:4</a> Roared have thine adversaries, In the midst of Thy  meeting-places, They have set their ensigns as ensigns.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:5">74:5</a> He is known as one bringing in on high Against a thicket of  wood -- axes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:6">74:6</a> And now, its carvings together With axe and hatchet they  break down,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:7">74:7</a> They have sent into fire Thy sanctuary, to the earth they  polluted the tabernacle of Thy name,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:8">74:8</a> They said in their hearts, `Let us oppress them together,'  They did burn all the meeting-places of God in the land.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:9">74:9</a> Our ensigns we have not seen, There is no more a prophet,  Nor with us is one knowing how long.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:10">74:10</a> Till when, O God, doth an adversary reproach? Doth an  enemy despise thy name for ever?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:11">74:11</a> Why dost Thou turn back Thy hand, Even Thy right hand?  From the midst of Thy bosom remove [it].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:12">74:12</a> And God [is] my king of old, Working salvation in the  midst of the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:13">74:13</a> Thou hast broken by Thy strength a sea-[monster], Thou  hast shivered Heads of dragons by the waters,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:14">74:14</a> Thou hast broken the heads of leviathan, Thou makest him  food, For the people of the dry places.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:15">74:15</a> Thou hast cleaved a fountain and a stream, Thou hast dried  up perennial flowings.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:16">74:16</a> Thine [is] the day, also Thine [is] the night, Thou hast  prepared a light giver -- the sun.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:17">74:17</a> Thou hast set up all the borders of earth, Summer and  winter Thou hast formed them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:18">74:18</a> Remember this -- an enemy reproached Jehovah, And a  foolish people have despised Thy name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:19">74:19</a> Give not up to a company, The soul of Thy turtle-dove, The  company of Thy poor ones forget not for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:20">74:20</a> Look attentively to the covenant, For the dark places of  earth, Have been full of habitations of violence.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:21">74:21</a> Let not the oppressed turn back ashamed, Let the poor and  needy praise Thy name,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:22">74:22</a> Arise, O God, plead Thy plea, Remember Thy reproach from a  fool all the day.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_74:23">74:23</a> Forget not the voice of Thine adversaries, The noise of  Thy withstanders is going up continually!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:1">75:1</a> To the Overseer. -- `Destroy not.' -- A Psalm of Asaph. --  A Song. We have given thanks to Thee, O God, We have given  thanks, and near [is] Thy name, They have recounted Thy  wonders.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:2">75:2</a> When I receive an appointment, I -- I do judge uprightly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:3">75:3</a> Melted is the earth and all its inhabitants, I -- I have  pondered its pillars. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:4">75:4</a> I have said to the boastful, `Be not boastful,' And to the  wicked, `Raise not up a horn.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:5">75:5</a> Raise not up on high your horn, (Ye speak with a stiff  neck.)</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:6">75:6</a> For not from the east, or from the west, Nor from the  wilderness -- [is] elevation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:7">75:7</a> But God [is] judge, This He maketh low -- and this He  lifteth up.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:8">75:8</a> For a cup [is] in the hand of Jehovah, And the wine hath  foamed, It is full of mixture, and He poureth out of it, Only  its dregs wring out, and drink, Do all the wicked of the earth,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:9">75:9</a> And I -- I declare [it] to the age, I sing praise to the  God of Jacob.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_75:10">75:10</a> And all horns of the wicked I cut off, Exalted are the  horns of the righteous!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:1">76:1</a> To the Overseer with stringed instruments. -- A Psalm of  Asaph. -- A Song. In Judah [is] God known, in Israel His name  [is] great.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:2">76:2</a> And His tabernacle is in Salem, And His habitation in Zion.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:3">76:3</a> There he hath shivered arrows of a bow, Shield, and sword,  and battle. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:4">76:4</a> Bright [art] Thou, honourable above hills of prey.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:5">76:5</a> Spoiled themselves have the mighty of heart, They have  slept their sleep, And none of the men of might found their  hands.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:6">76:6</a> From Thy rebuke, O God of Jacob, Both rider and horse have  been fast asleep.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:7">76:7</a> Thou, fearful [art] Thou, And who doth stand before Thee,  Since Thou hast been angry!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:8">76:8</a> From heaven Thou hast sounded judgment, Earth hath feared,  and hath been still,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:9">76:9</a> In the rising of God to judgment, To save all the humble of  earth. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:10">76:10</a> For the fierceness of man praiseth Thee, The remnant of  fierceness Thou girdest on.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:11">76:11</a> Vow and complete to Jehovah your God, All ye surrounding  him. They bring presents to the Fearful One.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_76:12">76:12</a> He doth gather the spirit of leaders, Fearful to the kings  of earth!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:1">77:1</a> To the Overseer, for Jeduthun. -- A Psalm of Asaph. My  voice [is] to God, and I cry, my voice [is] to God, And He hath  given ear unto me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:2">77:2</a> In a day of my distress the Lord I sought, My hand by night  hath been spread out, And it doth not cease, My soul hath  refused to be comforted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:3">77:3</a> I remember God, and make a noise, I meditate, and feeble is  my spirit. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:4">77:4</a> Thou hast taken hold of the watches of mine eyes, I have  been moved, and I speak not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:5">77:5</a> I have reckoned the days of old, The years of the ages.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:6">77:6</a> I remember my music in the night, With my heart I meditate,  and my spirit doth search diligently:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:7">77:7</a> To the ages doth the Lord cast off? Doth He add to be  pleased no more?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:8">77:8</a> Hath His kindness ceased for ever? The saying failed to all  generations?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:9">77:9</a> Hath God forgotten [His] favours? Hath He shut up in anger  His mercies? Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:10">77:10</a> And I say: `My weakness is, The changes of the right hand  of the Most High.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:11">77:11</a> I mention the doings of Jah, For I remember of old Thy  wonders,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:12">77:12</a> And I have meditated on all Thy working, And I talk  concerning Thy doings.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:13">77:13</a> O God, in holiness [is] Thy way, Who [is] a great god like  God?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:14">77:14</a> Thou [art] the God doing wonders. Thou hast made known  among the peoples Thy strength,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:15">77:15</a> Thou hast redeemed with strength Thy people, The sons of  Jacob and Joseph. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:16">77:16</a> The waters have seen Thee, O God, The waters have seen  Thee, They are afraid -- also depths are troubled.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:17">77:17</a> Poured out waters have thick clouds, The skies have given  forth a noise, Also -- Thine arrows go up and down.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:18">77:18</a> The voice of Thy thunder [is] in the spheres, Lightnings  have lightened the world, The earth hath trembled, yea, it  shaketh.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:19">77:19</a> In the sea [is] Thy way, And Thy paths [are] in many  waters, And Thy tracks have not been known.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_77:20">77:20</a> Thou hast led as a flock Thy people, By the hand of Moses  and Aaron!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:1">78:1</a> An Instruction of Asaph. Give ear, O my people, to my law,  Incline your ear to sayings of my mouth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:2">78:2</a> I open with a simile my mouth, I bring forth hidden things  of old,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:3">78:3</a> That we have heard and do know, And our fathers have  recounted to us.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:4">78:4</a> We do not hide from their sons, To a later generation  recounting praises of Jehovah, And His strength, and His  wonders that He hath done.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:5">78:5</a> And He raiseth up a testimony in Jacob, And a law hath  placed in Israel, That He commanded our fathers, To make them  known to their sons.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:6">78:6</a> So that a later generation doth know, Sons who are born, do  rise and recount to their sons,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:7">78:7</a> And place in God their confidence, And forget not the  doings of God, But keep His commands.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:8">78:8</a> And they are not like their fathers, A generation apostate  and rebellious, A generation! it hath not prepared its heart,  Nor stedfast with God [is] its spirit.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:9">78:9</a> Sons of Ephraim -- armed bearers of bow, Have turned in a  day of conflict.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:10">78:10</a> They have not kept the covenant of God, And in His law  they have refused to walk,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:11">78:11</a> And they forget His doings, And His wonders that He shewed  them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:12">78:12</a> Before their fathers He hath done wonders, In the land of  Egypt -- the field of Zoan.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:13">78:13</a> He cleft a sea, and causeth them to pass over, Yea, He  causeth waters to stand as a heap.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:14">78:14</a> And leadeth them with a cloud by day, And all the night  with a light of fire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:15">78:15</a> He cleaveth rocks in a wilderness, And giveth drink -- as  the great deep.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:16">78:16</a> And bringeth out streams from a rock, And causeth waters  to come down as rivers.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:17">78:17</a> And they add still to sin against Him, To provoke the Most  High in the dry place.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:18">78:18</a> And they try God in their heart, To ask food for their  lust.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:19">78:19</a> And they speak against God -- they said: `Is God able to  array a table in a wilderness?'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:20">78:20</a> Lo, He hath smitten a rock, And waters flow, yea, streams  overflow. `Also -- bread [is] He able to give? Doth He prepare  flesh for His people?'</p>
