 <p><a name="an_78:21">78:21</a> Therefore hath Jehovah heard, And He sheweth Himself  wroth, And fire hath been kindled against Jacob, And anger also  hath gone up against Israel,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:22">78:22</a> For they have not believed in God, Nor have they trusted  in His salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:23">78:23</a> And He commandeth clouds from above, Yea, doors of the  heavens He hath opened.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:24">78:24</a> And He raineth on them manna to eat, Yea, corn of heaven  He hath given to them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:25">78:25</a> Food of the mighty hath each eaten, Venison He sent to  them to satiety.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:26">78:26</a> He causeth an east wind to journey in the heavens, And  leadeth by His strength a south wind,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:27">78:27</a> And He raineth on them flesh as dust, And as sand of the  seas -- winged fowl,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:28">78:28</a> And causeth [it] to fall in the midst of His camp, Round  about His tabernacles.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:29">78:29</a> And they eat, and are greatly satisfied, And their desire  He bringeth to them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:30">78:30</a> They have not been estranged from their desire, Yet [is]  their food in their mouth,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:31">78:31</a> And the anger of God hath gone up against them, And He  slayeth among their fat ones, And youths of Israel He caused to  bend.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:32">78:32</a> With all this they have sinned again, And have not  believed in His wonders.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:33">78:33</a> And He consumeth in vanity their days, And their years in  trouble.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:34">78:34</a> If He slew them, then they sought Him, And turned back,  and sought God earnestly,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:35">78:35</a> And they remember that God [is] their rock, And God Most  High their redeemer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:36">78:36</a> And -- they deceive Him with their mouth, And with their  tongue do lie to Him,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:37">78:37</a> And their heart hath not been right with Him, And they  have not been stedfast in His covenant.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:38">78:38</a> And He -- the Merciful One, Pardoneth iniquity, and  destroyeth not, And hath often turned back His anger, And  waketh not up all His fury.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:39">78:39</a> And He remembereth that they [are] flesh, A wind going on  -- and it returneth not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:40">78:40</a> How often do they provoke Him in the wilderness, Grieve  Him in the desolate place?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:41">78:41</a> Yea, they turn back, and try God, And the Holy One of  Israel have limited.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:42">78:42</a> They have not remembered His hand The day He ransomed them  from the adversary.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:43">78:43</a> When He set His signs in Egypt, And His wonders in the  field of Zoan,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:44">78:44</a> And He turneth to blood their streams, And their floods  they drink not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:45">78:45</a> He sendeth among them the beetle, and it consumeth them,  And the frog, and it destroyeth them,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:46">78:46</a> And giveth to the caterpillar their increase, And their  labour to the locust.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:47">78:47</a> He destroyeth with hail their vine, And their sycamores  with frost,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:48">78:48</a> And delivereth up to the hail their beasts, And their  cattle to the burning flames.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:49">78:49</a> He sendeth on them the fury of His anger, Wrath, and  indignation, and distress -- A discharge of evil messengers.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:50">78:50</a> He pondereth a path for His anger, He kept not back their  soul from death, Yea, their life to the pestilence He delivered  up.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:51">78:51</a> And He smiteth every first-born in Egypt, The first-fruit  of the strong in tents of Ham.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:52">78:52</a> And causeth His people to journey as a flock, And guideth  them as a drove in a wilderness,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:53">78:53</a> And He leadeth them confidently, And they have not been  afraid, And their enemies hath the sea covered.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:54">78:54</a> And He bringeth them in unto the border of His sanctuary,  This mountain His right hand had got,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:55">78:55</a> And casteth out nations from before them, And causeth them  to fall in the line of inheritance, And causeth the tribes of  Israel to dwell in their tents,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:56">78:56</a> And they tempt and provoke God Most High, And His  testimonies have not kept.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:57">78:57</a> And they turn back, And deal treacherously like their  fathers, They have been turned like a deceitful bow,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:58">78:58</a> And make Him angry with their high places, And with their  graven images make Him zealous,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:59">78:59</a> God hath heard, and sheweth Himself wroth. And kicketh  exceedingly against Israel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:60">78:60</a> And He leaveth the tabernacle of Shiloh, The tent He had  placed among men,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:61">78:61</a> And He giveth His strength to captivity, And His beauty  into the hand of an adversary,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:62">78:62</a> And delivereth up to the sword His people, And with His  inheritance shewed Himself angry.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:63">78:63</a> His young men hath fire consumed, And His virgins have not  been praised.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:64">78:64</a> His priests by the sword have fallen, And their widows  weep not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:65">78:65</a> And the Lord waketh as a sleeper, As a mighty one crying  aloud from wine.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:66">78:66</a> And He smiteth His adversaries backward, A reproach  age-during He hath put on them,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:67">78:67</a> And He kicketh against the tent of Joseph, And on the  tribe of Ephraim hath not fixed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:68">78:68</a> And He chooseth the tribe of Judah, With mount Zion that  He loved,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:69">78:69</a> And buildeth His sanctuary as a high place, Like the  earth, He founded it to the age.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:70">78:70</a> And He fixeth on David His servant, And taketh him from  the folds of a flock,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:71">78:71</a> From behind suckling ones He hath brought him in, To rule  over Jacob His people, And over Israel His inheritance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_78:72">78:72</a> And he ruleth them according to the integrity of his  heart, And by the skilfulness of his hands leadeth them!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:1">79:1</a> A Psalm of Asaph. O God, nations have come into Thy  inheritance, They have defiled Thy holy temple, They made  Jerusalem become heaps,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:2">79:2</a> They gave the dead bodies of Thy servants Food for the  fowls of the heavens, The flesh of Thy saints For the wild  beast of the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:3">79:3</a> They have shed their blood As water round about Jerusalem,  And there is none burying.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:4">79:4</a> We have been a reproach to our neighbours, A scorn and a  derision to our surrounders.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:5">79:5</a> Till when, O Jehovah? art Thou angry for ever? Thy jealousy  doth burn as fire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:6">79:6</a> Pour Thy fury on the nations who have not known Thee, And  on kingdoms that have not called in Thy name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:7">79:7</a> For [one] hath devoured Jacob, And his habitation they have  made desolate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:8">79:8</a> Remember not for us the iniquities of forefathers, Haste,  let Thy mercies go before us, For we have been very weak.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:9">79:9</a> Help us, O God of our salvation, Because of the honour of  Thy name, And deliver us, and cover over our sins, For Thy  name's sake.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:10">79:10</a> Why do the nations say, `Where [is] their God?' Let be  known among the nations before our eyes, The vengeance of the  blood of Thy servants that is shed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:11">79:11</a> Let the groaning of the prisoner come in before Thee,  According to the greatness of Thine arm, Leave Thou the sons of  death.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:12">79:12</a> And turn Thou back to our neighbours, Sevenfold unto their  bosom, their reproach, Wherewith they reproached Thee, O Lord.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_79:13">79:13</a> And we, Thy people, and the flock of Thy pasture, We give  thanks to Thee to the age, To all generations we recount Thy  praise!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:1">80:1</a> To the Overseer. -- `On the Lilies.' A testimony of Asaph.  -- A Psalm. Shepherd of Israel, give ear, Leading Joseph as a  flock, Inhabiting the cherubs -- shine forth,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:2">80:2</a> Before Ephraim, and Benjamin, and Manasseh, Wake up Thy  might, and come for our salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:3">80:3</a> O God, cause us to turn back, And cause Thy face to shine,  and we are saved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:4">80:4</a> Jehovah, God of Hosts, till when? Thou hast burned against  the prayer of Thy people.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:5">80:5</a> Thou hast caused them to eat bread of tears, And causest  them to drink With tears a third time.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:6">80:6</a> Thou makest us a strife to our neighbors, And our enemies  mock at it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:7">80:7</a> God of Hosts, turn us back, And cause Thy face to shine,  and we are saved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:8">80:8</a> A vine out of Egypt Thou dost bring, Thou dost cast out  nations, and plantest it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:9">80:9</a> Thou hast looked before it, and dost root it, And it  filleth the land,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:10">80:10</a> Covered have been hills [with] its shadow, And its boughs  [are] cedars of God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:11">80:11</a> It sendeth forth its branches unto the sea, And unto the  river its sucklings.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:12">80:12</a> Why hast Thou broken down its hedges, And all passing by  the way have plucked it?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:13">80:13</a> A boar out of the forest doth waste it, And a wild beast  of the fields consumeth it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:14">80:14</a> God of Hosts, turn back, we beseech Thee, Look from  heaven, and see, and inspect this vine,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:15">80:15</a> And the root that Thy right hand planted, And the branch  Thou madest strong for Thee,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:16">80:16</a> Burnt with fire -- cut down, From the rebuke of Thy face  they perish.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:17">80:17</a> Let Thy hand be on the man of Thy right hand, On the son  of man Thou hast strengthened for Thyself.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:18">80:18</a> And we do not go back from Thee, Thou dost revive us, and  in Thy name we call.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_80:19">80:19</a> O Jehovah, God of Hosts, turn us back, Cause Thy face to  shine, and we are saved!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:1">81:1</a> To the Overseer. -- `On the Gittith.' By Asaph. Cry aloud  to God our strength, Shout to the God of Jacob.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:2">81:2</a> Lift up a song, and give out a timbrel, A pleasant harp  with psaltery.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:3">81:3</a> Blow in the month a trumpet, In the new moon, at the day of  our festival,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:4">81:4</a> For a statute to Israel it [is], An ordinance of the God of  Jacob.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:5">81:5</a> A testimony on Joseph He hath placed it, In his going forth  over the land of Egypt. A lip, I have not known -- I hear.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:6">81:6</a> From the burden his shoulder I turned aside, His hands from  the basket pass over.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:7">81:7</a> In distress thou hast called and I deliver thee, I answer  thee in the secret place of thunder, I try thee by the waters  of Meribah. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:8">81:8</a> Hear, O My people, and I testify to thee, O Israel, if thou  dost hearken to me:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:9">81:9</a> There is not in thee a strange god, And thou bowest not  thyself to a strange god.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:10">81:10</a> I [am] Jehovah thy God, Who bringeth thee up out of the  land of Egypt. Enlarge thy mouth, and I fill it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:11">81:11</a> But, My people hearkened not to My voice, And Israel hath  not consented to Me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:12">81:12</a> And I send them away in the enmity of their heart, They  walk in their own counsels.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:13">81:13</a> O that My people were hearkening to Me, Israel in My ways  would walk.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:14">81:14</a> As a little thing their enemies I cause to bow, And  against their adversaries I turn back My hand,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:15">81:15</a> Those hating Jehovah feign obedience to Him, But their  time is -- to the age.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_81:16">81:16</a> He causeth him to eat of the fat of wheat, And [with]  honey from a rock I satisfy thee!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:1">82:1</a> -- A Psalm of Asaph. God hath stood in the company of God,  In the midst God doth judge.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:2">82:2</a> Till when do ye judge perversely? And the face of the  wicked lift up? Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:3">82:3</a> Judge ye the weak and fatherless, The afflicted and the  poor declare righteous.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:4">82:4</a> Let the weak and needy escape, From the hand of the wicked  deliver them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:5">82:5</a> They knew not, nor do they understand, In darkness they  walk habitually, Moved are all the foundations of earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:6">82:6</a> I -- I have said, `Gods ye [are], And sons of the Most High  -- all of you,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:7">82:7</a> But as man ye die, and as one of the heads ye fall,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_82:8">82:8</a> Rise, O God, judge the earth, For Thou hast inheritance  among all the nations!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:1">83:1</a> A Song, -- A Psalm of Asaph. O God, let there be no silence  to Thee, Be not silent, nor be quiet, O God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:2">83:2</a> For, lo, Thine enemies do roar, And those hating Thee have  lifted up the head,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:3">83:3</a> Against Thy people they take crafty counsel, And consult  against Thy hidden ones.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:4">83:4</a> They have said, `Come, And we cut them off from [being] a  nation, And the name of Israel is not remembered any more.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:5">83:5</a> For they consulted in heart together, Against Thee a  covenant they make,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:6">83:6</a> Tents of Edom, and Ishmaelites, Moab, and the Hagarenes,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:7">83:7</a> Gebal, and Ammon, and Amalek, Philistia with inhabitants of  Tyre,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:8">83:8</a> Asshur also is joined with them, They have been an arm to  sons of Lot. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:9">83:9</a> Do to them as [to] Midian, As [to] Sisera, as [to] Jabin,  at the stream Kishon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:10">83:10</a> They were destroyed at Endor, They were dung for the  ground!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:11">83:11</a> Make their nobles as Oreb and as Zeeb, And as Zebah and  Zalmunna all their princes,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:12">83:12</a> Who have said, `Let us occupy for ourselves The comely  places of God.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:13">83:13</a> O my God, make them as a rolling thing, As stubble before  wind.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:14">83:14</a> As a fire doth burn a forest, And as a flame setteth hills  on fire,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:15">83:15</a> So dost Thou pursue them with Thy whirlwind, And with Thy  hurricane troublest them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:16">83:16</a> Fill their faces [with] shame, And they seek Thy name, O  Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:17">83:17</a> They are ashamed and troubled for ever, Yea, they are  confounded and lost.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_83:18">83:18</a> And they know that Thou -- (Thy name [is] Jehovah -- by  Thyself,) [Art] the Most High over all the earth!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:1">84:1</a> To the Overseer. -- `On the Gittith By sons of Korah.' -- A  Psalm. How beloved Thy tabernacles, Jehovah of Hosts!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:2">84:2</a> My soul desired, yea, it hath also been consumed, For the  courts of Jehovah, My heart and my flesh cry aloud unto the  living God,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:3">84:3</a> (Even a sparrow hath found a house, And a swallow a nest  for herself, Where she hath placed her brood,) Thine altars, O  Jehovah of Hosts, My king and my God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:4">84:4</a> O the happiness of those inhabiting Thy house, Yet do they  praise Thee. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:5">84:5</a> O the happiness of a man whose strength is in Thee,  Highways [are] in their heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:6">84:6</a> Those passing through a valley of weeping, A fountain do  make it, Blessings also cover the director.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:7">84:7</a> They go from strength unto strength, He appeareth unto God  in Zion.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:8">84:8</a> O Jehovah, God of Hosts, hear my prayer, Give ear, O God of  Jacob. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:9">84:9</a> Our shield, see, O God, And behold the face of Thine  anointed,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:10">84:10</a> For good [is] a day in Thy courts, O Teacher! I have  chosen rather to be at the threshold, In the house of my God,  Than to dwell in tents of wickedness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:11">84:11</a> For a sun and a shield [is] Jehovah God, Grace and honour  doth Jehovah give. He withholdeth not good To those walking in  uprightness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_84:12">84:12</a> Jehovah of Hosts! O the happiness of a man trusting in  Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:1">85:1</a> To the Overseer. -- By sons of Korah. A Psalm. Thou hast  accepted, O Jehovah, Thy land, Thou hast turned [to] the  captivity of Jacob.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:2">85:2</a> Thou hast borne away the iniquity of Thy people, Thou hast  covered all their sin. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:3">85:3</a> Thou hast gathered up all Thy wrath, Thou hast turned back  from the fierceness of Thine anger.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:4">85:4</a> Turn back [to] us, O God of our salvation, And make void  Thine anger with us.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:5">85:5</a> To the age art Thou angry against us? Dost Thou draw out  Thine anger To generation and generation?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:6">85:6</a> Dost Thou not turn back? Thou revivest us, And Thy people  do rejoice in Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:7">85:7</a> Show us, O Jehovah, thy kindness, And Thy salvation Thou  dost give to us.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:8">85:8</a> I hear what God Jehovah speaketh, For He speaketh peace  unto His people, And unto His saints, and they turn not back to  folly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:9">85:9</a> Only, near to those fearing Him [is] His salvation, That  honour may dwell in our land.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:10">85:10</a> Kindness and truth have met, Righteousness and peace have  kissed,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:11">85:11</a> Truth from the earth springeth up, And righteousness from  heaven looketh out,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:12">85:12</a> Jehovah also giveth that which is good, And our land doth  give its increase.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_85:13">85:13</a> Righteousness before Him goeth, And maketh His footsteps  for a way!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:1">86:1</a> A Prayer of David. Incline, O Jehovah, Thine ear, Answer  me, for I [am] poor and needy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:2">86:2</a> Keep my soul, for I [am] pious, Save Thy servant -- who is  trusting to Thee, O Thou, my God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:3">86:3</a> Favour me, O Lord, for to Thee I call all the day.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:4">86:4</a> Rejoice the soul of Thy servant, For unto Thee, O Lord, my  soul I lift up.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:5">86:5</a> For Thou, Lord, [art] good and forgiving. And abundant in  kindness to all calling Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:6">86:6</a> Hear, O Jehovah, my prayer, And attend to the voice of my  supplications.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:7">86:7</a> In a day of my distress I call Thee, For Thou dost answer  me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:8">86:8</a> There is none like Thee among the gods, O Lord, And like  Thy works there are none.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:9">86:9</a> All nations that Thou hast made Come and bow themselves  before Thee, O Lord, And give honour to Thy name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:10">86:10</a> For great [art] Thou, and doing wonders, Thou [art] God  Thyself alone.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:11">86:11</a> Show me, O Jehovah, Thy way, I walk in Thy truth, My heart  doth rejoice to fear Thy name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:12">86:12</a> I confess Thee, O Lord my God, with all my heart, And I  honour Thy name to the age.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:13">86:13</a> For Thy kindness [is] great toward me, And Thou hast  delivered my soul from the lowest Sheol.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:14">86:14</a> O God, the proud have risen up against me, And a company  of the terrible sought my soul, And have not placed Thee before  them,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:15">86:15</a> And Thou, O Lord, [art] God, merciful and gracious, Slow  to anger, and abundant in kindness and truth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:16">86:16</a> Look unto me, and favour me, Give Thy strength to Thy  servant, And give salvation to a son of Thine handmaid.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_86:17">86:17</a> Do with me a sign for good, And those hating me see and  are ashamed, For Thou, O Jehovah, hast helped me, Yea, Thou  hast comforted me!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:1">87:1</a> By sons of Korah. -- A Psalm, a song. His foundation [is]  in holy mountains.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:2">87:2</a> Jehovah is loving the gates of Zion Above all the  tabernacles of Jacob.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:3">87:3</a> Honourable things are spoken in Thee, O city of God. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:4">87:4</a> I mention Rahab and Babel to those knowing Me, Lo,  Philistia, and Tyre, with Cush! This [one] was born there.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:5">87:5</a> And of Zion it is said: Each one was born in her, And He,  the Most High, doth establish her.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:6">87:6</a> Jehovah doth recount in the describing of the peoples,  `This [one] was born there.' Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_87:7">87:7</a> Singers also as players on instruments, All my fountains  [are] in Thee!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:1">88:1</a> A Song, a Psalm, by sons of Korah, to the Overseer,  `Concerning the Sickness of Afflictions.' -- An instruction, by  Heman the Ezrahite. O Jehovah, God of my salvation, Daily I  have cried, nightly before Thee,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:2">88:2</a> My prayer cometh in before Thee, Incline Thine ear to my  loud cry,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:3">88:3</a> For my soul hath been full of evils, And my life hath come  to Sheol.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:4">88:4</a> I have been reckoned with those going down [to] the pit, I  have been as a man without strength.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:5">88:5</a> Among the dead -- free, As pierced ones lying in the grave,  Whom Thou hast not remembered any more, Yea, they by Thy hand  have been cut off.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:6">88:6</a> Thou hast put me in the lowest pit, In dark places, in  depths.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:7">88:7</a> Upon me hath Thy fury lain, And [with] all Thy breakers  Thou hast afflicted. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:8">88:8</a> Thou hast put mine acquaintance far from me, Thou hast made  me an abomination to them, Shut up -- I go not forth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:9">88:9</a> Mine eye hath grieved because of affliction, I called Thee,  O Jehovah, all the day, I have spread out unto Thee my hands.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:10">88:10</a> To the dead dost Thou do wonders? Do Rephaim rise? do they  thank Thee? Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:11">88:11</a> Is Thy kindness recounted in the grave? Thy faithfulness  in destruction?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:12">88:12</a> Are Thy wonders known in the darkness? And Thy  righteousness in the land of forgetfulness?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:13">88:13</a> And I, unto Thee, O Jehovah, I have cried, And in the  morning doth my prayer come before Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:14">88:14</a> Why, O Jehovah, castest Thou off my soul? Thou hidest Thy  face from me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:15">88:15</a> I [am] afflicted, and expiring from youth, I have borne  Thy terrors -- I pine away.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:16">88:16</a> Over me hath Thy wrath passed, Thy terrors have cut me  off,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:17">88:17</a> They have surrounded me as waters all the day, They have  gone round against me together,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_88:18">88:18</a> Thou hast put far from me lover and friend, Mine  acquaintance [is] the place of darkness!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:1">89:1</a> An instruction, by Ethan the Ezrahite. Of the kind acts of  Jehovah, to the age I sing, To all generations I make known Thy  faithfulness with my mouth,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:2">89:2</a> For I said, `To the age is kindness built, The heavens!  Thou dost establish Thy faithfulness in them.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:3">89:3</a> I have made a covenant for My chosen, I have sworn to David  My servant:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:4">89:4</a> `Even to the age do I establish thy seed, And have built to  generation and generation thy throne. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:5">89:5</a> and the heavens confess Thy wonders, O Jehovah, Thy  faithfulness also [is] in an assembly of holy ones.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:6">89:6</a> For who in the sky, Compareth himself to Jehovah? Is like  to Jehovah among sons of the mighty?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:7">89:7</a> God is very terrible, In the secret counsel of His holy  ones, And fearful over all surrounding Him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:8">89:8</a> O Jehovah, God of Hosts, Who [is] like Thee -- a strong  Jah? And Thy faithfulness [is] round about Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:9">89:9</a> Thou [art] ruler over the pride of the sea, In the lifting  up of its billows Thou dost restrain them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:10">89:10</a> Thou hast bruised Rahab, as one wounded. With the arm of  Thy strength Thou hast scattered Thine enemies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:11">89:11</a> Thine [are] the heavens -- the earth also [is] Thine, The  habitable world and its fulness, Thou hast founded them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:12">89:12</a> North and south Thou hast appointed them, Tabor and Hermon  in Thy name do sing.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:13">89:13</a> Thou hast an arm with might, Strong is Thy hand -- high  Thy right hand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:14">89:14</a> Righteousness and judgment [Are] the fixed place of Thy  throne, Kindness and truth go before Thy face.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:15">89:15</a> O the happiness of the people knowing the shout, O  Jehovah, in the light of Thy face they walk habitually.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:16">89:16</a> In Thy name they rejoice all the day, And in Thy  righteousness they are exalted,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:17">89:17</a> For the beauty of their strength [art] Thou, And in Thy  good will is our horn exalted,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:18">89:18</a> For of Jehovah [is] our shield, And of the Holy One of  Israel our king.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:19">89:19</a> Then Thou hast spoken in vision, To Thy saint, yea, Thou  sayest, I have placed help upon a mighty one, Exalted a chosen  one out of the people,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:20">89:20</a> I have found David My servant, With My holy oil I have  anointed him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:21">89:21</a> With whom My hand is established, My arm also doth  strengthen him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:22">89:22</a> An enemy exacteth not upon him, And a son of perverseness  afflicteth him not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:23">89:23</a> And I have beaten down before him his adversaries, And  those hating him I plague,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:24">89:24</a> And My faithfulness and kindness [are] with him, And in My  name is his horn exalted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:25">89:25</a> And I have set on the sea his hand, And on the rivers his  right hand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:26">89:26</a> He proclaimeth me: `Thou [art] my Father, My God, and the  rock of my salvation.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:27">89:27</a> I also first-born do appoint him, Highest of the kings of  the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:28">89:28</a> To the age I keep for him My kindness, And My covenant  [is] stedfast with him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:29">89:29</a> And I have set his seed for ever, And his throne as the  days of the heavens.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:30">89:30</a> If his sons forsake My law, And in My judgments do not  walk;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:31">89:31</a> If My statutes they pollute, And My commands do not keep,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:32">89:32</a> I have looked after with a rod their transgression, And  with strokes their iniquity,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:33">89:33</a> And My kindness I break not from him, Nor do I deal  falsely in My faithfulness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:34">89:34</a> I profane not My covenant, And that which is going forth  from My lips I change not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:35">89:35</a> Once I have sworn by My holiness, I lie not to David,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:36">89:36</a> His seed is to the age, And his throne [is] as the sun  before Me,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:37">89:37</a> As the moon it is established -- to the age, And the  witness in the sky is stedfast. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:38">89:38</a> And Thou, Thou hast cast off, and dost reject, Thou hast  shown Thyself wroth With Thine anointed,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:39">89:39</a> Hast rejected the covenant of Thy servant, Thou hast  polluted to the earth his crown,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:40">89:40</a> Thou hast broken down all his hedges, Thou hast made his  fenced places a ruin.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:41">89:41</a> Spoiled him have all passing by the way, He hath been a  reproach to his neighbours,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:42">89:42</a> Thou hast exalted the right hand of his adversaries, Thou  hast caused all his enemies to rejoice.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:43">89:43</a> Also -- Thou turnest back the sharpness of his sword, And  hast not established him in battle,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:44">89:44</a> Hast caused [him] to cease from his brightness, And his  throne to the earth hast cast down.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:45">89:45</a> Thou hast shortened the days of his youth, Hast covered  him over [with] shame. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:46">89:46</a> Till when, O Jehovah, art Thou hidden? For ever doth Thy  fury burn as fire?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:47">89:47</a> Remember, I pray Thee, what [is] life-time? Wherefore in  vain hast Thou created All the sons of men?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:48">89:48</a> Who [is] the man that liveth, and doth not see death? He  delivereth his soul from the hand of Sheol. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:49">89:49</a> Where [are] Thy former kindnesses, O Lord. Thou hast sworn  to David in Thy faithfulness,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:50">89:50</a> Remember, O Lord, the reproach of Thy servants, I have  borne in my bosom all the strivings of the peoples,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:51">89:51</a> Wherewith Thine enemies reproached, O Jehovah, Wherewith  they have reproached The steps of Thine anointed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_89:52">89:52</a> Blessed [is] Jehovah to the age. Amen, and amen!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:1">90:1</a> A Prayer of Moses, the man of God. Lord, a habitation Thou  -- Thou hast been, To us -- in generation and generation,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:2">90:2</a> Before mountains were brought forth, And Thou dost form the  earth and the world, Even from age unto age Thou [art] God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:3">90:3</a> Thou turnest man unto a bruised thing, And sayest, Turn  back, ye sons of men.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:4">90:4</a> For a thousand years in Thine eyes [are] as yesterday, For  it passeth on, yea, a watch by night.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:5">90:5</a> Thou hast inundated them, they are asleep, In the morning  as grass he changeth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:6">90:6</a> In the morning it flourisheth, and hath changed, At evening  it is cut down, and hath withered.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:7">90:7</a> For we were consumed in Thine anger, And in Thy fury we  have been troubled.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:8">90:8</a> Thou hast set our iniquities before Thee, Our hidden things  at the light of Thy face,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:9">90:9</a> For all our days pined away in Thy wrath, We consumed our  years as a meditation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:10">90:10</a> Days of our years, in them [are] seventy years, And if, by  reason of might, eighty years, Yet [is] their enlargement  labour and vanity, For it hath been cut off hastily, and we fly  away.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:11">90:11</a> Who knoweth the power of Thine anger? And according to Thy  fear -- Thy wrath?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:12">90:12</a> To number our days aright let [us] know, And we bring the  heart to wisdom.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:13">90:13</a> Turn back, O Jehovah, till when? And repent concerning Thy  servants.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:14">90:14</a> Satisfy us at morn [with] Thy kindness, And we sing and  rejoice all our days.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:15">90:15</a> Cause us to rejoice according to the days Wherein Thou  hast afflicted us, The years we have seen evil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:16">90:16</a> Let Thy work appear unto Thy servants, And Thine honour on  their sons.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_90:17">90:17</a> And let the pleasantness of Jehovah our God be upon us,  And the work of our hands establish on us, Yea, the work of our  hands establish it!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:1">91:1</a> He who is dwelling In the secret place of the Most High, In  the shade of the Mighty lodgeth habitually,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:2">91:2</a> He is saying of Jehovah, `My refuge, and my bulwark, my God,  I trust in Him,'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:3">91:3</a> For He delivereth thee from the snare of a fowler, From a  calamitous pestilence.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:4">91:4</a> With His pinion He covereth thee over, And under His wings  thou dost trust, A shield and buckler [is] His truth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:5">91:5</a> Thou art not afraid of fear by night, Of arrow that flieth  by day,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:6">91:6</a> Of pestilence in thick darkness that walketh, Of  destruction that destroyeth at noon,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:7">91:7</a> There fall at thy side a thousand, And a myriad at thy  right hand, Unto thee it cometh not nigh.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:8">91:8</a> But with thine eyes thou lookest, And the reward of the  wicked thou seest,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:9">91:9</a> (For Thou, O Jehovah, [art] my refuge,) The Most High thou  madest thy habitation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:10">91:10</a> Evil happeneth not unto thee, And a plague cometh not near  thy tent,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:11">91:11</a> For His messengers He chargeth for thee, To keep thee in  all thy ways,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:12">91:12</a> On the hands they bear thee up, Lest thou smite against a  stone thy foot.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:13">91:13</a> On lion and asp thou treadest, Thou trampest young lion  and dragon.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:14">91:14</a> Because in Me he hath delighted, I also deliver him -- I  set him on high, Because he hath known My name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:15">91:15</a> He doth call Me, and I answer him, I [am] with him in  distress, I deliver him, and honour him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_91:16">91:16</a> With length of days I satisfy him, And I cause him to look  on My salvation!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:1">92:1</a> A Psalm. -- A Song for the sabbath-day. Good to give thanks  to Jehovah, And to sing praises to Thy name, O Most High,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:2">92:2</a> To declare in the morning Thy kindness, And Thy  faithfulness in the nights.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:3">92:3</a> On ten strings and on psaltery, On higgaion, with harp.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:4">92:4</a> For Thou hast caused me to rejoice, O Jehovah, in Thy work,  Concerning the works of Thy hands I sing.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:5">92:5</a> How great have been Thy works, O Jehovah, Very deep have  been Thy thoughts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:6">92:6</a> A brutish man doth not know, And a fool understandeth not  this; --</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:7">92:7</a> When the wicked flourish as a herb, And blossom do all  workers of iniquity -- For their being destroyed for ever and  ever!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:8">92:8</a> And Thou [art] high to the age, O Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:9">92:9</a> For, lo, Thine enemies, O Jehovah, For, lo, Thine enemies,  do perish, Separate themselves do all workers of iniquity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:10">92:10</a> And Thou exaltest as a reem my horn, I have been anointed  with fresh oil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:11">92:11</a> And mine eye looketh on mine enemies, Of those rising up  against me, The evil doers, do mine ears hear.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:12">92:12</a> The righteous as a palm-tree flourisheth, As a cedar in  Lebanon he groweth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:13">92:13</a> Those planted in the house of Jehovah, In the courts of  our God do flourish.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:14">92:14</a> Still they bring forth in old age, Fat and flourishing are  they,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_92:15">92:15</a> To declare that upright [is] Jehovah my rock, And there is  no perverseness in Him!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:1">93:1</a> Jehovah hath reigned, Excellency He hath put on, Jehovah  put on strength, He girded Himself, Also -- established is the  world, unmoved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:2">93:2</a> Established is Thy throne since then, From the age Thou  [art].</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:3">93:3</a> Floods have lifted up, O Jehovah, Floods have lifted up  their voice, Floods lift up their breakers.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:4">93:4</a> Than the voices of many mighty waters, Breakers of a sea,  mighty on high [is] Jehovah,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_93:5">93:5</a> Thy testimonies have been very stedfast, To Thy house  comely [is] holiness, O Jehovah, for length of days!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:1">94:1</a> God of vengeance -- Jehovah! God of vengeance, shine forth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:2">94:2</a> Be lifted up, O Judge of the earth, Send back a recompence  on the proud.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:3">94:3</a> Till when [do] the wicked, O Jehovah? Till when do the  wicked exult?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:4">94:4</a> They utter -- they speak an old saw, All working iniquity  do boast themselves.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:5">94:5</a> Thy people, O Jehovah, they bruise, And Thine inheritance  they afflict.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:6">94:6</a> Widow and sojourner they slay, And fatherless ones they  murder.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:7">94:7</a> And they say, `Jehovah doth not see, And the God of Jacob  doth not consider.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:8">94:8</a> Consider, ye brutish among the people, And ye foolish, when  do ye act wisely?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:9">94:9</a> He who planteth the ear doth He not hear? He who formeth  the eye doth He not see?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:10">94:10</a> He who is instructing nations, Doth He not reprove? He who  is teaching man knowledge [is] Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:11">94:11</a> He knoweth the thoughts of man, that they [are] vanity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:12">94:12</a> O the happiness of the man Whom Thou instructest, O Jah,  And out of Thy law teachest him,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:13">94:13</a> To give rest to him from days of evil, While a pit is  digged for the wicked.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:14">94:14</a> For Jehovah leaveth not His people, And His inheritance  forsaketh not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:15">94:15</a> For to righteousness judgment turneth back, And after it  all the upright of heart,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:16">94:16</a> Who riseth up for me with evil doers? Who stationeth  himself for me with workers of iniquity?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:17">94:17</a> Unless Jehovah [were] a help to me, My soul had almost  inhabited silence.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:18">94:18</a> If I have said, `My foot hath slipped,' Thy kindness, O  Jehovah, supporteth me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:19">94:19</a> In the abundance of my thoughts within me, Thy comforts  delight my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:20">94:20</a> Is a throne of mischief joined [with] Thee? A framer of  perverseness by statute?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:21">94:21</a> They decree against the soul of the righteous, And  innocent blood declare wicked.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:22">94:22</a> And Jehovah is for a high place to me, And my God [is] for  a rock -- my refuge,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_94:23">94:23</a> And turneth back on them their iniquity, And in their  wickedness cutteth them off; Jehovah our God doth cut them off!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:1">95:1</a> Come, we sing to Jehovah, We shout to the rock of our  salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:2">95:2</a> We come before His face with thanksgiving, With psalms we  shout to Him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:3">95:3</a> For a great God [is] Jehovah, And a great king over all  gods.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:4">95:4</a> In whose hand [are] the deep places of earth, And the  strong places of hills [are] His.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:5">95:5</a> Whose is the sea, and He made it, And His hands formed the  dry land.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:6">95:6</a> Come in, we bow ourselves, and we bend, We kneel before  Jehovah our Maker.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:7">95:7</a> For He [is] our God, and we the people of His pasture, And  the flock of His hand, To-day, if to His voice ye hearken,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:8">95:8</a> Harden not your heart as [in] Meribah, As [in] the day of  Massah in the wilderness,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:9">95:9</a> Where your fathers have tried Me, Have proved Me, yea, have  seen My work.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:10">95:10</a> Forty years I am weary of the generation, And I say, `A  people erring in heart -- they! And they have not known My  ways:'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_95:11">95:11</a> Where I sware in Mine anger, `If they come in unto My rest  -- !'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:1">96:1</a> Sing to Jehovah a new song, Sing to Jehovah all the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:2">96:2</a> Sing to Jehovah, bless His name, Proclaim from day to day  His salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:3">96:3</a> Declare among nations His honour, Among all the peoples His  wonders.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:4">96:4</a> For great [is] Jehovah, and praised greatly, Fearful He  [is] over all gods.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:5">96:5</a> For all the gods of the peoples [are] nought, And Jehovah  made the heavens.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:6">96:6</a> Honour and majesty [are] before Him, Strength and beauty in  His sanctuary.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:7">96:7</a> Ascribe to Jehovah, O families of the peoples, Ascribe to  Jehovah honour and strength.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:8">96:8</a> Ascribe to Jehovah the honour of His name, Lift up a  present and come in to His courts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:9">96:9</a> Bow yourselves to Jehovah, In the honour of holiness, Be  afraid of His presence, all the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:10">96:10</a> Say among nations, `Jehovah hath reigned, Also --  established is the world, unmoved, He judgeth the peoples in  uprightness.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:11">96:11</a> The heavens joy, and the earth is joyful, The sea and its  fulness roar.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:12">96:12</a> The field exulteth, and all that [is] in it, Then sing do  all trees of the forest,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_96:13">96:13</a> Before Jehovah, for He hath come, For He hath come to  judge the earth. He judgeth the world in righteousness, And the  peoples in His faithfulness!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:1">97:1</a> Jehovah hath reigned, The earth is joyful, many isles  rejoice.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:2">97:2</a> Cloud and darkness [are] round about Him, Righteousness and  judgment the basis of His throne.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:3">97:3</a> Fire before Him goeth, And burneth round about His  adversaries.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:4">97:4</a> Lightened have His lightnings the world, The earth hath  seen, and is pained.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:5">97:5</a> Hills, like wax, melted before Jehovah, Before the Lord of  all the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:6">97:6</a> The heavens declared His righteousness, And all the peoples  have seen His honour.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:7">97:7</a> Ashamed are all servants of a graven image, Those boasting  themselves in idols, Bow yourselves to him, all ye gods.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:8">97:8</a> Zion hath heard and rejoiceth, And daughters of Judah are  joyful, Because of Thy judgments, O Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:9">97:9</a> For Thou, Jehovah, [art] Most High over all the earth,  Greatly Thou hast been exalted over all gods.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:10">97:10</a> Ye who love Jehovah, hate evil, He is keeping the souls of  His saints, From the hand of the wicked he delivereth them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:11">97:11</a> Light [is] sown for the righteous, And for the upright of  heart -- joy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_97:12">97:12</a> Rejoice, ye righteous, in Jehovah, And give thanks at the  remembrance of his holiness!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:1">98:1</a> A Psalm. Sing ye to Jehovah a new song, For wonders He hath  done, Given salvation to Him hath His right hand and His holy  arm.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:2">98:2</a> Jehovah hath made known His salvation, Before the eyes of  the nations, He hath revealed His righteousness,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:3">98:3</a> He hath remembered His kindness, And His faithfulness to  the house of Israel, All ends of earth have seen the salvation  of our God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:4">98:4</a> Shout to Jehovah, all the earth, Break forth, and cry  aloud, and sing.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:5">98:5</a> Sing to Jehovah with harp, With harp, and voice of praise,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:6">98:6</a> With trumpets, and voice of a cornet, Shout ye before the  king Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:7">98:7</a> Roar doth the sea and its fulness, The world and the  inhabitants in it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:8">98:8</a> Floods clap hand, together hills cry aloud,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_98:9">98:9</a> Before Jehovah, For He hath come to judge the earth, He  judgeth the world in righteousness, And the people in  uprightness!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:1">99:1</a> Jehovah hath reigned, peoples tremble, The Inhabitant of  the cherubs, the earth shaketh.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:2">99:2</a> Jehovah in Zion [is] great, And high He [is] over all the  peoples.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:3">99:3</a> They praise Thy name, `Great, and fearful, holy [it] is.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:4">99:4</a> And the strength of the king Hath loved judgment, Thou --  Thou hast established uprightness; Judgment and righteousness  in Jacob, Thou -- Thou hast done.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:5">99:5</a> Exalt ye Jehovah our God, And bow yourselves at His  footstool, holy [is] He.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:6">99:6</a> Moses and Aaron among His priests, And Samuel among those  proclaiming His name. They are calling unto Jehovah, And He  doth answer them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:7">99:7</a> In a pillar of cloud He speaketh unto them, They have kept  His testimonies, And the statute He hath given to them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:8">99:8</a> O Jehovah, our God, Thou hast afflicted them, A God  forgiving Thou hast been to them, And taking vengeance on their  actions.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_99:9">99:9</a> Exalt ye Jehovah our God, And bow yourselves at His holy  hill, For holy [is] Jehovah our God!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:1">100:1</a> A Psalm of Thanksgiving. Shout to Jehovah, all the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:2">100:2</a> Serve Jehovah with joy, come before him with singing.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:3">100:3</a> Know that Jehovah He [is] God, He made us, and we are His,  His people -- and the flock of His pasture.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:4">100:4</a> Enter ye His gates with thanksgiving, His courts with  praise, Give ye thanks to Him, bless ye His Name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_100:5">100:5</a> For good [is] Jehovah, to the age His kindness, And to  generation and generation His faithfulness!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:1">101:1</a> A Psalm of David. Kindness and judgment I sing, To Thee, O  Jehovah, I sing praise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:2">101:2</a> I act wisely in a perfect way, When dost Thou come in unto  me? I walk habitually in the integrity of my heart, In the  midst of my house.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:3">101:3</a> I set not before mine eyes a worthless thing, The work of  those turning aside I have hated, It adhereth not to me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:4">101:4</a> A perverse heart turneth aside from me, Wickedness I know  not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:5">101:5</a> Whoso slandereth in secret his neighbour, Him I cut off,  The high of eyes and proud of heart, him I endure not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:6">101:6</a> Mine eyes are on the faithful of the land, To dwell with  me, Whoso is walking in a perfect way, he serveth me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:7">101:7</a> He dwelleth not in my house who is working deceit, Whoso  is speaking lies Is not established before mine eyes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_101:8">101:8</a> At morning I cut off all the wicked of the land, To cut  off from the city of Jehovah All the workers of iniquity!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:1">102:1</a> A Prayer of the afflicted when he is feeble, and before  Jehovah poureth out his plaint. O Jehovah, hear my prayer, yea,  my cry to Thee cometh.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:2">102:2</a> Hide not Thou Thy face from me, In a day of mine  adversity, Incline unto me Thine ear, In the day I call, haste,  answer me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:3">102:3</a> For consumed in smoke have been my days, And my bones as a  fire-brand have burned.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:4">102:4</a> Smitten as the herb, and withered, is my heart, For I have  forgotten to eat my bread.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:5">102:5</a> From the voice of my sighing Hath my bone cleaved to my  flesh.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:6">102:6</a> I have been like to a pelican of the wilderness, I have  been as an owl of the dry places.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:7">102:7</a> I have watched, and I am As a bird alone on the roof.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:8">102:8</a> All the day mine enemies reproached me, Those mad at me  have sworn against me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:9">102:9</a> Because ashes as bread I have eaten, And my drink with  weeping have mingled,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:10">102:10</a> From Thine indignation and Thy wrath, For Thou hast  lifted me up, And dost cast me down.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:11">102:11</a> My days as a shadow [are] stretched out, And I -- as the  herb I am withered.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:12">102:12</a> And Thou, O Jehovah, to the age abidest, And Thy memorial  to all generations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:13">102:13</a> Thou -- Thou risest -- Thou pitiest Zion, For the time to  favour her, For the appointed time hath come.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:14">102:14</a> For Thy servants have been pleased with her stones, And  her dust they favour.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:15">102:15</a> And nations fear the name of Jehovah, And all kings of  the earth Thine honour,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:16">102:16</a> For Jehovah hath builded Zion, He hath been seen in His  honour,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:17">102:17</a> He turned unto the prayer of the destitute, And He hath  not despised their prayer.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:18">102:18</a> This is written for a later generation, And the people  created do praise Jah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:19">102:19</a> For He hath looked From the high place of His sanctuary.  Jehovah from heaven unto earth looked attentively,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:20">102:20</a> To hear the groan of the prisoner, To loose sons of  death,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:21">102:21</a> To declare in Zion the name of Jehovah, And His praise in  Jerusalem,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:22">102:22</a> In the peoples being gathered together, And the kingdoms  -- to serve Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:23">102:23</a> He hath humbled in the way my power, He hath shortened my  days.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:24">102:24</a> I say, `My God, take me not up in the midst of my days,'  Through all generations [are] Thine years.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:25">102:25</a> Beforetime the earth Thou didst found, And the work of  Thy hands [are] the heavens.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:26">102:26</a> They -- They perish, and Thou remainest, And all of them  as a garment become old, As clothing Thou changest them, And  they are changed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:27">102:27</a> And Thou [art] the same, and Thine years are not  finished.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_102:28">102:28</a> The sons of Thy servants do continue, And their seed  before Thee is established!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:1">103:1</a> By David. Bless, O my soul, Jehovah, And all my inward  parts -- His Holy Name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:2">103:2</a> Bless, O my soul, Jehovah, And forget not all His  benefits,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:3">103:3</a> Who is forgiving all thine iniquities, Who is healing all  thy diseases,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:4">103:4</a> Who is redeeming from destruction thy life, Who is  crowning thee -- kindness and mercies,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:5">103:5</a> Who is satisfying with good thy desire, Renew itself as an  eagle doth thy youth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:6">103:6</a> Jehovah is doing righteousness and judgments For all the  oppressed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:7">103:7</a> He maketh known His ways to Moses, To the sons of Israel  His acts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:8">103:8</a> Merciful and gracious [is] Jehovah, Slow to anger, and  abundant in mercy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:9">103:9</a> Not for ever doth He strive, Nor to the age doth He watch.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:10">103:10</a> Not according to our sins hath He done to us, Nor  according to our iniquities Hath He conferred benefits upon us.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:11">103:11</a> For, as the height of the heavens [is] above the earth,  His kindness hath been mighty over those fearing Him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:12">103:12</a> As the distance of east from west He hath put far from us  our transgressions.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:13">103:13</a> As a father hath mercy on sons, Jehovah hath mercy on  those fearing Him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:14">103:14</a> For He hath known our frame, Remembering that we [are]  dust.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:15">103:15</a> Mortal man! as grass [are] his days, As a flower of the  field so he flourisheth;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:16">103:16</a> For a wind hath passed over it, and it is not, And its  place doth not discern it any more.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:17">103:17</a> And the kindness of Jehovah [Is] from age even unto age  on those fearing Him, And His righteousness to sons' sons,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:18">103:18</a> To those keeping His covenant, And to those remembering  His precepts to do them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:19">103:19</a> Jehovah in the heavens Hath established His throne, And  His kingdom over all hath ruled.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:20">103:20</a> Bless Jehovah, ye His messengers, Mighty in power --  doing His word, To hearken to the voice of His Word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:21">103:21</a> Bless Jehovah, all ye His hosts, His ministers -- doing  His pleasure.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_103:22">103:22</a> Bless Jehovah, all ye His works, In all places of His  dominion. Bless, O my soul, Jehovah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:1">104:1</a> Bless, O my soul, Jehovah! Jehovah, my God, Thou hast been  very great, Honour and majesty Thou hast put on.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:2">104:2</a> Covering himself [with] light as a garment, Stretching out  the heavens as a curtain,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:3">104:3</a> Who is laying the beam of His upper chambers in the  waters, Who is making thick clouds His chariot, Who is walking  on wings of wind,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:4">104:4</a> Making His messengers -- the winds, His ministers -- the  flaming fire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:5">104:5</a> He hath founded earth on its bases, It is not moved to the  age and for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:6">104:6</a> The abyss! as with clothing Thou hast covered it, Above  hills do waters stand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:7">104:7</a> From Thy rebuke they flee, From the voice of Thy thunder  haste away.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:8">104:8</a> They go up hills -- they go down valleys, Unto a place  Thou hast founded for them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:9">104:9</a> A border Thou hast set, they pass not over, They turn not  back to cover the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:10">104:10</a> Who is sending forth fountains in valleys, Between hills  they go on.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:11">104:11</a> They water every beast of the field, Wild asses break  their thirst.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:12">104:12</a> By them the fowl of the heavens doth dwell, From between  the branches They give forth the voice.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:13">104:13</a> Watering hills from His upper chambers, From the fruit of  Thy works is the earth satisfied.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:14">104:14</a> Causing grass to spring up for cattle, And herb for the  service of man, To bring forth bread from the earth,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:15">104:15</a> And wine -- it rejoiceth the heart of man, To cause the  face to shine from oil, And bread -- the heart of man it  supporteth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:16">104:16</a> Satisfied [are] the trees of Jehovah, Cedars of Lebanon  that He hath planted,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:17">104:17</a> Where birds do make nests, The stork -- the firs [are]  her house.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:18">104:18</a> The high hills [are] for wild goats, Rocks [are] a refuge  for conies,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:19">104:19</a> He made the moon for seasons, The sun hath known his  place of entrance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:20">104:20</a> Thou settest darkness, and it is night, In it doth every  beast of the forest creep.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:21">104:21</a> The young lions are roaring for prey, And to seek from  God their food.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:22">104:22</a> The sun riseth, they are gathered, And in their dens they  crouch.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:23">104:23</a> Man goeth forth to his work, And to his service -- till  evening.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:24">104:24</a> How many have been Thy works, O Jehovah, All of them in  wisdom Thou hast made, Full is the earth of thy possessions.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:25">104:25</a> This, the sea, great and broad of sides, There [are]  moving things -- innumerable, Living creatures -- small with  great.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:26">104:26</a> There do ships go: leviathan, That Thou hast formed to  play in it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:27">104:27</a> All of them unto Thee do look, To give their food in its  season.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:28">104:28</a> Thou dost give to them -- they gather, Thou dost open Thy  hand -- they [are] satisfied [with] good.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:29">104:29</a> Thou hidest Thy face -- they are troubled, Thou gatherest  their spirit -- they expire, And unto their dust they turn  back.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:30">104:30</a> Thou sendest out Thy Spirit, they are created, And Thou  renewest the face of the ground.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:31">104:31</a> The honour of Jehovah is to the age, Jehovah rejoiceth in  His works,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:32">104:32</a> Who is looking to earth, and it trembleth, He cometh  against hills, and they smoke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:33">104:33</a> I sing to Jehovah during my life, I sing praise to my God  while I exist.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:34">104:34</a> Sweet is my meditation on Him, I -- I do rejoice in  Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_104:35">104:35</a> Consumed are sinners from the earth, And the wicked are  no more. Bless, O my soul, Jehovah. Praise ye Jehovah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:1">105:1</a> Give ye thanks to Jehovah -- call ye in His name, Make  known among the peoples His acts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:2">105:2</a> Sing ye to Him -- sing praise to Him, Meditate ye on all  His wonders.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:3">105:3</a> Boast yourselves in His Holy Name, The heart of those  seeking Jehovah rejoiceth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:4">105:4</a> Seek ye Jehovah and His strength, Seek ye His face  continually.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:5">105:5</a> Remember His wonders that He did, His signs and the  judgments of His mouth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:6">105:6</a> O seed of Abraham, His servant, O sons of Jacob, His  chosen ones.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:7">105:7</a> He [is] Jehovah our God, In all the earth [are] His  judgments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:8">105:8</a> He hath remembered to the age His covenant, The word He  commanded to a thousand generations,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:9">105:9</a> That He hath made with Abraham, And His oath to Isaac,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:10">105:10</a> And doth establish it to Jacob for a statute, To Israel  -- a covenant age-during,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:11">105:11</a> Saying, `To thee I give the land of Canaan, The portion  of your inheritance,'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:12">105:12</a> In their being few in number, But a few, and sojourners  in it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:13">105:13</a> And they go up and down, from nation unto nation, From a  kingdom unto another people.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:14">105:14</a> He hath not suffered any to oppress them And He reproveth  for their sakes kings.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:15">105:15</a> `Strike not against Mine anointed, And to My prophets do  not evil.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:16">105:16</a> And He calleth a famine on the land, The whole staff of  bread He hath broken.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:17">105:17</a> He hath sent before them a man, For a servant hath Joseph  been sold.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:18">105:18</a> They have afflicted with fetters his feet, Iron hath  entered his soul,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:19">105:19</a> Till the time of the coming of His word The saying of  Jehovah hath tried him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:20">105:20</a> The king hath sent, and looseth him, The ruler of the  peoples, and draweth him out.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:21">105:21</a> He hath made him lord of his house, And ruler over all  his possessions.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:22">105:22</a> To bind his chiefs at his pleasure, And his elders he  maketh wise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:23">105:23</a> And Israel cometh in to Egypt, And Jacob hath sojourned  in the land of Ham.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:24">105:24</a> And He maketh His people very fruitful, And maketh it  mightier than its adversaries.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:25">105:25</a> He turned their heart to hate His people, To conspire  against His servants.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:26">105:26</a> He hath sent Moses His servant, Aaron whom He had fixed  on.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:27">105:27</a> They have set among them the matters of His signs, And  wonders in the land of Ham.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:28">105:28</a> He hath sent darkness, and it is dark, And they have not  provoked His word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:29">105:29</a> He hath turned their waters to blood, And putteth to  death their fish.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:30">105:30</a> Teemed hath their land [with] frogs, In the inner  chambers of their kings.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:31">105:31</a> He hath said, and the beetle cometh, Lice into all their  border.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:32">105:32</a> He hath made their showers hail, A flaming fire [is] in  their land.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:33">105:33</a> And He smiteth their vine and their fig, And shivereth  the trees of their border.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:34">105:34</a> He hath said, and the locust cometh, And the cankerworm  -- innumerable,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:35">105:35</a> And it consumeth every herb in their land, And it  consumeth the fruit of their ground.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:36">105:36</a> And He smiteth every first-born in their land, The  first-fruit of all their strength,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:37">105:37</a> And bringeth them out with silver and gold, And there is  not in its tribes a feeble one.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:38">105:38</a> Rejoiced hath Egypt in their going forth, For their fear  had fallen upon them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:39">105:39</a> He hath spread a cloud for a covering, And fire to  enlighten the night.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:40">105:40</a> They have asked, and He bringeth quails, And [with] bread  of heaven satisfieth them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:41">105:41</a> He hath opened a rock, and waters issue, They have gone  on in dry places -- a river.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:42">105:42</a> For He hath remembered His holy word, With Abraham His  servant,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:43">105:43</a> And He bringeth forth His people with joy, With singing  His chosen ones.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:44">105:44</a> And He giveth to them the lands of nations, And the  labour of peoples they possess,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_105:45">105:45</a> That they may observe His statutes, And His laws may  keep. Praise ye Jehovah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:1">106:1</a> Praise ye Jah, give thanks to Jehovah, For good, for to  the age, [is] His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:2">106:2</a> Who doth utter the mighty acts of Jehovah? Soundeth all  His praise?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:3">106:3</a> O the happiness of those keeping judgment, Doing  righteousness at all times.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:4">106:4</a> Remember me, O Jehovah, With the favour of Thy people,  Look after me in Thy salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:5">106:5</a> To look on the good of Thy chosen ones, To rejoice in the  joy of Thy nation, To boast myself with Thine inheritance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:6">106:6</a> We have sinned with our fathers, We have done perversely,  we have done wickedly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:7">106:7</a> Our fathers in Egypt, Have not considered wisely Thy  wonders, They have not remembered The abundance of Thy kind  acts, And provoke by the sea, at the sea of Suph.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:8">106:8</a> And He saveth them for His name's sake, To make known His  might,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:9">106:9</a> And rebuketh the sea of Suph, and it is dried up, And  causeth them to go Through depths as a wilderness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:10">106:10</a> And He saveth them from the hand Of him who is hating,  And redeemeth them from the hand of the enemy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:11">106:11</a> And waters cover their adversaries, One of them hath not  been left.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:12">106:12</a> And they believe in His words, they sing His praise,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:13">106:13</a> They have hasted -- forgotten His works, They have not  waited for His counsel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:14">106:14</a> And they lust greatly in a wilderness, And try God in a  desert.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:15">106:15</a> And He giveth to them their request, And sendeth leanness  into their soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:16">106:16</a> And they are envious of Moses in the camp, Of Aaron,  Jehovah's holy one.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:17">106:17</a> Earth openeth, and swalloweth up Dathan, And covereth  over the company of Abiram.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:18">106:18</a> And fire burneth among their company, A flame setteth on  fire the wicked.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:19">106:19</a> They make a calf in Horeb, And bow themselves to a molten  image,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:20">106:20</a> And change their Honour Into the form of an ox eating  herbs.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:21">106:21</a> They have forgotten God their saviour, The doer of great  things in Egypt,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:22">106:22</a> Of wonderful things in the land of Ham, Of fearful things  by the sea of Suph.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:23">106:23</a> And He saith to destroy them, Unless Moses, His chosen  one, Had stood in the breach before Him, To turn back His wrath  from destroying.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:24">106:24</a> And they kick against the desirable land, They have not  given credence to His word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:25">106:25</a> And they murmur in their tents, They have not hearkened  to the voice of Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:26">106:26</a> And He lifteth up His hand to them, To cause them to fall  in a wilderness,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:27">106:27</a> And to cause their seed to fall among nations, And to  scatter them through lands.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:28">106:28</a> And they are coupled to Baal-Peor, And eat the sacrifices  of the dead,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:29">106:29</a> And they provoke to anger by their actions, And a plague  breaketh forth upon them,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:30">106:30</a> And Phinehas standeth, and executeth judgment, And the  plague is restrained,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:31">106:31</a> And it is reckoned to him to righteousness, To all  generations -- unto the age.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:32">106:32</a> And they cause wrath by the waters of Meribah, And it is  evil to Moses for their sakes,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:33">106:33</a> For they have provoked his spirit, And he speaketh  wrongfully with his lips.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:34">106:34</a> They have not destroyed the peoples, As Jehovah had said  to them,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:35">106:35</a> And mix themselves among nations, and learn their works,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:36">106:36</a> And serve their idols, And they are to them for a snare.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:37">106:37</a> And they sacrifice their sons And their daughters to  destroyers,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:38">106:38</a> And they shed innocent blood -- Blood of their sons and  of their daughters, Whom they have sacrificed to idols of  Canaan, And the land is profaned with blood.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:39">106:39</a> And they are defiled with their works, And commit  whoredom in their habitual doings.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:40">106:40</a> And the anger of Jehovah Is kindled against His people,  And He doth abominate His inheritance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:41">106:41</a> And giveth them into the hand of nations, And those  hating them rule over them,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:42">106:42</a> And their enemies oppress them, And they are humbled  under their hand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:43">106:43</a> Many times He doth deliver them, And they rebel in their  counsel, And they are brought low in their iniquity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:44">106:44</a> And He looketh on their distress When He heareth their  cry,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:45">106:45</a> And remembereth for them His covenant, And is comforted,  According to the abundance of His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:46">106:46</a> And He appointeth them for mercies Before all their  captors.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:47">106:47</a> Save us, O Jehovah our God, and gather us from the  nations, To give thanks to Thy holy name, To glory in Thy  praise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_106:48">106:48</a> Blessed [is] Jehovah, God of Israel, From the age even  unto the age. And all the people said, `Amen, praise Jah!'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:1">107:1</a> `Give ye thanks to Jehovah, For good, for to the age [is]  His kindness:'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:2">107:2</a> Let the redeemed of Jehovah say, Whom He redeemed from the  hand of an adversary.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:3">107:3</a> And from the lands hath gathered them, From east and from  west, From north, and from the sea.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:4">107:4</a> They wandered in a wilderness, in a desert by the way, A  city of habitation they have not found.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:5">107:5</a> Hungry -- yea -- thirsty, Their soul in them becometh  feeble,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:6">107:6</a> And they cry unto Jehovah in their adversity, From their  distress He delivereth them,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:7">107:7</a> And causeth them to tread in a right way, To go unto a  city of habitation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:8">107:8</a> They confess to Jehovah His kindness, And His wonders to  the sons of men.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:9">107:9</a> For He hath satisfied a longing soul, And a hungry soul  hath filled [with] goodness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:10">107:10</a> Inhabitants of dark places and death-shade, Prisoners of  affliction and of iron,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:11">107:11</a> Because they changed the saying of God, And the counsel  of the Most High despised.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:12">107:12</a> And He humbleth with labour their heart, They have been  feeble, and there is no helper.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:13">107:13</a> And they cry unto Jehovah in their adversity, From their  distresses He saveth them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:14">107:14</a> He bringeth them out from the dark place, And  death-shade, And their bands He draweth away.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:15">107:15</a> They confess to Jehovah His kindness, And His wonders to  the sons of men.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:16">107:16</a> For He hath broken doors of brass, And bars of iron He  hath cut.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:17">107:17</a> Fools, by means of their transgression, And by their  iniquities, afflict themselves.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:18">107:18</a> All food doth their soul abominate, And they come nigh  unto the gates of death,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:19">107:19</a> And cry unto Jehovah in their adversity, From their  distresses He saveth them,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:20">107:20</a> He sendeth His word and healeth them, And delivereth from  their destructions.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:21">107:21</a> They confess to Jehovah His kindness, And His wonders to  the sons of men,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:22">107:22</a> And they sacrifice sacrifices of thanksgiving, And  recount His works with singing.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:23">107:23</a> Those going down [to] the sea in ships, Doing business in  many waters,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:24">107:24</a> They have seen the works of Jehovah, And His wonders in  the deep.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:25">107:25</a> And He saith, and appointeth a tempest, And it lifteth up  its billows,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:26">107:26</a> They go up [to] the heavens, they go down [to] the  depths, Their soul in evil is melted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:27">107:27</a> They reel to and fro, and move as a drunkard, And all  their wisdom is swallowed up.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:28">107:28</a> And they cry to Jehovah in their adversity, And from  their distresses He bringeth them out.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:29">107:29</a> He establisheth a whirlwind to a calm, And hushed are  their billows.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:30">107:30</a> And they rejoice because they are quiet, And He leadeth  them to the haven of their desire.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:31">107:31</a> They confess to Jehovah His kindness, And His wonders to  the sons of men,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:32">107:32</a> And they exalt Him in the assembly of the people, And in  the seat of the elders praise Him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:33">107:33</a> He maketh rivers become a wilderness, And fountains of  waters become dry land.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:34">107:34</a> A fruitful land becometh a barren place, For the  wickedness of its inhabitants.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:35">107:35</a> He maketh a wilderness become a pool of water, And a dry  land become fountains of waters.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:36">107:36</a> And He causeth the hungry to dwell there, And they  prepare a city of habitation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:37">107:37</a> And they sow fields, and plant vineyards, And they make  fruits of increase.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:38">107:38</a> And He blesseth them, and they multiply exceedingly, And  their cattle He doth not diminish.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:39">107:39</a> And they are diminished, and bow down, By restraint,  evil, and sorrow.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:40">107:40</a> He is pouring contempt upon nobles, And causeth them to  wander in vacancy -- no way.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:41">107:41</a> And setteth on high the needy from affliction, And  placeth families as a flock.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:42">107:42</a> The upright do see and rejoice, And all perversity hath  shut her mouth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_107:43">107:43</a> Who [is] wise, and observeth these? They understand the  kind acts of Jehovah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:1">108:1</a> A Song, a Psalm of David. Prepared is my heart, O God, I  sing, yea, I sing praise, also my honour.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:2">108:2</a> Awake, psaltery and harp, I awake the dawn.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:3">108:3</a> I thank Thee among peoples, O Jehovah, And I praise Thee  among the nations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:4">108:4</a> For great above the heavens [is] Thy kindness, And unto  the clouds Thy truth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:5">108:5</a> Be Thou exalted above the heavens, O God, And above all  the earth Thy honour.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:6">108:6</a> That Thy beloved ones may be delivered, Save [with] Thy  right hand, and answer us.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:7">108:7</a> God hath spoken in His holiness: I exult, I apportion  Shechem, And the valley of Succoth I measure,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:8">108:8</a> Mine [is] Gilead, mine [is] Manasseh, And Ephraim [is] the  strength of my head, Judah [is] my lawgiver,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:9">108:9</a> Moab [is] a pot for my washing, Upon Edom I cast my shoe,  Over Philistia I shout habitually.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:10">108:10</a> Who doth bring me in to the fenced city? Who hath led me  unto Edom?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:11">108:11</a> Hast not Thou, O God, cast us off? And Thou goest not  out, O God, with our hosts!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:12">108:12</a> Give to us help from adversity, And vain is the salvation  of man.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_108:13">108:13</a> In God we do mightily, And He doth tread down our  adversaries!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:1">109:1</a> To the Overseer. -- A Psalm of David. O God of my praise,  be not silent,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:2">109:2</a> For the mouth of wickedness, and the mouth of deceit,  Against me they have opened, They have spoken with me -- A  tongue of falsehood, and words of hatred!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:3">109:3</a> They have compassed me about, And they fight me without  cause.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:4">109:4</a> For my love they oppose me, and I -- prayer!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:5">109:5</a> And they set against me evil for good, And hatred for my  love.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:6">109:6</a> Appoint Thou over him the wicked, And an adversary  standeth at his right hand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:7">109:7</a> In his being judged, he goeth forth wicked, And his prayer  is for sin.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:8">109:8</a> His days are few, his oversight another taketh,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:9">109:9</a> His sons are fatherless, and his wife a widow.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:10">109:10</a> And wander continually do his sons, Yea, they have  begged, And have sought out of their dry places.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:11">109:11</a> An exactor layeth a snare for all that he hath, And  strangers spoil his labour.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:12">109:12</a> He hath none to extend kindness, Nor is there one showing  favour to his orphans.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:13">109:13</a> His posterity is for cutting off, In another generation  is their name blotted out.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:14">109:14</a> The iniquity of his fathers Is remembered unto Jehovah,  And the sin of his mother is not blotted out.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:15">109:15</a> They are before Jehovah continually, And He cutteth off  from earth their memorial.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:16">109:16</a> Because that he hath not remembered to do kindness, And  pursueth the poor man and needy, And the smitten of heart -- to  slay,</p>
