 <p><a name="an_109:17">109:17</a> And he loveth reviling, and it meeteth him, And he hath  not delighted in blessing, And it is far from him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:18">109:18</a> And he putteth on reviling as his robe, And it cometh in  as water into his midst, And as oil into his bones.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:19">109:19</a> It is to him as apparel -- he covereth himself, And for a  continual girdle he girdeth it on.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:20">109:20</a> This [is] the wage of mine accusers from Jehovah, And of  those speaking evil against my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:21">109:21</a> And Thou, O Jehovah Lord, Deal with me for Thy name's  sake, Because Thy kindness [is] good, deliver me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:22">109:22</a> For I [am] poor and needy, And my heart hath been pierced  in my midst.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:23">109:23</a> As a shadow when it is stretched out I have gone, I have  been driven away as a locust.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:24">109:24</a> My knees have been feeble from fasting, And my flesh hath  failed of fatness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:25">109:25</a> And I -- I have been a reproach to them, They see me,  they shake their head.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:26">109:26</a> Help me, O Jehovah my God, Save me, according to Thy  kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:27">109:27</a> And they know that this [is] Thy hand, Thou, O Jehovah,  Thou hast done it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:28">109:28</a> They revile, and Thou dost bless, They have risen, and  are ashamed, And Thy servant doth rejoice.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:29">109:29</a> Mine accusers put on blushing, and are covered, As an  upper robe [is] their shame.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:30">109:30</a> I thank Jehovah greatly with my mouth, And in the midst  of many I praise Him,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_109:31">109:31</a> For He standeth at the right hand of the needy, To save  from those judging his soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:1">110:1</a> A Psalm of David. The affirmation of Jehovah to my Lord:  `Sit at My right hand, Till I make thine enemies thy  footstool.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:2">110:2</a> The rod of thy strength doth Jehovah send from Zion, Rule  in the midst of thine enemies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:3">110:3</a> Thy people [are] free-will gifts in the day of Thy  strength, in the honours of holiness, From the womb, from the  morning, Thou hast the dew of thy youth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:4">110:4</a> Jehovah hath sworn, and doth not repent, `Thou [art] a  priest to the age, According to the order of Melchizedek.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:5">110:5</a> The Lord on thy right hand smote kings In the day of His  anger.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:6">110:6</a> He doth judge among the nations, He hath completed the  carcases, Hath smitten the head over the mighty earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_110:7">110:7</a> From a brook in the way he drinketh, Therefore he doth  lift up the head!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:1">111:1</a> Praise ye Jah! I thank Jehovah with the whole heart, In  the secret meeting of the upright, And of the company.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:2">111:2</a> Great [are] the works of Jehovah, Sought out by all  desiring them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:3">111:3</a> Honourable and majestic is His work, And His righteousness  is standing for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:4">111:4</a> A memorial He hath made of His wonders, Gracious and  merciful [is] Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:5">111:5</a> Prey He hath given to those fearing Him, He remembereth to  the age His covenant.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:6">111:6</a> The power of His works He hath declared to His people, To  give to them the inheritance of nations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:7">111:7</a> The works of His hands [are] true and just, Stedfast [are]  all His appointments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:8">111:8</a> They are sustained for ever to the age. They are made in  truth and uprightness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:9">111:9</a> Redemption He hath sent to His people, He hath appointed  to the age His covenant, Holy and fearful [is] His name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_111:10">111:10</a> The beginning of wisdom [is] fear of Jehovah, Good  understanding have all doing them, His praise [is] standing for  ever!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:1">112:1</a> Praise ye Jah! O the happiness of one fearing Jehovah, In  His commands he hath delighted greatly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:2">112:2</a> Mighty in the earth is his seed, The generation of the  upright is blessed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:3">112:3</a> Wealth and riches [are] in his house, And his  righteousness is standing for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:4">112:4</a> Light hath risen in darkness to the upright, Gracious, and  merciful, and righteous.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:5">112:5</a> Good [is] the man -- gracious and lending, He sustaineth  his matters in judgment.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:6">112:6</a> For -- to the age he is not moved; For a memorial  age-during is the righteous.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:7">112:7</a> Of an evil report he is not afraid, Prepared is His heart,  confident in Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:8">112:8</a> Sustained is his heart -- he feareth not, Till that he  look on his adversaries.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:9">112:9</a> He hath scattered -- hath given to the needy, His  righteousness is standing for ever, His horn is exalted with  honour.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_112:10">112:10</a> The wicked seeth, and hath been angry, His teeth he  gnasheth, and hath melted, The desire of the wicked doth  perish!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:1">113:1</a> Praise ye Jah! Praise, ye servants of Jehovah. Praise the  name of Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:2">113:2</a> The name of Jehovah is blessed, From henceforth, and unto  the age.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:3">113:3</a> From the rising of the sun unto its going in, Praised [is]  the name of Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:4">113:4</a> High above all nations [is] Jehovah, Above the heavens  [is] his honour.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:5">113:5</a> Who [is] as Jehovah our God, He is exalting [Himself] to  sit?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:6">113:6</a> He is humbling [Himself] to look On the heavens and on the  earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:7">113:7</a> He is raising up from the dust the poor, From a dunghill  He exalteth the needy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:8">113:8</a> To cause to sit with princes, With the princes of His  people.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_113:9">113:9</a> Causing the barren one of the house to sit, A joyful  mother of sons; praise ye Jah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:1">114:1</a> In the going out of Israel from Egypt, The house of Jacob  from a strange people,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:2">114:2</a> Judah became His sanctuary, Israel his dominion.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:3">114:3</a> The sea hath seen, and fleeth, The Jordan turneth  backward.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:4">114:4</a> The mountains have skipped as rams, Heights as sons of a  flock.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:5">114:5</a> What -- to thee, O sea, that thou fleest? O Jordan, thou  turnest back!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:6">114:6</a> O mountains, ye skip as rams! O heights, as sons of a  flock!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:7">114:7</a> From before the Lord be afraid, O earth, From before the  God of Jacob,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_114:8">114:8</a> He is turning the rock to a pool of waters, The flint to a  fountain of waters!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:1">115:1</a> Not to us, O Jehovah, not to us, But to Thy name give  honour, For Thy kindness, for Thy truth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:2">115:2</a> Why do the nations say, `Where, pray, [is] their God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:3">115:3</a> And our God [is] in the heavens, All that He hath pleased  He hath done.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:4">115:4</a> Their idols [are] silver and gold, work of man's hands,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:5">115:5</a> A mouth they have, and they speak not, Eyes they have, and  they see not,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:6">115:6</a> Ears they have, and they hear not, A nose they have, and  they smell not,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:7">115:7</a> Their hands, but they handle not, Their feet, and they  walk not;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:8">115:8</a> Nor do they mutter through their throat, Like them are  their makers, Every one who is trusting in them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:9">115:9</a> O Israel, trust in Jehovah, `Their help and their shield  [is] He.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:10">115:10</a> O house of Aaron, trust in Jehovah, `Their help and their  shield [is] He.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:11">115:11</a> Ye fearing Jehovah, trust in Jehovah, `Their help and  their shield [is] He.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:12">115:12</a> Jehovah hath remembered us, He blesseth, He blesseth the  house of Israel, He blesseth the house of Aaron,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:13">115:13</a> He blesseth those fearing Jehovah, The small with the  great.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:14">115:14</a> Jehovah addeth to you, to you, and to your sons.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:15">115:15</a> Blessed [are] ye of Jehovah, maker of heaven and earth,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:16">115:16</a> The heavens -- the heavens [are] Jehovah's, And the earth  He hath given to sons of men,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:17">115:17</a> The dead praise not Jah, Nor any going down to silence.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_115:18">115:18</a> And we, we bless Jah, From henceforth, and unto the age.  Praise ye Jah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:1">116:1</a> I have loved, because Jehovah heareth My voice, my  supplication,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:2">116:2</a> Because He hath inclined His ear to me, And during my days  I call.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:3">116:3</a> Compassed me have cords of death, And straits of Sheol  have found me, Distress and sorrow I find.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:4">116:4</a> And in the name of Jehovah I call: I pray Thee, O Jehovah,  deliver my soul,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:5">116:5</a> Gracious [is] Jehovah, and righteous, Yea, our God [is]  merciful,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:6">116:6</a> A preserver of the simple [is] Jehovah, I was low, and to  me He giveth salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:7">116:7</a> Turn back, O my soul, to thy rest, For Jehovah hath  conferred benefits on thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:8">116:8</a> For Thou hast delivered my soul from death, My eyes from  tears, my feet from overthrowing.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:9">116:9</a> I walk habitually before Jehovah In the lands of the  living.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:10">116:10</a> I have believed, for I speak, I -- I have been afflicted  greatly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:11">116:11</a> I said in my haste, `Every man [is] a liar.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:12">116:12</a> What do I return to Jehovah? All His benefits [are] upon  me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:13">116:13</a> The cup of salvation I lift up, And in the name of  Jehovah I call.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:14">116:14</a> My vows to Jehovah let me complete, I pray you, before  all His people.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:15">116:15</a> Precious in the eyes of Jehovah [is] the death for His  saints.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:16">116:16</a> Cause [it] to come, O Jehovah, for I [am] Thy servant. I  [am] Thy servant, son of Thy handmaid, Thou hast opened my  bonds.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:17">116:17</a> To Thee I sacrifice a sacrifice of thanks, And in the  name of Jehovah I call.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:18">116:18</a> My vows to Jehovah let me complete, I pray you, before  all His people,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_116:19">116:19</a> In the courts of the house of Jehovah, In thy midst, O  Jerusalem, praise ye Jah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:1">117:1</a> Praise Jehovah, all ye nations, Glorify Him, all ye  peoples.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_117:2">117:2</a> For mighty to us hath been His kindness, And the truth of  Jehovah [is] to the age. Praise ye Jah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:1">118:1</a> Give ye thanks to Jehovah, For good, for to the age [is]  His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:2">118:2</a> I pray you, let Israel say, That, to the age [is] His  kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:3">118:3</a> I pray you, let the house of Aaron say, That, to the age  [is] His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:4">118:4</a> I pray you, let those fearing Jehovah say, That, to the  age [is] His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:5">118:5</a> From the straitness I called Jah, Jah answered me in a  broad place.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:6">118:6</a> Jehovah [is] for me, I do not fear what man doth to me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:7">118:7</a> Jehovah [is] for me among my helpers, And I -- I look on  those hating me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:8">118:8</a> Better to take refuge in Jehovah than to trust in man,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:9">118:9</a> Better to take refuge in Jehovah, Than to trust in  princes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:10">118:10</a> All nations have compassed me about, In the name of  Jehovah I surely cut them off.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:11">118:11</a> They have compassed me about, Yea, they have compassed me  about, In the name of Jehovah I surely cut them off.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:12">118:12</a> They compassed me about as bees, They have been  extinguished as a fire of thorns, In the name of Jehovah I  surely cut them off.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:13">118:13</a> Thou hast sorely thrust me to fall, And Jehovah hath  helped me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:14">118:14</a> My strength and song [is] Jah, And He is to me for  salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:15">118:15</a> A voice of singing and salvation, [Is] in the tents of  the righteous, The right hand of Jehovah is doing valiantly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:16">118:16</a> The right hand of Jehovah is exalted, The right hand of  Jehovah is doing valiantly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:17">118:17</a> I do not die, but live, And recount the works of Jah,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:18">118:18</a> Jah hath sorely chastened me, And to death hath not given  me up.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:19">118:19</a> Open ye to me gates of righteousness, I enter into them  -- I thank Jah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:20">118:20</a> This [is] the gate to Jehovah, The righteous enter into  it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:21">118:21</a> I thank Thee, for Thou hast answered me, And art to me  for salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:22">118:22</a> A stone the builders refused Hath become head of a  corner.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:23">118:23</a> From Jehovah hath this been, It [is] wonderful in our  eyes,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:24">118:24</a> This [is] the day Jehovah hath made, We rejoice and are  glad in it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:25">118:25</a> I beseech Thee, O Jehovah, save, I pray Thee, I beseech  Thee, O Jehovah, prosper, I pray Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:26">118:26</a> Blessed [is] he who is coming In the name of Jehovah, We  blessed you from the house of Jehovah,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:27">118:27</a> God [is] Jehovah, and He giveth to us light, Direct ye  the festal-sacrifice with cords, Unto the horns of the altar.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:28">118:28</a> My God Thou [art], and I confess Thee, My God, I exalt  Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_118:29">118:29</a> Give ye thanks to Jehovah, For good, for to the age, [is]  His kindness!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:1">119:1</a> [Aleph.] O the happiness of those perfect in the way, They  are walking in the law of Jehovah,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:2">119:2</a> O the happiness of those keeping His testimonies, With the  whole heart they seek Him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:3">119:3</a> Yea, they have not done iniquity, In His ways they have  walked.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:4">119:4</a> Thou hast commanded us Thy precepts to keep diligently,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:5">119:5</a> O that my ways were prepared to keep Thy statutes,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:6">119:6</a> Then I am not ashamed In my looking unto all Thy commands.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:7">119:7</a> I confess Thee with uprightness of heart, In my learning  the judgments of Thy righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:8">119:8</a> Thy statutes I keep, leave me not utterly!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:9">119:9</a> [Beth.] With what doth a young man purify his path? To  observe -- according to Thy word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:10">119:10</a> With all my heart I have sought Thee, Let me not err from  Thy commands.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:11">119:11</a> In my heart I have hid Thy saying, That I sin not before  Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:12">119:12</a> Blessed [art] Thou, O Jehovah, teach me Thy statutes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:13">119:13</a> With my lips I have recounted All the judgments of Thy  mouth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:14">119:14</a> In the way of Thy testimonies I have joyed, As over all  wealth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:15">119:15</a> In Thy precepts I meditate, And I behold attentively Thy  paths.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:16">119:16</a> In Thy statutes I delight myself, I do not forget Thy  word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:17">119:17</a> [Gimel.] Confer benefits on Thy servant, I live, and I  keep Thy word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:18">119:18</a> Uncover mine eyes, and I behold wonders out of Thy law.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:19">119:19</a> A sojourner I [am] on earth, Hide not from me Thy  commands.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:20">119:20</a> Broken hath my soul for desire Unto Thy judgments at all  times.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:21">119:21</a> Thou hast rebuked the cursed proud, Who are erring from  Thy commands.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:22">119:22</a> Remove from me reproach and contempt, For Thy testimonies  I have kept.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:23">119:23</a> Princes also sat -- against me they spoke, Thy servant  doth meditate in Thy statutes,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:24">119:24</a> Thy testimonies also [are] my delight, The men of my  counsel!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:25">119:25</a> [Daleth.] Cleaved to the dust hath my soul, Quicken me  according to Thy word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:26">119:26</a> My ways I have recounted, And Thou answerest me, teach me  Thy statutes,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:27">119:27</a> The way of Thy precepts cause me to understand, And I  meditate in Thy wonders.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:28">119:28</a> My soul hath dropped from affliction, Establish me  according to Thy word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:29">119:29</a> The way of falsehood turn aside from me And with Thy law  favour me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:30">119:30</a> The way of faithfulness I have chosen, Thy judgments I  have compared,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:31">119:31</a> I have adhered to Thy testimonies, O Jehovah, put me not  to shame.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:32">119:32</a> The way of Thy commands I run, For Thou dost enlarge my  heart!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:33">119:33</a> [He.] Show me, O Jehovah, the way of Thy statutes, And I  keep it -- [to] the end.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:34">119:34</a> Cause me to understand, and I keep Thy law, And observe  it with the whole heart.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:35">119:35</a> Cause me to tread in the path of Thy commands, For in it  I have delighted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:36">119:36</a> Incline my heart unto Thy testimonies, And not unto  dishonest gain.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:37">119:37</a> Remove mine eyes from seeing vanity, In Thy way quicken  Thou me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:38">119:38</a> Establish to Thy servant Thy saying, That [is] concerning  Thy fear.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:39">119:39</a> Remove my reproach that I have feared, For Thy judgments  [are] good.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:40">119:40</a> Lo, I have longed for Thy precepts, In Thy righteousness  quicken Thou me,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:41">119:41</a> [Waw.] And meet me doth Thy kindness, O Jehovah, Thy  salvation according to Thy saying.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:42">119:42</a> And I answer him who is reproaching me a word, For I have  trusted in Thy word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:43">119:43</a> And Thou takest not utterly away From my mouth the word  of truth, Because for Thy judgment I have hoped.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:44">119:44</a> And I keep Thy law continually, To the age and for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:45">119:45</a> And I walk habitually in a broad place, For Thy precepts  I have sought.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:46">119:46</a> And I speak of Thy testimonies before kings, And I am not  ashamed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:47">119:47</a> And I delight myself in Thy commands, That I have loved,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:48">119:48</a> And I lift up my hands unto Thy commands, That I have  loved, And I do meditate on Thy statutes!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:49">119:49</a> [Zain.] Remember the word to Thy servant, On which Thou  hast caused me to hope.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:50">119:50</a> This [is] my comfort in mine affliction, That Thy saying  hath quickened me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:51">119:51</a> The proud have utterly scorned me, From Thy law I have  not turned aside.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:52">119:52</a> I remembered Thy judgments of old, O Jehovah, And I  comfort myself.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:53">119:53</a> Horror hath seized me, Because of the wicked forsaking  Thy law.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:54">119:54</a> Songs have been to me Thy statutes, In the house of my  sojournings.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:55">119:55</a> I have remembered in the night Thy name, O Jehovah, And I  do keep Thy law.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:56">119:56</a> This hath been to me, That Thy precepts I have kept!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:57">119:57</a> [Cheth.] My portion [is] Jehovah; I have said -- to keep  Thy words,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:58">119:58</a> I appeased Thy face with the whole heart, Favour me  according to Thy saying.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:59">119:59</a> I have reckoned my ways, And turn back my feet unto Thy  testimonies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:60">119:60</a> I have made haste, And delayed not, to keep Thy commands.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:61">119:61</a> Cords of the wicked have surrounded me, Thy law I have  not forgotten.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:62">119:62</a> At midnight I rise to give thanks to Thee, For the  judgments of Thy righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:63">119:63</a> A companion I [am] to all who fear Thee, And to those  keeping Thy precepts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:64">119:64</a> Of Thy kindness, O Jehovah, the earth is full, Thy  statutes teach Thou me!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:65">119:65</a> [Teth.] Good Thou didst with Thy servant, O Jehovah,  According to Thy word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:66">119:66</a> The goodness of reason and knowledge teach me, For in Thy  commands I have believed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:67">119:67</a> Before I am afflicted, I -- I am erring, And now Thy  saying I have kept.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:68">119:68</a> Good Thou [art], and doing good, Teach me Thy statutes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:69">119:69</a> Forged against me falsehood have the proud, I with the  whole heart keep Thy precepts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:70">119:70</a> Insensate as fat hath been their heart, I -- in Thy law I  have delighted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:71">119:71</a> Good for me that I have been afflicted, That I might  learn Thy statutes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:72">119:72</a> Better to me [is] the law of Thy mouth Than thousands of  gold and silver!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:73">119:73</a> [Yod.] Thy hands made me and establish me, Cause me to  understand, and I learn Thy commands.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:74">119:74</a> Those fearing Thee see me and rejoice, Because for Thy  word I have hoped.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:75">119:75</a> I have known, O Jehovah, That righteous [are] Thy  judgments, And [in] faithfulness Thou hast afflicted me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:76">119:76</a> Let, I pray Thee, Thy kindness be to comfort me,  According to Thy saying to Thy servant.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:77">119:77</a> Meet me do Thy mercies, and I live, For Thy law [is] my  delight.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:78">119:78</a> Ashamed are the proud, For [with] falsehood they dealt  perversely with me. I meditate in Thy precepts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:79">119:79</a> Those fearing Thee turn back to me, And those knowing Thy  testimonies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:80">119:80</a> My heart is perfect in Thy statutes, So that I am not  ashamed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:81">119:81</a> [Kaph.] Consumed for Thy salvation hath been my soul, For  Thy word I have hoped.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:82">119:82</a> Consumed have been mine eyes for Thy word, Saying, `When  doth it comfort me?'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:83">119:83</a> For I have been as a bottle in smoke, Thy statutes I have  not forgotten.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:84">119:84</a> How many [are] the days of Thy servant? When dost Thou  execute Against my pursuers judgment?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:85">119:85</a> The proud have digged for me pits, That [are] not  according to Thy law.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:86">119:86</a> All Thy commands [are] faithfulness, [With] falsehood  they have pursued me, Help Thou me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:87">119:87</a> Almost consumed me on earth have they, And I -- I have  not forsaken Thy precepts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:88">119:88</a> According to Thy kindness quicken Thou me, And I keep the  testimony of Thy mouth!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:89">119:89</a> [Lamed.] To the age, O Jehovah, Thy word is set up in the  heavens.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:90">119:90</a> To all generations Thy faithfulness, Thou didst establish  earth, and it standeth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:91">119:91</a> According to Thine ordinances They have stood this day,  for the whole [are] Thy servants.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:92">119:92</a> Unless Thy law [were] my delights, Then had I perished in  mine affliction.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:93">119:93</a> To the age I forget not Thy precepts, For by them Thou  hast quickened me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:94">119:94</a> I [am] Thine, save Thou me, For Thy precepts I have  sought.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:95">119:95</a> Thy wicked waited for me to destroy me, Thy testimonies I  understand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:96">119:96</a> Of all perfection I have seen an end, Broad [is] Thy  command -- exceedingly!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:97">119:97</a> [Mem.] O how I have loved Thy law! All the day it [is] my  meditation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:98">119:98</a> Than mine enemies Thy command maketh me wiser, For it  [is] before me to the age.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:99">119:99</a> Above all my teachers I have acted wisely. For Thy  testimonies [are] my meditation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:100">119:100</a> Above elders I understand more, For Thy precepts I have  kept.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:101">119:101</a> From every evil path I restrained my feet, So that I  keep Thy word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:102">119:102</a> From Thy judgments I turned not aside, For Thou -- Thou  hast directed me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:103">119:103</a> How sweet to my palate hath been Thy saying, Above honey  to my mouth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:104">119:104</a> From Thy precepts I have understanding, Therefore I have  hated every false path!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:105">119:105</a> [Nun.] A lamp to my foot [is] Thy word, And a light to  my path.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:106">119:106</a> I have sworn, and I confirm [it], To keep the judgments  of Thy righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:107">119:107</a> I have been afflicted very much, O Jehovah, quicken me,  according to Thy word.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:108">119:108</a> Free-will-offerings of my mouth, Accept, I pray Thee, O  Jehovah, And Thy judgments teach Thou me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:109">119:109</a> My soul [is] in my hand continually, And Thy law I have  not forgotten.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:110">119:110</a> The wicked have laid a snare for me, And from thy  precepts I wandered not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:111">119:111</a> I have inherited Thy testimonies to the age, For the joy  of my heart [are] they.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:112">119:112</a> I have inclined my heart To do Thy statutes, to the age  -- [to] the end!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:113">119:113</a> [Samech.] Doubting ones I have hated, And Thy law I have  loved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:114">119:114</a> My hiding place and my shield [art] Thou, For Thy word I  have hoped.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:115">119:115</a> Turn aside from me, ye evil-doers, And I keep the  commands of my God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:116">119:116</a> Sustain me according to Thy saying, And I live, and Thou  puttest me not to shame Because of my hope.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:117">119:117</a> Support Thou me, and I am saved, And I look on Thy  statutes continually.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:118">119:118</a> Thou hast trodden down All going astray from Thy  statutes, For falsehood [is] their deceit.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:119">119:119</a> Dross! Thou hast caused to cease All the wicked of the  earth; Therefore I have loved Thy testimonies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:120">119:120</a> Trembled from Thy fear hath my flesh, And from Thy  judgments I have been afraid!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:121">119:121</a> [Ain.] I have done judgment and righteousness, Leave me  not to mine oppressors.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:122">119:122</a> Make sure Thy servant for good, Let not the proud  oppress me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:123">119:123</a> Mine eyes have been consumed for Thy salvation. And for  the saying of Thy righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:124">119:124</a> Do with Thy servant according to Thy kindness. And Thy  statutes teach Thou me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:125">119:125</a> Thy servant [am] I -- cause me to understand, And I know  Thy testimonies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:126">119:126</a> Time for Jehovah to work! they have made void Thy law.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:127">119:127</a> Therefore I have loved Thy commands Above gold -- even  fine gold.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:128">119:128</a> Therefore all my appointments I have declared wholly  right, Every path of falsehood I have hated!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:129">119:129</a> [Pe.] Wonderful [are] Thy testimonies, Therefore hath my  soul kept them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:130">119:130</a> The opening of Thy words enlighteneth, Instructing the  simple.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:131">119:131</a> My mouth I have opened, yea, I pant, For, for Thy  commands I have longed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:132">119:132</a> Look unto me, and favour me, As customary to those  loving Thy name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:133">119:133</a> My steps establish by Thy saying, And any iniquity doth  not rule over me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:134">119:134</a> Ransom me from the oppression of man, And I observe Thy  precepts,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:135">119:135</a> Thy face cause to shine on Thy servant, And teach me Thy  statutes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:136">119:136</a> Rivulets of waters have come down mine eyes, Because  they have not kept Thy law!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:137">119:137</a> [Tzade.] Righteous [art] Thou, O Jehovah, And upright  [are] Thy judgments.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:138">119:138</a> Thou hast appointed Thy testimonies, Righteous and  exceeding faithful,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:139">119:139</a> Cut me off hath my zeal, For mine adversaries forgot Thy  words.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:140">119:140</a> Tried [is] thy saying exceedingly, And Thy servant hath  loved it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:141">119:141</a> Small I [am], and despised, Thy precepts I have not  forgotten.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:142">119:142</a> Thy righteousness [is] righteousness to the age, And Thy  law [is] truth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:143">119:143</a> Adversity and distress have found me, Thy commands [are]  my delights.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:144">119:144</a> The righteousness of Thy testimonies [is] to Cause me to  understand, and I live!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:145">119:145</a> [Koph.] I have called with the whole heart, Answer me, O  Jehovah, Thy statutes I keep,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:146">119:146</a> I have called Thee, save Thou me, And I do keep Thy  testimonies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:147">119:147</a> I have gone forward in the dawn, and I cry, For Thy word  I have hoped.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:148">119:148</a> Mine eyes have gone before the watches, To meditate in  Thy saying.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:149">119:149</a> My voice hear, according to Thy kindness, Jehovah,  according to Thy judgment quicken me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:150">119:150</a> Near have been my wicked pursuers, From Thy law they  have been far off.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:151">119:151</a> Near [art] Thou, O Jehovah, And all Thy commands [are]  truth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:152">119:152</a> Of old I have known Thy testimonies, That to the age  Thou hast founded them!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:153">119:153</a> [Resh.] See my affliction, and deliver Thou me, For Thy  law I have not forgotten.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:154">119:154</a> Plead my plea, and redeem me, According to Thy saying  quicken me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:155">119:155</a> Far from the wicked [is] salvation, For Thy statutes  they have not sought.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:156">119:156</a> Thy mercies [are] many, O Jehovah, According to Thy  judgments quicken me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:157">119:157</a> Many [are] my pursuers, and adversaries, From Thy  testimonies I have not turned aside.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:158">119:158</a> I have seen treacherous ones, And grieve myself, Because  Thy saying they have not kept.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:159">119:159</a> See, for thy precepts I have loved, Jehovah, According  to Thy kindness quicken me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:160">119:160</a> The sum of Thy word [is] truth, And to the age [is]  every judgment of Thy righteousness!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:161">119:161</a> [Shin.] Princes have pursued me without cause, And  because of Thy words was my heart afraid.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:162">119:162</a> I do rejoice concerning Thy saying, As one finding  abundant spoil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:163">119:163</a> Falsehood I have hated, yea I abominate [it], Thy law I  have loved.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:164">119:164</a> Seven [times] in a day I have praised Thee, Because of  the judgments of Thy righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:165">119:165</a> Abundant peace have those loving Thy law, And they have  no stumbling-block.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:166">119:166</a> I have waited for Thy salvation, O Jehovah, And Thy  commands I have done.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:167">119:167</a> Kept hath my soul Thy testimonies, And I do love them  exceedingly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:168">119:168</a> I have kept Thy precepts and Thy testimonies, For all my  ways are before Thee!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:169">119:169</a> [Taw.] My loud cry cometh near before Thee, O Jehovah;  According to Thy word cause me to understand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:170">119:170</a> My supplication cometh in before Thee, According to Thy  saying deliver Thou me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:171">119:171</a> My lips do utter praise, For Thou dost teach me Thy  statutes.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:172">119:172</a> My tongue doth sing of Thy saying, For all Thy commands  [are] righteous.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:173">119:173</a> Thy hand is for a help to me, For Thy commands I have  chosen.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:174">119:174</a> I have longed for Thy salvation, O Jehovah, And Thy law  [is] my delight.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:175">119:175</a> My soul liveth, and it doth praise Thee, And Thy  judgments do help me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_119:176">119:176</a> I wandered as a lost sheep, seek Thy servant, For Thy  precepts I have not forgotten!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:1">120:1</a> A Song of the Ascents. Unto Jehovah in my distress I have  called, And He answereth me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:2">120:2</a> O Jehovah, deliver my soul from a lying lip, From a  deceitful tongue!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:3">120:3</a> What doth He give to thee? And what doth He add to thee? O  deceitful tongue!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:4">120:4</a> Sharp arrows of a mighty one, with broom-coals.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:5">120:5</a> Wo to me, for I have inhabited Mesech, I have dwelt with  tents of Kedar.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:6">120:6</a> Too much hath my soul dwelt with him who is hating peace.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_120:7">120:7</a> I [am] peace, and when I speak they [are] for war!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:1">121:1</a> A Song of the Ascents. I lift up mine eyes unto the hills,  Whence doth my help come?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:2">121:2</a> My help [is] from Jehovah, maker of heaven and earth,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:3">121:3</a> He suffereth not thy foot to be moved, Thy preserver  slumbereth not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:4">121:4</a> Lo, He slumbereth not, nor sleepeth, He who is preserving  Israel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:5">121:5</a> Jehovah [is] thy preserver, Jehovah [is] thy shade on thy  right hand,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:6">121:6</a> By day the sun doth not smite thee, Nor the moon by night.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:7">121:7</a> Jehovah preserveth thee from all evil, He doth preserve  thy soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_121:8">121:8</a> Jehovah preserveth thy going out and thy coming in, From  henceforth even unto the age!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:1">122:1</a> A Song of the Ascents, by David. I have rejoiced in those  saying to me, `To the house of Jehovah we go.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:2">122:2</a> Our feet have been standing in thy gates, O Jerusalem!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:3">122:3</a> Jerusalem -- the builded one -- [Is] as a city that is  joined to itself together.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:4">122:4</a> For thither have tribes gone up, Tribes of Jah, companies  of Israel, To give thanks to the name of Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:5">122:5</a> For there have sat thrones of judgment, Thrones of the  house of David.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:6">122:6</a> Ask ye the peace of Jerusalem, At rest are those loving  thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:7">122:7</a> Peace is in thy bulwark, rest in thy high places,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:8">122:8</a> For the sake of my brethren and my companions, Let me  speak, I pray thee, `Peace [be] in thee.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_122:9">122:9</a> For the sake of the house of Jehovah our God, I seek good  for thee!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:1">123:1</a> A Song of the Ascents. Unto Thee I have lifted up mine  eyes, O dweller in the heavens.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:2">123:2</a> Lo, as eyes of men-servants [Are] unto the hand of their  masters, As eyes of a maid-servant [Are] unto the hand of her  mistress, So [are] our eyes unto Jehovah our God, Till that He  doth favour us.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:3">123:3</a> Favour us, O Jehovah, favour us, For greatly have we been  filled with contempt,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_123:4">123:4</a> Greatly hath our soul been filled With the scorning of the  easy ones, With the contempt of the arrogant!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:1">124:1</a> A Song of the Ascents, by David. Save [for] Jehovah -- who  hath been for us, (Pray, let Israel say),</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:2">124:2</a> Save [for] Jehovah -- who hath been for us, In the rising  up of man against us,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:3">124:3</a> Then alive they had swallowed us up, In the burning of  their anger against us,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:4">124:4</a> Then the waters had overflowed us, The stream passed over  our soul,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:5">124:5</a> Then passed over our soul had the proud waters.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:6">124:6</a> Blessed [is] Jehovah who hath not given us, A prey to  their teeth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:7">124:7</a> Our soul as a bird hath escaped from a snare of fowlers,  The snare was broken, and we have escaped.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_124:8">124:8</a> Our help [is] in the name of Jehovah, Maker of the heavens  and earth!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:1">125:1</a> A Song of the Ascents. Those trusting in Jehovah [are] as  Mount Zion, It is not moved -- to the age it abideth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:2">125:2</a> Jerusalem! mountains [are] round about her, And Jehovah  [is] round about His people, From henceforth even unto the age.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:3">125:3</a> For the rod of wickedness resteth not On the lot of the  righteous, That the righteous put not forth on iniquity their  hands.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:4">125:4</a> Do good, O Jehovah, to the good, And to the upright in  their hearts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_125:5">125:5</a> As to those turning [to] their crooked ways, Jehovah  causeth them to go with workers of iniquity. Peace on Israel!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:1">126:1</a> A Song of the Ascents. In Jehovah's turning back [to] the  captivity of Zion, We have been as dreamers.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:2">126:2</a> Then filled [with] laughter is our mouth, And our tongue  [with] singing, Then do they say among nations, `Jehovah did  great things with these.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:3">126:3</a> Jehovah did great things with us, We have been joyful.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:4">126:4</a> Turn again, O Jehovah, [to] our captivity, As streams in  the south.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:5">126:5</a> Those sowing in tears, with singing do reap,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_126:6">126:6</a> Whoso goeth on and weepeth, Bearing the basket of seed,  Surely cometh in with singing, bearing his sheaves!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:1">127:1</a> A Song of the Ascents, by Solomon. If Jehovah doth not  build the house, In vain have its builders laboured at it, If  Jehovah doth not watch a city, In vain hath a watchman waked.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:2">127:2</a> Vain for you who are rising early, Who delay sitting,  eating the bread of griefs, So He giveth to His beloved one  sleep.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:3">127:3</a> Lo, an inheritance of Jehovah [are] sons, A reward [is]  the fruit of the womb.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:4">127:4</a> As arrows in the hand of a mighty one, So [are] the sons  of the young men.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_127:5">127:5</a> O the happiness of the man Who hath filled his quiver with  them, They are not ashamed, For they speak with enemies in the  gate!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:1">128:1</a> A Song of the Ascents. O the happiness of every one  fearing Jehovah, Who is walking in His ways.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:2">128:2</a> The labour of thy hands thou surely eatest, Happy [art]  thou, and good [is] to thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:3">128:3</a> Thy wife [is] as a fruitful vine in the sides of thy  house, Thy sons as olive plants around thy table.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:4">128:4</a> Lo, surely thus is the man blessed who is fearing Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:5">128:5</a> Jehovah doth bless thee out of Zion, Look, then, on the  good of Jerusalem, All the days of thy life,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_128:6">128:6</a> And see the sons of thy sons! Peace on Israel!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:1">129:1</a> A Song of the Ascents. Often they distressed me from my  youth, Pray, let Israel say:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:2">129:2</a> Often they distressed me from my youth, Yet they have not  prevailed over me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:3">129:3</a> Over my back have ploughers ploughed, They have made long  their furrows.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:4">129:4</a> Jehovah [is] righteous, He hath cut asunder cords of the  wicked.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:5">129:5</a> Confounded and turn backward do all hating Zion.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:6">129:6</a> They are as grass of the roofs, That before it was drawn  out withereth,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:7">129:7</a> That hath not filled the hand of a reaper, And the bosom  of a binder of sheaves.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_129:8">129:8</a> And the passers by have not said, `The blessing of Jehovah  [is] on you, We blessed you in the Name of Jehovah!'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:1">130:1</a> A Song of the Ascents. From depths I have called Thee,  Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:2">130:2</a> Lord, hearken to my voice, Thine ears are attentive to the  voice of my supplications.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:3">130:3</a> If iniquities Thou dost observe, O Lord, who doth stand?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:4">130:4</a> But with Thee [is] forgiveness, that Thou mayest be  feared.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:5">130:5</a> I hoped [for] Jehovah -- hoped hath my soul, And for His  word I have waited.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:6">130:6</a> My soul [is] for the Lord, More than those watching for  morning, Watching for morning!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:7">130:7</a> Israel doth wait on Jehovah, For with Jehovah [is]  kindness, And abundant with Him [is] redemption.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_130:8">130:8</a> And He doth redeem Israel from all his iniquities!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:1">131:1</a> A Song of the Ascents, by David. Jehovah, my heart hath  not been haughty, Nor have mine eyes been high, Nor have I  walked in great things, And in things too wonderful for me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:2">131:2</a> Have I not compared, and kept silent my soul, As a weaned  one by its mother? As a weaned one by me [is] my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_131:3">131:3</a> Israel doth wait on Jehovah, From henceforth, and unto the  age!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:1">132:1</a> A Song of the Ascents. Remember, Jehovah, for David, all  his afflictions.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:2">132:2</a> Who hath sworn to Jehovah. He hath vowed to the Mighty One  of Jacob:</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:3">132:3</a> `If I enter into the tent of my house, If I go up on the  couch of my bed,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:4">132:4</a> If I give sleep to mine eyes, To mine eyelids -- slumber,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:5">132:5</a> Till I do find a place for Jehovah, Tabernacles for the  Mighty One of Jacob.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:6">132:6</a> `Lo, we have heard it in Ephratah, We have found it in the  fields of the forest.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:7">132:7</a> We come in to His tabernacles, We bow ourselves at His  footstool.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:8">132:8</a> Arise, O Jehovah, to Thy rest, Thou, and the ark of Thy  strength,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:9">132:9</a> Thy priests do put on righteousness, And Thy pious ones  cry aloud.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:10">132:10</a> For the sake of David Thy servant, Turn not back the face  of Thine anointed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:11">132:11</a> Jehovah hath sworn truth to David, He turneth not back  from it: Of the fruit of thy body, I set on the throne for  thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:12">132:12</a> If thy sons keep My covenant, And My testimonies that I  teach them, Their sons also for ever and ever, Do sit on the  throne for thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:13">132:13</a> For Jehovah hath fixed on Zion, He hath desired [it] for  a seat to Himself,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:14">132:14</a> This [is] My rest for ever and ever, Here do I sit, for I  have desired it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:15">132:15</a> Her provision I greatly bless, Her needy ones I satisfy  [with] bread,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:16">132:16</a> And her priests I clothe [with] salvation, And her pious  ones do sing aloud.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:17">132:17</a> There I cause to spring up a horn for David, I have  arranged a lamp for Mine anointed.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_132:18">132:18</a> His enemies I do clothe [with] shame, And upon him doth  his crown flourish!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_133:1">133:1</a> A Song of the Ascents, by David. Lo, how good and how  pleasant The dwelling of brethren -- even together!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_133:2">133:2</a> As the good oil on the head, Coming down on the beard, the  beard of Aaron, That cometh down on the skirt of his robes,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_133:3">133:3</a> As dew of Hermon -- That cometh down on hills of Zion, For  there Jehovah commanded the blessing -- Life unto the age!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:1">134:1</a> A Song of the Ascents. Lo, bless Jehovah, all servants of  Jehovah, Who are standing in the house of Jehovah by night.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:2">134:2</a> Lift up your hands [in] the sanctuary, And bless ye  Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_134:3">134:3</a> Jehovah doth bless thee out of Zion, The maker of the  heavens and earth!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:1">135:1</a> Praise ye Jah! Praise ye the name of Jehovah, Praise, ye  servants of Jehovah,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:2">135:2</a> Who are standing in the house of Jehovah, In the courts of  the house of our God.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:3">135:3</a> Praise ye Jah! for Jehovah [is] good, Sing praise to His  name, for [it is] pleasant.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:4">135:4</a> For Jacob hath Jah chosen for Himself, Israel for His  peculiar treasure.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:5">135:5</a> For I have known that great [is] Jehovah, Yea, our Lord  [is] above all gods.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:6">135:6</a> All that Jehovah pleased He hath done, In the heavens and  in earth, In the seas and all deep places,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:7">135:7</a> Causing vapours to ascend from the end of the earth,  Lightnings for the rain He hath made, Bringing forth wind from  His treasures.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:8">135:8</a> Who smote the first-born of Egypt, From man unto beast.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:9">135:9</a> He sent tokens and wonders into thy midst, O Egypt, On  Pharaoh and on all his servants.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:10">135:10</a> Who smote many nations, and slew strong kings,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:11">135:11</a> Even Sihon king of the Amorite, And Og king of Bashan,  And all kingdoms of Canaan.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:12">135:12</a> And He gave their land an inheritance, An inheritance to  Israel His people,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:13">135:13</a> O Jehovah, Thy name [is] to the age, O Jehovah, Thy  memorial to all generations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:14">135:14</a> For Jehovah doth judge His people, And for His servants  comforteth Himself.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:15">135:15</a> The idols of the nations [are] silver and gold, Work of  the hands of man.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:16">135:16</a> A mouth they have, and they speak not, Eyes they have,  and they see not,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:17">135:17</a> Ears they have, and they give not ear, Nose -- there is  no breath in their mouth!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:18">135:18</a> Like them are their makers, Every one who is trusting in  them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:19">135:19</a> O house of Israel, bless ye Jehovah, O house of Aaron,  bless ye Jehovah,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:20">135:20</a> O house of Levi, bless ye Jehovah, Those fearing Jehovah,  bless ye Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_135:21">135:21</a> Blessed [is] Jehovah from Zion, Inhabiting Jerusalem --  praise ye Jah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:1">136:1</a> Give ye thanks to Jehovah, For good, for to the age [is]  His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:2">136:2</a> Give ye thanks to the God of gods, For to the age [is] His  kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:3">136:3</a> Give ye thanks to the Lord of lords, For to the age [is]  His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:4">136:4</a> To Him doing great wonders by Himself alone, For to the  age [is] His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:5">136:5</a> To Him making the heavens by understanding, For to the age  [is] His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:6">136:6</a> To Him spreading the earth over the waters, For to the age  [is] His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:7">136:7</a> To Him making great lights, For to the age [is] His  kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:8">136:8</a> The sun to rule by day, For to the age [is] His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:9">136:9</a> The moon and stars to rule by night, For to the age [is]  His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:10">136:10</a> To Him smiting Egypt in their first-born, For to the age  [is] His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:11">136:11</a> And bringing forth Israel from their midst, For to the  age [is] His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:12">136:12</a> By a strong hand, and a stretched-out-arm, For to the age  [is] His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:13">136:13</a> To Him cutting the sea of Suph into parts, For to the age  [is] His kindness,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:14">136:14</a> And caused Israel to pass through its midst, For to the  age [is] His kindness,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:15">136:15</a> And shook out Pharaoh and his force in the sea of Suph,  For to the age [is] His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:16">136:16</a> To Him leading His people in a wilderness, For to the age  [is] His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:17">136:17</a> To Him smiting great kings, For to the age [is] His  kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:18">136:18</a> Yea, He doth slay honourable kings, For to the age [is]  His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:19">136:19</a> Even Sihon king of the Amorite, For to the age [is] His  kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:20">136:20</a> And Og king of Bashan, For to the age [is] His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:21">136:21</a> And He gave their land for inheritance, For to the age  [is] His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:22">136:22</a> An inheritance to Israel His servant, For to the age [is]  His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:23">136:23</a> Who in our lowliness hath remembered us, For to the age  [is] His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:24">136:24</a> And He delivereth us from our adversaries, For to the age  [is] His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:25">136:25</a> Giving food to all flesh, For to the age [is] His  kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_136:26">136:26</a> Give ye thanks to the God of the heavens, For to the age  [is] His kindness!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:1">137:1</a> By rivers of Babylon -- There we did sit, Yea, we wept  when we remembered Zion.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:2">137:2</a> On willows in its midst we hung our harps.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:3">137:3</a> For there our captors asked us the words of a song, And  our spoilers -- joy: `Sing ye to us of a song of Zion.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:4">137:4</a> How do we sing the song of Jehovah, On the land of a  stranger?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:5">137:5</a> If I forget thee, O Jerusalem, my right hand forgetteth!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:6">137:6</a> My tongue doth cleave to my palate, If I do not remember  thee, If I do not exalt Jerusalem above my chief joy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:7">137:7</a> Remember, Jehovah, for the sons of Edom, The day of  Jerusalem, Those saying, `Rase, rase to its foundation!'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:8">137:8</a> O daughter of Babylon, O destroyed one, O the happiness of  him who repayeth to thee thy deed, That thou hast done to us.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_137:9">137:9</a> O the happiness of him who doth seize, And hath dashed thy  sucklings on the rock!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:1">138:1</a> By David. I confess Thee, with all my heart, Before the  gods I do praise Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:2">138:2</a> I bow myself toward Thy holy temple, And I confess Thy  name, For Thy kindness, and for Thy truth, For Thou hast made  great Thy saying above all Thy name.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:3">138:3</a> In the day I called, when Thou dost answer me, Thou dost  strengthen me in my soul [with] strength.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:4">138:4</a> O Jehovah, all kings of earth confess Thee, When they have  heard the sayings of Thy mouth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:5">138:5</a> And they sing in the ways of Jehovah, For great [is] the  honour of Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:6">138:6</a> For high [is] Jehovah, and the lowly He seeth, And the  haughty from afar He knoweth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:7">138:7</a> If I walk in the midst of distress Thou quickenest me,  Against the anger of mine enemies Thou sendest forth Thy hand,  And Thy right hand doth save me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_138:8">138:8</a> Jehovah doth perfect for me, O Jehovah, Thy kindness [is]  to the age, The works of Thy hands let not fall!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:1">139:1</a> To the Overseer. -- A Psalm by David. Jehovah, Thou hast  searched me, and knowest.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:2">139:2</a> Thou -- Thou hast known my sitting down, And my rising up,  Thou hast attended to my thoughts from afar.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:3">139:3</a> My path and my couch Thou hast fanned, And [with] all my  ways hast been acquainted.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:4">139:4</a> For there is not a word in my tongue, Lo, O Jehovah, Thou  hast known it all!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:5">139:5</a> Behind and before Thou hast besieged me, And Thou dost  place on me Thy hand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:6">139:6</a> Knowledge too wonderful for me, It hath been set on high,  I am not able for it.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:7">139:7</a> Whither do I go from Thy Spirit? And whither from Thy face  do I flee?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:8">139:8</a> If I ascend the heavens -- there Thou [art], And spread  out a couch in Sheol, lo, Thee!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:9">139:9</a> I take the wings of morning, I dwell in the uttermost part  of the sea,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:10">139:10</a> Also there Thy hand doth lead me, And Thy right hand doth  hold me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:11">139:11</a> And I say, `Surely darkness bruiseth me, Then night [is]  light to me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:12">139:12</a> Also darkness hideth not from Thee, And night as day  shineth, as [is] darkness so [is] light.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:13">139:13</a> For Thou -- Thou hast possessed my reins, Thou dost cover  me in my mother's belly.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:14">139:14</a> I confess Thee, because that [with] wonders I have been  distinguished. Wonderful [are] Thy works, And my soul is  knowing [it] well.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:15">139:15</a> My substance was not hid from Thee, When I was made in  secret, Curiously wrought in the lower part of earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:16">139:16</a> Mine unformed substance Thine eyes saw, And on Thy book  all of them are written, The days they were formed -- And not  one among them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:17">139:17</a> And to me how precious have been Thy thoughts, O God, how  great hath been their sum!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:18">139:18</a> I recount them! than the sand they are more, I have  waked, and I am still with Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:19">139:19</a> Dost Thou slay, O God, the wicked? Then, men of blood,  turn aside from me!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:20">139:20</a> Who exchange Thee for wickedness, Lifted up to vanity  [are] Thine enemies.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:21">139:21</a> Do not I hate, Jehovah, those hating Thee? And with Thy  withstanders grieve myself?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:22">139:22</a> [With] perfect hatred I have hated them, Enemies they  have become to me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:23">139:23</a> Search me, O God, and know my heart, Try me, and know my  thoughts,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_139:24">139:24</a> And see if a grievous way be in me, And lead me in a way  age-during!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:1">140:1</a> To the Overseer. -- A Psalm of David. Deliver me, O  Jehovah, from an evil man, From one of violence Thou keepest  me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:2">140:2</a> Who have devised evils in the heart, All the day they  assemble [for] wars.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:3">140:3</a> They sharpened their tongue as a serpent, Poison of an  adder [is] under their lips. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:4">140:4</a> Preserve me, Jehovah, from the hands of the wicked, From  one of violence Thou keepest me, Who have devised to overthrow  my steps.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:5">140:5</a> The proud hid a snare for me -- and cords, They spread a  net by the side of the path, Snares they have set for me.  Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:6">140:6</a> I have said to Jehovah, `My God [art] Thou, Hear, Jehovah,  the voice of my supplications.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:7">140:7</a> O Jehovah, my Lord, strength of my salvation, Thou hast  covered my head in the day of armour.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:8">140:8</a> Grant not, O Jehovah, the desires of the wicked, His  wicked device bring not forth, They are high. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:9">140:9</a> The chief of my surrounders, The perverseness of their  lips covereth them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:10">140:10</a> They cause to fall on themselves burning coals, Into fire  He doth cast them, Into deep pits -- they arise not.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:11">140:11</a> A talkative man is not established in the earth, One of  violence -- evil hunteth to overflowing.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:12">140:12</a> I have known that Jehovah doth execute The judgment of  the afflicted, The judgment of the needy.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_140:13">140:13</a> Only -- the righteous give thanks to Thy name, The  upright do dwell with Thy presence!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:1">141:1</a> A Psalm, by David. O Jehovah, I have called Thee, haste to  me, Give ear [to] my voice when I call to Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:2">141:2</a> My prayer is prepared -- incense before Thee, The lifting  up of my hands -- the evening present.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:3">141:3</a> Set, O Jehovah, a watch for my mouth, Watch Thou over the  door of my lips.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:4">141:4</a> Incline not my heart to an evil thing, To do habitually  actions in wickedness, With men working iniquity, Yea, I eat  not of their pleasant things.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:5">141:5</a> The righteous doth beat me [in] kindness. And doth reprove  me, Oil of the head my head disalloweth not, For still my  prayer [is] about their vexations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:6">141:6</a> Their judges have been released by the sides of a rock,  And they have heard my sayings, For they have been pleasant.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:7">141:7</a> As one tilling and ripping up in the land, Have our bones  been scattered at the command of Saul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:8">141:8</a> But to Thee, O Jehovah, my Lord, [are] mine eyes, In Thee  I have trusted, Make not bare my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:9">141:9</a> Keep me from the gin they laid for me, Even snares of  workers of iniquity.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_141:10">141:10</a> The wicked fall in their nets together, till I pass over!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:1">142:1</a> An Instruction of David, a Prayer when he is in the cave.  My voice [is] unto Jehovah, I cry, My voice [is] unto Jehovah,  I entreat grace.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:2">142:2</a> I pour forth before Him my meditation, My distress before  Him I declare.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:3">142:3</a> When my spirit hath been feeble in me, Then Thou hast  known my path; In the way [in] which I walk, They have hid a  snare for me.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:4">142:4</a> Looking on the right hand -- and seeing, And I have none  recognizing; Perished hath refuge from me, There is none  inquiring for my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:5">142:5</a> I have cried unto thee, O Jehovah, I have said, `Thou  [art] my refuge, My portion in the land of the living.'</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:6">142:6</a> Attend Thou unto my loud cry, For I have become very low,  Deliver Thou me from my pursuers, For they have been stronger  than I.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_142:7">142:7</a> Bring forth from prison my soul to confess Thy name, The  righteous do compass me about, When Thou conferrest benefits  upon me!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:1">143:1</a> A Psalm of David. O Jehovah, hear my prayer, Give ear unto  my supplications, In Thy faithfulness answer me -- in Thy  righteousness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:2">143:2</a> And enter not into judgment with Thy servant, For no one  living is justified before Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:3">143:3</a> For an enemy hath pursued my soul, He hath bruised to the  earth my life, He hath caused me to dwell in dark places, As  the dead of old.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:4">143:4</a> And my spirit in me is become feeble, Within me is my  heart become desolate.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:5">143:5</a> I have remembered days of old, I have meditated on all  Thine acts, On the work of Thy hand I muse.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:6">143:6</a> I have spread forth my hands unto Thee, My soul [is] as a  weary land for Thee. Selah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:7">143:7</a> Haste, answer me, O Jehovah, My spirit hath been consumed,  Hide not Thou Thy face from me, Or I have been compared with  those going down [to] the pit.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:8">143:8</a> Cause me to hear in the morning Thy kindness, For in Thee  I have trusted, Cause me to know the way that I go, For unto  Thee I have lifted up my soul.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:9">143:9</a> Deliver me from mine enemies, O Jehovah, Near Thee I am  covered.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:10">143:10</a> Teach me to do Thy good pleasure, For Thou [art] my God  -- Thy Spirit [is] good, Lead me into a land of uprightness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:11">143:11</a> For Thy name's sake O Jehovah, Thou dost quicken me, In  Thy righteousness, Thou bringest out from distress my soul,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_143:12">143:12</a> And in Thy kindness cuttest off mine enemies, And hast  destroyed all the adversaries of my soul, For I [am] Thy  servant!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:1">144:1</a> By David. Blessed [is] Jehovah my rock, who is teaching My  hands for war, my fingers for battle.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:2">144:2</a> My kind one, and my bulwark, My tower, and my deliverer,  My shield, and in whom I have trusted, Who is subduing my  people under me!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:3">144:3</a> Jehovah, what [is] man that Thou knowest him? Son of man,  that Thou esteemest him?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:4">144:4</a> Man to vanity hath been like, His days [are] as a shadow  passing by.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:5">144:5</a> Jehovah, incline Thy heavens and come down, Strike against  mountains, and they smoke.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:6">144:6</a> Send forth lightning, and scatter them, Send forth Thine  arrows, and trouble them,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:7">144:7</a> Send forth Thy hand from on high, Free me, and deliver me  from many waters, From the hand of sons of a stranger,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:8">144:8</a> Because their mouth hath spoken vanity, And their right  hand [is] a right hand of falsehood.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:9">144:9</a> O God, a new song I sing to Thee, On a psaltery of ten  strings I sing praise to Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:10">144:10</a> Who is giving deliverance to kings, Who is freeing David  His servant from the sword of evil.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:11">144:11</a> Free me, and deliver me From the hand of sons of a  stranger, Because their mouth hath spoken vanity, And their  right hand [is] a right hand of falsehood,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:12">144:12</a> Because our sons [are] as plants, Becoming great in their  youth, Our daughters as hewn stones, Polished -- the likeness  of a palace,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:13">144:13</a> Our garners [are] full, bringing out from kind to kind,  Our flocks are bringing forth thousands, Ten thousands in our  out-places,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:14">144:14</a> Our oxen are carrying, there is no breach, And there is  no outgoing, And there is no crying in our broad places.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_144:15">144:15</a> O the happiness of the people that is thus, O the  happiness of the people whose God [is] Jehovah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:1">145:1</a> Praise by David. I exalt Thee, my God, O king, And bless  Thy name to the age and for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:2">145:2</a> Every day do I bless Thee, And praise Thy name to the age  and for ever.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:3">145:3</a> Great [is] Jehovah, and praised greatly, And of His  greatness there is no searching.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:4">145:4</a> Generation to generation praiseth Thy works, And Thy  mighty acts they declare.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:5">145:5</a> The honour -- the glory of Thy majesty, And the matters of  Thy wonders I declare.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:6">145:6</a> And the strength of Thy fearful acts they tell, And Thy  greatness I recount.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:7">145:7</a> The memorial of the abundance of Thy goodness they send  forth. And Thy righteousness they sing.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:8">145:8</a> Gracious and merciful [is] Jehovah, Slow to anger, and  great in kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:9">145:9</a> Good [is] Jehovah to all, And His mercies [are] over all  His works.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:10">145:10</a> Confess Thee O Jehovah, do all Thy works, And Thy saints  do bless Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:11">145:11</a> The honour of Thy kingdom they tell, And [of] Thy might  they speak,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:12">145:12</a> To make known to sons of men His mighty acts, The honour  of the majesty of His kingdom.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:13">145:13</a> Thy kingdom [is] a kingdom of all ages, And Thy dominion  [is] in all generations.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:14">145:14</a> Jehovah is supporting all who are falling, And raising up  all who are bowed down.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:15">145:15</a> The eyes of all unto Thee do look, And Thou art giving to  them their food in its season,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:16">145:16</a> Opening Thy hand, and satisfying The desire of every  living thing.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:17">145:17</a> Righteous [is] Jehovah in all His ways, And kind in all  His works.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:18">145:18</a> Near [is] Jehovah to all those calling Him, To all who  call Him in truth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:19">145:19</a> The desire of those fearing Him He doth, And their cry He  heareth, and saveth them.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:20">145:20</a> Jehovah preserveth all those loving Him, And all the  wicked He destroyeth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_145:21">145:21</a> The praise of Jehovah my mouth speaketh, And all flesh  doth bless His holy name, To the age and for ever!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:1">146:1</a> Praise ye Jah! Praise, O my soul, Jehovah.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:2">146:2</a> I praise Jehovah during my life, I sing praise to my God  while I exist.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:3">146:3</a> Trust not in princes -- in a son of man, For he hath no  deliverance.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:4">146:4</a> His spirit goeth forth, he returneth to his earth, In  that day have his thoughts perished.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:5">146:5</a> O the happiness of him Who hath the God of Jacob for his  help, His hope [is] on Jehovah his God,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:6">146:6</a> Making the heavens and earth, The sea and all that [is] in  them, Who is keeping truth to the age,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:7">146:7</a> Doing judgment for the oppressed, Giving bread to the  hungry.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:8">146:8</a> Jehovah is loosing the prisoners, Jehovah is opening (the  eyes of) the blind, Jehovah is raising the bowed down, Jehovah  is loving the righteous,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:9">146:9</a> Jehovah is preserving the strangers, The fatherless and  widow He causeth to stand, And the way of the wicked He turneth  upside down.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_146:10">146:10</a> Jehovah doth reign to the age, Thy God, O Zion, to  generation and generation, Praise ye Jah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:1">147:1</a> Praise ye Jah! For [it is] good to praise our God, For  pleasant -- comely [is] praise.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:2">147:2</a> Building Jerusalem [is] Jehovah, The driven away of Israel  He gathereth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:3">147:3</a> Who is giving healing to the broken of heart, And is  binding up their griefs.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:4">147:4</a> Appointing the number of the stars, To all them He giveth  names.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:5">147:5</a> Great [is] our Lord, and abundant in power, Of His  understanding there is no narration.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:6">147:6</a> Jehovah is causing the meek to stand, Making low the  wicked unto the earth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:7">147:7</a> Answer ye to Jehovah with thanksgiving, Sing ye to our God  with a harp.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:8">147:8</a> Who is covering the heavens with clouds, Who is preparing  for the earth rain, Who is causing grass to spring up [on]  mountains,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:9">147:9</a> Giving to the beast its food, To the young of the ravens  that call.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:10">147:10</a> Not in the might of the horse doth He delight, Not in the  legs of a man is He pleased.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:11">147:11</a> Jehovah is pleased with those fearing Him, With those  waiting for His kindness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:12">147:12</a> Glorify, O Jerusalem, Jehovah, Praise thy God, O Zion.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:13">147:13</a> For He did strengthen the bars of thy gates, He hath  blessed thy sons in thy midst.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:14">147:14</a> Who is making thy border peace, [With] the fat of wheat  He satisfieth Thee.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:15">147:15</a> Who is sending forth His saying [on] earth, Very speedily  doth His word run.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:16">147:16</a> Who is giving snow like wool, Hoar-frost as ashes He  scattereth.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:17">147:17</a> Casting forth His ice like morsels, Before His cold who  doth stand?</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:18">147:18</a> He sendeth forth His word and melteth them, He causeth  His wind to blow -- the waters flow.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:19">147:19</a> Declaring His words to Jacob, His statutes and His  judgments to Israel.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_147:20">147:20</a> He hath not done so to any nation, As to judgments, they  have not known them. Praise ye Jah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:1">148:1</a> Praise ye Jah! Praise ye Jehovah from the heavens, Praise  ye Him in high places.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:2">148:2</a> Praise ye Him, all His messengers, Praise ye Him, all His  hosts.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:3">148:3</a> Praise ye Him, sun and moon, Praise ye Him, all stars of  light.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:4">148:4</a> Praise ye Him, heavens of heavens, And ye waters that are  above the heavens.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:5">148:5</a> They do praise the name of Jehovah, For He commanded, and  they were created.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:6">148:6</a> And He establisheth them for ever to the age, A statute He  gave, and they pass not over.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:7">148:7</a> Praise ye Jehovah from the earth, Dragons and all deeps,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:8">148:8</a> Fire and hail, snow and vapour, Whirlwind doing His word;</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:9">148:9</a> The mountains and all heights, Fruit tree, and all cedars,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:10">148:10</a> The wild beast, and all cattle, Creeping thing, and  winged bird,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:11">148:11</a> Kings of earth, and all peoples, Chiefs, and all judges  of earth,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:12">148:12</a> Young men, and also maidens, Aged men, with youths,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:13">148:13</a> They praise the name of Jehovah, For His name alone hath  been set on high, His honour [is] above earth and heavens.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_148:14">148:14</a> And He exalteth the horn of His people, The praise of all  His saints, Of the sons of Israel, a people near Him. Praise ye  Jah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:1">149:1</a> Praise ye Jah! Sing ye to Jehovah a new song, His praise  in an assembly of saints.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:2">149:2</a> Israel doth rejoice in his Maker, Sons of Zion do joy in  their king.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:3">149:3</a> They praise His name in a dance, With timbrel and harp  sing praise to Him.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:4">149:4</a> For Jehovah is pleased with His people, He beautifieth the  humble with salvation.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:5">149:5</a> Exult do saints in honour, They sing aloud on their beds.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:6">149:6</a> The exaltation of God [is] in their throat, And a  two-edged sword in their hand.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:7">149:7</a> To do vengeance among nations, Punishments among the  peoples.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:8">149:8</a> To bind their kings with chains, And their honoured ones  with fetters of iron,</p> 
 <p><a name="an_149:9">149:9</a> To do among them the judgment written, An honour it [is]  for all his saints. Praise ye Jah!</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:1">150:1</a> Praise ye Jah! Praise ye God in His holy place, Praise Him  in the expanse of His strength.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:2">150:2</a> Praise Him in His mighty acts, Praise Him according to the  abundance of His greatness.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:3">150:3</a> Praise Him with blowing of trumpet, Praise Him with  psaltery and harp.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:4">150:4</a> Praise Him with timbrel and dance, Praise Him with  stringed instruments and organ.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:5">150:5</a> Praise Him with cymbals of sounding, Praise Him with  cymbals of shouting.</p> 
 <p><a name="an_150:6">150:6</a> All that doth breathe doth praise Jah! Praise ye Jah!</p> 
 <p></p><hr>
